# 太上洞渊神咒经

*The Supreme Cavernous Abyss Divine Incantations Sutra*

**Title:** *The Supreme Cavernous Abyss Divine Incantations Sutra*. Author unknown. Twenty scrolls. Source text: *Daoist Canon of the Zhengtong Era*, Cavernous Mystery Division, *Benwen* Category.

**Preface to *The Supreme Cavernous Abyss Divine Incantations Sutra***
Composed by Du Guangting, Supreme Perfected of the Celestial Chariot Transmission, Heavenly Master with Special Advancement, Grand Mentor of the Heir Apparent, Grand Master of Splendid Happiness, Acting Minister of the Ministry of Revenue in the Department of State Affairs, Grand Academician of the Chongzhen Institute, Pillar of the State, Duke of the Cai Principality of Pengcheng Commandery, Grand Master of Vast Teachings, Feathered Guest of the Golden Gate, Literary Master in Attendance to the Imperial Compositions, Palace Attendant of the Inner Court, Master of the Three Teachings’ Discourses, and Broadly Accomplished Master, enfeoffed with five thousand households and granted an additional one thousand six hundred in true seal, bestowed with the Purple Robe.

At the close of the Western Jin, the Central Plains fell into chaos, famine pressed hard, and pestilence arose. Wang Zuan, a Daoist of Horse Hoof Mountain in Jintan, had long practiced hidden virtue to succor beings, his benevolence extending even to the lowest creatures. As poisonous miasmas spread at the time, many perished, villages lay desolate, and the dead filled the streets like bedding. In his quiet chamber, Zuan soared petitions to Heaven, weeping through three nights without cease.

By the third night, a radiance bright as daylight filled the courtyard, and auspicious winds with scenic clouds suffused the heavens. Suddenly, celestial fragrance and heavenly music descended into the courtyard, where over three thousand armored warriors, armed with golden armor and sharp weapons, arrayed themselves as if awaiting command. In but a moment, pearl-encrusted canopies and jeweled banners, rainbow streamers and crimson standards, red flags and embroidered pennants advanced in pairs to receive them, while white cranes soared in flight and vermilion phoenixes danced in unison. Two azure-clad attendants bore flowers and incense, and four jade maidens held aloft a jade table. The earth unfolded into brocade mats, a great screen stood before them, and on either side stood Dragon and Tiger Generals with over twenty attendants and officials, as if in solemn guard. Beyond the Dragon and Tiger Lords, dozens of golden-armored generals and great divine kings arrayed themselves in orderly ranks.

Presently, pipes and flutes resounded through the sky, descending from the northwest, while five-colored lights blazed with dazzling brilliance. One bearing a tablet and girded with a sword stepped forward and announced to Zuan: "The Supreme Dao Lord has arrived." Then a throne of a hundred treasures descended from the void, and there appeared the Dao Lord seated upon a five-colored flying dragon and lotus throne, hovering over ten feet above the ground, attended by two Perfected Ones and two Celestial Masters. Zuan bowed deeply, advancing with reverent steps to receive him.

The Dao Lord said: "You have pitied the people, expressing it in your memorials, carving out your heart and weeping tears that have moved both the seen and unseen realms. The earthly officials have reported this, and I have taken note of you." Zuan prostrated himself in gratitude.

The Dao Lord continued: "The interplay of yin and yang nurtures the myriad things, endowing them with the five phases for their use. Yet the five phases overcome one another, and all things wax and wane, ceaselessly succeeding one another without pause. Thus life begets life without end, qi follows qi in unbroken succession, and since kalpas immemorial, this has never once ceased. Those who attain life harmonize with pure yang, ascending to heaven as immortals. Those who meet death sink into utmost yin, becoming ghosts upon the earth. Among ghostly beings, there are distinctions of superiority and inferiority, strength and weakness, firmness and softness, good and evil—no different from the world of men.

The Jade Emperor, fearing the wantonness of ghosts and spirits bringing calamity upon humanity, has commanded the Five Emperors and the Three Officials to enforce the laws and decrees that restrain and govern them, with punishments and statutes fully established. Yet in this degenerate age, deceitful people abound, the wellspring of purity has scattered, and malevolent qi sprouts forth. They are disloyal to their lords, unfilial to their parents, violating the teachings of the Three Bonds and Five Constants, casting themselves into death’s embrace. Thus the demonic ghosts of the Six Heavens’ old qi, along with the defeated armies and dead generals of past ages, band together to harm the living, riding the winds and rains, seizing upon weakness and opportunity to spread manifold diseases, inflicting grievous harm. Many do not live out their allotted years, cut down in untimely deaths.

Long ago in the Du Yang Palace, I revealed the *Divine Incantations Scripture* and entrusted it to the Perfected One Tang Ping, bidding him disseminate it to save humanity. Yet the ignorant and foolish of the world, seeing names like Wang Jian and Bai Qi, dismiss it as mere fabrication. These were once generals in life, leading armies in death as ghostly commanders. Those who accumulated merit were promoted to yin officials, while the cruel and violent remained bound to demonic ranks, riding the败 qi of the five phases to bring plague and pestilence. Yet they fear the might of yang and are subdued by divine incantations, which shall surely eradicate them.

Now I bestow upon you the transformed scripture of divine incantations. Follow and practice it to protect and shelter the myriad people." Thereupon, he commanded an attendant to open the ninefold radiance and present the scripture along with the secrets of the Three and Five Great Fasts, saying: "Strive to practice these hidden merits, and you may hope to fulfill the ranks of immortality." With these words, the Dao Lord and his retinue of Perfected Ones ascended toward the northwest.

Zuan then followed the scripture’s teachings and fasts, practicing them throughout the Jiangnan region. The people thrived in peace, and pestilence was dispelled. From the Jin dynasty to the present, those who have received its blessings are beyond count. This depends on purity, reverence, utmost sincerity, and diligence—clarity and sincerity evoke response as surely as echo answers sound. Should one grow lax, careless, or recklessly divulge these teachings, one will incur fault and guilt. Those who cultivate and uphold these practices must heed this warning.

Moreover, this scripture is vast and profound, proclaimed by the Golden Mouth of the Primordial Emperor himself, its principles deep and abstruse. The Supreme’s subtle words and secret instructions, if recited with a devoted heart and unwavering intent, will kindle incense and summon the true spirits in an instant. Divine soldiers and celestial officers will sweep away evil like lightning, while fierce steeds and heavenly escorts will dispel pestilential miasmas wherever they go. Now, seeking skilled hands once more, we reopen this auspicious cause, exhausting the art of carving and the subtlety of ink, hoping its practice will not fade and its dissemination will know no bounds. May the imperial reign endure and surpass the Zhou’s divination, may the emperor’s years stretch far and exceed Yao’s longevity. May the realm’s chariots unite under one sky, its calendar extend to all lands. Praise the power and virtue of the Great Dao, aiding the imperial court’s benevolent nurturing. Boundless are the vast blessings and mysterious grace!

*The Supreme Cavernous Abyss Divine Incantations Scripture*, Scroll One
*The Vow Against Demons* Chapter

The Dao spoke: "Long ago, above the Three Heavens, I expounded the immeasurable scriptures to all men and women, teaching and transforming all beings. At that time, the Perfected One Wei Mingluo and four hundred ninety thousand heavenly hosts from the lower worlds arrived above the Three Heavens to hear the immeasurable great scriptures, bringing peace within and without. Mingluo and the others arose, bowing thrice to the Supreme, and inquired: 'Is the teaching and transformation of the Heavenly Worthy difficult?' They humbly expressed their sentiments.

The Supreme said: 'Have you come from Jambudvīpa?'
Mingluo and the others replied: 'Yes.'
The Supreme said: 'Among the people of the world, are there any who follow the Dao, uphold the scriptures, and study immortality?'
Mingluo and the others said: 'The people of the world accumulate evil and do not believe in the Dao or its methods.'"

Amidst these sounds, only the wails of mourning corpses are heard, never the melodies of immortals’ songs. The people are filthy and defiled, the Three Caverns blocked and obstructed. The calamities of the hundred and six disasters—blades, warfare, epidemics, and sickness—rage unchecked. Demon kings unleash their poisons, slaughtering the good and virtuous. Every household suffers misfortune, and cries of sorrow follow one after another. Beings devour one another, inflicting suffering upon themselves. Drawn into death together, they cling to ignorance and endure torment, utterly unaware of escape. How can such people be delivered?

Upon hearing Mingluo and the others speak thus, the Supreme addressed the assembled gods and humans: “What do beings ponder? They know not the Dao or its methods, nor do they understand what they endure. They commit evil of their own accord, then slander one another. The Three Caverns’ teachings circulate widely, yet none receive and uphold them—like blind men wandering beneath the sun and moon. Are the sun and moon not bright? The blind cannot see. Though Dharma masters proclaim and transform, fools remain unmoved.”

Then the Supreme, leading eighty million billion heavenly beings and jade maidens, descended to save them, passing through Jade Capital. Atop Jade Capital Mountain stood a peach tree, its height spanning three hundred ninety billion miles. Its eastern branch sheltered the eastern lands, its southern branch covered the southern realms, its western branch shaded the west, and its northern branch blanketed the north. Once every forty-nine billion years it bloomed, and once every eighty billion years it bore a single fruit. When ripe, the fruit was as large as a cartwheel; one who ate of it would hunger no more for three thousand years. Ghosts who beheld this peach tree would perish of their own accord. Each heavenly being took up a branch of this peach wood and descended to slay the plague ghosts, and all manner of auspicious signs arose.

The Dao declared: “From the years *xinsi* and *renwu* onward, ghostly soldiers have run rampant, and demon kings have spread their poisons, afflicting the people with toxic illnesses. I now dispatch forty-nine billion enforcers to seize the thirty-six heavenly demon kings and bring them down to swear an oath: ‘From this day forward, if the people of any land suffer unjust deaths, sudden illnesses, imprisonment, or bondage, it is because these demon kings have failed to restrain their underlings, allowing them to harm the seed of the people. Henceforth, by the golden decree of the Supreme, any who disobey shall cause the people of their lands to suffer epidemics, warfare, hardship, imprisonment, bondage, and deaths without reason. This will be the fault of the demon kings who first failed to restrain their underlings—thus they shall be slain without mercy.’”

Thereupon, the Supreme sent forth forty-nine myriad officials from the ten directions, along with thirty million heavenly maidens and the Great Brahmā King, to summon the thirty-six heavenly demon kings and eighty billion myriad lesser ghost kings, together with their wives, children, and retinues, to swear a solemn oath. The Queen Consorts of the Dark Maiden and Māhādevī, numbering thirty-six myriad, all came as well to assist the Supreme in reprimanding the demon kings. The demon kings prostrated themselves and each dispatched their demonic sons and warrior attendants to patrol the borders of the lands, protecting the people within, lest the Supreme execute them.

The Brahmā Sons of the Nine Heavens, the great demon kings, their kings and consorts, and their multicolored maidens all bowed thrice and submitted to the Supreme’s teachings.

The Dao declared: “From the time of Fuxi until the end of the Han, the people lived in great joy, yet most did not believe in the Dao. They all received the natural *qi* of heaven’s demonic influences, unaware of the Dao, unaware of the Dharma, unaware of the scriptures, serving only the natural order. Later, those who believed in the scriptures were few indeed. In the era of the Great Jin, as the world approached its end, the people lacked purity. Lineages arose to govern the people of the world, first enduring much suffering—oppressed from above and below—before gradually flourishing. Their prosperity lay in the lands east of the Yangzi, where heaven and humanity converged, and the *qi* of the Dao flourished.

The kalpa’s end draws near, yet within it, some will attain the Three Treasures, the immeasurable *Shangqing*, the *Huangting* records of immortality, the *Taisu*, and the *Lingbao* samādhi. These people all possess great blessings from past lives, their fortune flowing into future incarnations. Upon hearing and seeing these scriptures, they will escape the calamities of the Three Rivers’ great floods.

Excellent! Excellent! You men and women—whether kings, emperors, lords, governors of two thousand households, or even the lowliest, including slaves and servants—if you can attain these scriptures and receive these covenants and registers, your names will enter the ranks of immortals, and you shall never suffer unjust deaths.”

In the Palace of Mystic Radiance, the Supreme expounded this divine incantation scripture. Eight hundred million myriad of the Nine Heavens’ great demons, rākṣasas, ghostly bandits, and the retinues of all the heavens gathered in attendance, listening to the Heavenly Worthy’s discourse. Each clasped their hands and prostrated themselves upon the ground. The Heavenly Worthy then expounded the great scripture of immortal records, and all who heard it felt their bodies undergo wondrous transformations.

The Dao declared: “Listen carefully, for I shall now speak to you of the kalpa’s end in the ages to come. Three thousand years after Fuxi, great floods overflowed, and half the people perished. For thirty-six years, the myriad clans rebelled, slaughtering one another. By the time of the Zhou and Qin’s fall, the people were nearly annihilated. By the end of the Han and Wei, the people were displaced, and half died. When the Liu clan’s fifth-generation descendants inherited their ancestors’ legacy, the four directions cried out in distress, the world teetered on the brink of ruin, and the people could not dwell in peace. Driven and oppressed by the Six Barbarians, they fled to the lands east of the Yangzi, while the gentry concealed their traces, also taking refuge along the Huai and the sea. In the year *jiawu*, the people returned to dwell in the Central Kingdom. Chang’an flourished, the Qin Plain rejoiced, the Six Barbarians submitted as vassals, and all dwelt in the mountains and marshes, not within the central plains. The Dao’s teachings prospered.

Yet the *Wooden Son with Bow Mouth* shall rise again.”

The Dao declared: “As the great kalpa nears its end, the ruling kings fail to govern, and the people sigh in despair. Winds and rains come untimely, the five grains do not ripen, and the hearts of the people turn wicked, rebelling and defying authority. Fathers and sons, brothers and kin plot against one another, leading to annihilation. Grievances and banditry spread, slaughtering the innocent. In such an age, epidemic *qi* abounds, and ninety kinds of illness afflict the world, killing the wicked. Among them is the Red-Headed Slayer Ghost, a ghost king a myriad leagues tall, leading thirty-six billion slayer ghosts.”

Each ghost wields a crimson staff, roaming the world to seek out the living—awaiting them in the fourth month. Where blue *qi* appears, people die suddenly; where red *qi* appears, swelling diseases arise; where yellow *qi* appears, dysentery strikes; where white *qi* appears, cholera rages; where black *qi* appears, legal troubles befall. These ghosts carry such *qi* and spread it across the world, slaying the foolish. Only Daoist masters and dharma teachers who receive this divine incantation sutra are attended by ninety billion myriad great spirits, spontaneous warriors, celestial beings, and jade maidens, all coming to guard and protect. Those who uphold and venerate it will see all illnesses vanish and never suffer an untimely death. Should neighboring states send great bandits to invade, recite this sutra, and the bandits will retreat of their own accord.

As the men and women present heard the Most High expound this sutra, each rose in alarm and performed the threefold bow. The disciples then declared their wish to receive this sutra.

The Dao declared: “As the kalpa’s end draws near, the people grow ever more wicked. Yet among them, those who believe in the Dao and uphold the sutras are all celestial beings, not foolish worldly folk. The Great Sage, seeing the world’s corruption and chaos, dispatched celestial beings to descend and be born in the Middle Kingdom, aiding the times and transforming through teaching. Among the Son of Heaven’s ministers, dukes, governors, and military officers—even those of lowly station—if they wholeheartedly believe in the Dao, heed the sutra, and put it into practice, immortals will guide them. But those who hear this sutra and refuse to receive and uphold it—know that such people have come from the six kinds of livestock and share no karmic affinity with the sutra. Thus, when the great flood comes, they will be devoured by fish and turtles, swept away with the mud, and none will escape.”

The Dao declared: “From this day forth, whether man or woman, if one hears and receives this sutra—regardless of status, be they slave or free, public or private—those who copy, uphold, and venerate its scrolls will gain blessings in every life, rise in rank day by day, recover from illness, and see all wishes fulfilled. For those who uphold this sutra, the Great Demons of the Three Heavens, the Great Demons of the Nine Heavens, the thirty-six generations of demons, and the ten directions’ slayer ghosts—along with their kings, wives, children, and retinues—all swear a dark oath. The Queen of the Dark Maidens, the Lady of the Hemp Maiden, and thirty-six million royal consorts unite to serve as the Most High’s Demon-Subduing King. The demon kings all submit, each dispatching their demon offspring and warrior attendants to patrol the borders, shielding the people within the realm, fearing the Most High’s punishment. The Brahma Sons of the Nine Heavens, the Great Demon Kings of the Celestial Beings, their kings, consorts, and maidens—all perform the threefold bow and obey the Most High’s teachings.”

The Dao declared: “From Fuxi’s time to the end of the Han, the people lived in great joy, yet most did not believe in the Dao. They all received the spontaneous demonic *qi* of Heaven, unaware of the Dao, unaware of the dharma, unaware of the sutras, serving only the spontaneous. Later, those who believed in the sutras were few indeed. In the Great Jin’s era, as the world neared its end, the people lacked purity. Yet from the imperial line, a successor arose to govern the world’s people. At first, they endured much suffering—oppression from above, urgency from below—before gradually flourishing. Their prosperity lay in the lands east of the Yangtze, where celestial and mortal realms converged, and the *qi* of the Dao flourished. As the celestial kalpa’s end approaches, some will attain the Three Treasures, the immeasurable Upper Clarity, the *Huangting* Records of Immortals, the *Taisu* Scripture, and the *Lingbao* Samadhi. Such people all possess great blessings from past lives, their fortune flowing into future incarnations. Hearing this sutra, they will escape the calamity of the Three Rivers’ great flood.

“Excellent indeed! Whether you are men or women—kings, emperors, regional lords, or governors of two thousand households; even the foolish, regardless of slaves—if you encounter this sutra, receive this covenant and register, your names will enter the ranks of immortals, and you will never suffer an unjust death.”

The Most High, in the Palace of Mystic Radiance, expounded this divine incantation sutra. The Great Demons of the Nine Heavens, rakshasa ghosts, bandits, and the retinues of all heavens—eight hundred million myriad beings—all gathered in attendance, listening to the Heavenly Worthy’s discourse. Each clasped their hands and prostrated themselves in reverence. The Heavenly Worthy then revealed the great sutra of immortal records. All who heard it felt a wondrous transformation within.

The Dao declared: “Listen carefully, for I shall now speak of the kalpa’s end in the age to come. From Fuxi’s time, after three thousand years, great floods overflowed, and half the people perished. For thirty-six years, the myriad clans rebelled, slaughtering one another. By the time of the Zhou and Qin’s fall, the people were nearly wiped out. By the end of the Han and Wei, the people were displaced, and half died. Then, the five generations of Liu’s descendants restored their ancestral foundation. At that time, the four directions cried out in distress, the world teetered on the brink, and the people could not live in peace. Driven by the six barbarians, they fled to the lands east of the Yangtze, while the gentry concealed their traces, also seeking refuge in the Huai and the sea. In the year of *jiawu*, the people returned to dwell in the Middle Kingdom. Chang’an opened its gates, the Qin River plains rejoiced, the six barbarians submitted as vassals, and all dwelt in the mountains and marshes, not within the central plains. The Dao’s teachings prospered.

Yet the *Wooden Son with Bow Mouth* shall rise again.”

The Dao declared: “As the great kalpa nears its end, the ruling kings fail to govern, and the people sigh in despair. Winds and rains come untimely, the five grains do not ripen, and the hearts of the people turn wicked, rebelling and defying authority. Fathers and sons, brothers and kin plot against one another, leading to annihilation. Grievances and banditry spread, slaughtering the innocent. In such an age, epidemic *qi* abounds, and ninety kinds of illness afflict the world, killing the wicked. Among them is the Red-Headed Slayer Ghost, a ghost king a myriad leagues tall, leading thirty-six billion slayer ghosts. Each ghost wields a crimson staff, roaming the world to seek out the living—awaiting them in the fourth month. Where blue *qi* appears, people die suddenly; where red *qi* appears, swelling diseases arise; where yellow *qi* appears, dysentery strikes; where white *qi* appears, cholera rages; where black *qi* appears, legal troubles befall. These ghosts carry such *qi* and spread it across the world, slaying the foolish. Only Daoist masters and dharma teachers who receive this divine incantation sutra are attended by ninety billion myriad great spirits, spontaneous warriors, celestial beings, and jade maidens, all coming to guard and protect.”

Should any uphold and venerate this sutra, all maladies shall vanish of themselves, and none shall meet untimely death. Should neighboring states send great bandits to invade, recite this sutra in turn, and the bandits shall depart of their own accord.

At this, the men and women seated before the Most High, upon hearing this sutra expounded, each rose in astonishment and performed the threefold bow. The disciples then declared their wish to receive this sutra.

The Dao spoke: The kalpa’s end draws near, and the people grow ever more wicked. Yet among them, those who believe in the Dao and uphold this sutra are all heavenly beings, not the foolish of this world. The Great Sage, seeing the world mired in chaos, dispatched heavenly beings to descend and be born in the Middle Kingdom, to aid in the teaching and transformation of the age.

Among the Son of Heaven’s ministers, the dukes and princes, the magistrates and commanders, even those of lowly station—if they wholeheartedly believe in the Dao, hear this sutra, and put faith in its use, immortals shall guide them. But if one hears and sees this sutra yet refuses to receive and uphold it, know that such a person has come from among the six kinds of livestock and shares no karmic affinity with this sutra. Thus, when the great flood comes, they shall be devoured by fish and turtles, swept away with the mud, and ten thousand shall not escape.

The Dao spoke: From this day forward, whether man or woman, should any hear and see this sutra and receive and uphold it—regardless of whether they be male or female, bondservant or free, public or private—those who receive it, copy it, and venerate its scrolls shall, in every life, reap benefit: their official ranks shall rise daily, illnesses shall be cured, and all wishes shall accord with their hearts. Should any receive and uphold this sutra, the great demons of the Three Heavens, the great demons of the Nine Heavens, the demons of thirty-six worlds, and the slayer ghosts of the ten directions shall be swept away, and the people shall perish utterly. Only the Daoists and those who receive this sutra shall be welcomed by nine dragons, and a hundred billion heavenly beings shall come to distinguish good from evil—you must believe this.

If one falls ill, first examine the affliction, then receive and uphold this sutra. If one faces legal troubles or imprisonment, or suffers constant misfortune, receive this sutra. If one is plagued by madness, slander, or myriad disputes, receive this sutra. For all that is inauspicious, receive this sutra. Those who receive this sutra shall not be harassed by demon kings.

The Dao spoke: In this age of the Five Turbidities, worldly officials oppress with severity, showing no mercy to those below. The people sigh in distress, and the myriad folk harbor resentment. The world drifts in chaos, the sun and moon lose their measure, the five grains fail to ripen, many become refugees, and great floods arise. The wise, upon seeing this sutra, should hasten to receive it, transcribe its scrolls, and store them in bamboo chests, baskets, or boxes, placing them upon a high seat. If not, they may also be kept in five-colored pouches. Those who recite it in turn shall see demonic soldiers scatter of themselves and legal troubles resolved. Should one in a household receive this sutra, it shall avert calamity from that entire household. Even if one is illiterate, merely receiving it and hiring another to copy it, then venerating it within the home, shall cause evil ghosts to submit, and none shall dare approach.

The Dao spoke: From this day forward, wherever this sutra is recited, should there be illness, legal troubles, slander, or depletion within the household, hear this sutra’s admonition and recite the demon-subduing incantation. Should any ghost refuse to depart, falsely claiming to be a great spirit—whether a mountain or forest deity, a local earth god, a temple master, a fallen soldier or general, or a ghost freed from the registers—if they come to aid the demon kings, afflicting the people of the world and refusing the Great Dharma, the slayer gods of the ten directions shall seize and execute them. Should they return again, persisting in violence and inflicting cruel harm, the ghost kings shall slay them, and the demon kings shall rend their bodies into ten thousand pieces, granting no mercy.

Swiftly, swiftly, as in the statutes and ordinances!

The Dao spoke: The world grows ever more hurried, and the people ever more wicked, while those who believe in the Dharma are few. The great flood draws near, and I fear many of you shall drown and perish, unaware of the time of deliverance. My compassion is deep, and so from the Ninefold Chamber of the Dark Radiance Palace, I build a bridge for all future sentient beings, open the path of the Dharma, point out the Way, and guide them with the Dharma, that they may escape the Three Calamities, dispel the Nine Perils, avoid the Eight Difficulties, be born among heavenly beings, and ascend to immortality, their blessings endless through countless lives. I move the demon kings to pacify the myriad folk, preemptively reciting this incantation to restrain and banish evil ghosts.

From this day forward, wherever this sutra is received and upheld or recited in turn, all shall enjoy every kind of fortune and benefit. In future generations, should men or women receive this sutra and honor their masters, they too shall attain immortality.

The Dao spoke: The fifth-generation descendant, Liu Zi, shall assist in governing the realm, continuing the lineage of immortals. Among the people of the Great Han, many shall encounter the Three Treasures. Why is this? Because in this world, there are those of auspicious destiny who can awaken the mind of the Dao.

Countless recluses dwell in mountains and forests. As the great kalpa nears its end, seven or eight out of ten have received this sutra. The three disasters loom over you all, yet only those destined for the Dao can believe and uphold it. For the sake of all beings, the Most High wept tears of the Five Phases. If you trust my words, the nine-dragon chariot shall come to welcome you. If you do not, the Three Rivers of Mengjin shall claim you.

Here, three hundred million men and women have all come to receive this sutra.

The Dao spoke: You have received these twenty scrolls. Honor them, practice them, and maintain them in all actions. The myriad illnesses within your bodies shall heal of themselves. Officials shall rise in rank, and all wishes shall align with your hearts. You shall also behold the True Lord of the future. The True Lord is not far—when the disaster of the *jiashen* year arises, great chaos shall engulf the world. The world shall be swept clean, and heaven and earth shall be reborn. Then the True Lord shall appear.

When the True Lord comes, sages, immortals, and all who have received this sutra shall gather to assist. Daoists from the east, west, south, and north shall serve as aides, and none shall be fools. You, the people of this world, need only receive this sutra to naturally behold the True Lord.

The Dao spoke: The True Lord shall be surnamed *Mu*, given name *Gongkou*, and shall rule the world. The world shall know great joy, with ninefold harvests and human lifespans extended by three thousand years. Heaven and earth shall be renewed, level and harmonious. The sun and moon shall shine brighter than before. Only those who received this sutra in past or present lives shall come to aid the True Lord.

Thus, wise Daoists must guide the ignorant, urging them to receive this sutra. All epidemics and illnesses shall be dispelled, demonic bandits shall scatter and flee, and every wish shall bear fruit, all aspirations fulfilled. Wherever this sutra is received and practiced, demon kings shall aid in its propagation, ensuring no evil befalls its bearers.

The Dao spoke: Male and female Daoists with the bone destiny for immortality shall encounter this sutra. Those whose lifespans align with the True Lord’s advent shall receive it. This sutra holds divine power, opening the hearts of men.

When the True Lord appears, the world shall be governed without striving. There shall be no suffering from blades, weapons, or prisons. Under the rule of sages, the people shall prosper in joy, free from greed for wealth. There shall be no chickens, pigs, dogs, rats, oxen, or horses—no six livestock. Phoenixes and white cranes shall be as common as barnyard fowl, and qilin and lions shall be as tame as household beasts. The Dao and its methods shall be the sole concern, and Daoists shall be the great ministers. Men and women shall be chaste, free from lustful thoughts. The people shall grow tall, no longer resembling the Daoists of today. Unaware, their forms shall transform, becoming upright and grand. Humans shall stand thirteen feet tall, and the True Lord sixteen feet. Their faces shall glow with radiance, and among the people, none shall be ugly—all shall be pleasing to behold, their appearance never wearying the eye.

Hearing the Most High speak of the True Lord’s realm of great joy, the great assembly was overjoyed. Each rose of their own accord, bowing thrice in reverence. The disciples declared: We too shall uphold this sutra.

*Thus concludes the first scroll of the* Most High’s Cavernous Abyss Divine Incantation Sutra.
*Here begins the second scroll of the* Most High’s Cavernous Abyss Divine Incantation Sutra.

**Chapter on Dispatching Ghosts**

The Dao spoke: While I resided in the Ninefold Palace of Mystic Capital, expounding the *Supreme Clarity Middle Mystery Sutra* to the great assembly, there arrived from the lower worlds the World-Transcending Divine Marshal, the Perceptive Knowledge-Sentence Lord’s Disciple, and eighty thousand perfected ones. Together they prostrated, bowing thrice before the Heavenly Worthy, and declared: “The people of the world are wicked, disbelieving in the utmost words. Though the Three Caverns’ scriptures have now emerged, none know to receive them. Plague ghosts and blade-wielding soldiers slaughter sentient beings, and when all beings perish, none seek deliverance. We disciples constantly witness this, and the suffering is unbearable to hear. In the lands today, those who govern are but walking corpses, devoid of those who embody the Dao and virtue. Lords and ministers slaughter one another; fathers and sons punish each other. When Daoists practice the Dao, fools mock them ceaselessly. They drag themselves into evil, neglecting the immortal ranks. The great kalpa draws near, yet they remain unaware. Pestilential qi and malignant epidemics will slaughter nearly all. Unable to endure this sight, we have come to earnestly implore.”

Then the Heavenly Worthy raised His gaze to heaven and sighed deeply: “Alas! Sentient beings fail to grasp the great purpose, neglecting to cultivate their minds, thus inviting calamity and the ravages of plague. I shall now dispatch eight hundred million celestial marshals and celestial infantry, eight hundred million celestial cavalry, four hundred thousand celestial censors, four hundred thousand celestial executioners, and forty-nine thousand celestial garrison guards to expel these ghosts for humanity. You shall carry this *Divine Incantation Sutra* and propagate it throughout the lands. Wherever people receive this sutra, plague ghosts will depart of their own accord.”

The Dao spoke: “From the years *gengchen*, *xinsi*, *renwu*, and *guiwei*, nearing the *jiashen* year, the world will suffer ninety-two kinds of epidemics, slaying the wicked. Without those who embody the Dao, none shall escape this plague. These epidemics will cause alternating chills and fever, headaches and dizziness, disharmony of the five viscera, piercing pain in the heart, nasal congestion, sore throat, coughing, abdominal distension, qi stabbing the heart, cramping of hands and feet, pain piercing the chest and back to the brain, deafness, jaundice, paralysis and swelling, red and black discoloration of the body, and five types of dysentery. There will also be cholera with vomiting of blood, nosebleeds, suppurating sores, shattering pain in the limbs, aching joints, feverish qi driving one to frenzy, sorrowful and disoriented thoughts, sleeplessness at midnight, tossing and turning, incoherent speech, hallucinations of gods and ghosts, swelling of the genitals and lower abdomen, paralysis of hands and feet, and sudden death with loss of consciousness. All such afflictions are the work of plague ghosts come to slay the wicked. If you uphold the teachings of the Three Caverns’ scriptures, I shall command celestial marshals to drive away these ghosts and spare you distress. The deluge is not far off—hasten, all you sentient beings, to cultivate good hearts, receive and transmit the scriptures, and only then shall you escape the great calamity.”

The Dao spoke: “From this day forward, if there are Daoists whose hearts covet the immortal Dao, who seek no worldly glory, who devote themselves entirely to the teachings, who savor the Three Caverns’ scriptures, who follow their masters into the mountains, and who teach and transform others—such people shall have forty-nine billion celestial marshals and infantry dispatched to accompany and protect them. Wherever they go, ten thousand ghosts shall not oppose them. I now command the demon kings: from this day forward, strive for sentient beings and expel all plague ghosts.”

The Dao spoke: “The *jiashen* year approaches, and the great flood is not far off. Plague ghosts now slaughter people, for the world is rife with evil and scarce in goodness. Sentient beings do not recognize the true words; though the Three Caverns’ scriptures have long been propagated, none seek to receive them, thus bringing suffering upon themselves. What more can be done? Sentient beings are pitiable. I shall now dispatch the eight divisions of celestial censors to drive away and slay plague ghosts, banishing them so that Daoists may transform people and lead them to uphold the Three Caverns’ teachings.”

The Dao spoke: “From this day forward, those who receive and uphold this *Divine Incantation Sutra* shall have thirty thousand celestial generals with dark blades covering their bodies. You need only teach and transform all foolish people daily. Fools cling to delusion and mock those who practice goodness—heaven shall dispatch plague ghosts to drive away and slay such people. Their souls shall all enter the three evil destinies, with no hope of escape.”

The Dao of old said: “In the *xinsi* and *renwu* years, eighty million great ghosts shall come to annihilate the wicked. Those who slander the Dao and its teachings with double tongues, who utter the names of masters, who criticize the scriptures, who disbelieve in the Three Caverns, and who refuse to receive the Dao—such people shall be destroyed by the great ghost kings.”

The Dao spoke: “From this day forward, where Daoists submit to the Three Caverns’ teachings and practice the Dao to save people, I shall dispatch ninety trillion celestial soldiers from the Nine Heavens to descend at once and protect you. If a single ghost remains, the marshals of the ten directions shall come to seize it.”

The Dao spoke: “From this day forward, where Daoists transmit this sutra, heaven shall command four hundred ninety thousand marshals of the Three Caverns, eight hundred thousand marshals of the Six Heavens, and ninety billion celestial soldiers from the Thirty-Six Heavens to descend together and slay these plague ghosts. Those among the living who are afflicted with illness or entangled in official matters shall swiftly gain liberation, their ailments lightened and cured, their myriad spirits harmonized, and their families filled with joy. Domestic and external altars and stoves shall all be settled, sparing the living from unjust harassment. All ghosts not of ancestral worship shall be exorcised, banished forever to distant lands. If any ghost disobeys My command and refuses to depart, the demon kings shall each be beheaded without mercy. Beware, for the sage does not speak idly.”

The Dao spoke: “This *Divine Incantation Sutra* names thirty-six celestial demon kings and seventy trillion lesser kings. Where Daoists transmit this sutra, the thirty-six celestial demon kings and the seventy-two lesser kings, including the Perceptive Knowledge-Sentence Lord’s Disciple, shall all submit. Thus, those who, at the end of the kalpa, receive and enshrine this *Divine Incantation Sutra* in their homes shall have all evil ghosts barred from reckless approach.”

“Why is this so? All great demon kings dispatch divine warriors to guard this sutra. Heavenly beings, jade maidens, and immortals—hundreds of millions in number—also come to protect it, so that no ghostly soldiers dare approach recklessly.

The Dao spoke: “From this day forward, wherever this sutra is transmitted, if any evil ghosts or malevolent spirits dare harbor ill intent toward the living or the Dharma masters, the ghost kings and the eight hundred million great demon kings shall swear to suffer the Three Beheadings, their heads shattered into thirty thousand pieces.”

The demon kings declared: “From this day forward, if Daoists heal the sick, transmit the sutras, or perform meritorious deeds, we shall ensure their every endeavor succeeds, their every wish fulfilled, with no desire left unanswered. Should we violate this oath, we, your disciples—including the Sentence Lord’s Disciple—shall each suffer ten thousand beheadings.”

The Dao spoke: “From this day forward, as the Three Caverns’ teachings spread and perfected beings receive them, how much more so for the ignorant. Whoever upholds these Three Caverns’ sutras shall have ghostly soldiers aid them, their works accomplished, their deeds aligned, and the great demon kings protect them. You, Daoists, must diligently convert the ignorant. Those who receive these teachings shall become masters of the Three Caverns, traversing the world to deliver salvation. If one suffers a sudden illness, let the Daoist transmit the sutra and recite this divine incantation, and the thirty-six celestial demon kings shall summon all lesser ghost kings to lend their strength to the disciple.

The Dao spoke: “When Daoists receive this *Divine Incantation Sutra*, it must not be received alongside other sutras but separately. Why? Because the great demon kings within this sutra possess immense divine power, and thus it must not be mixed with others. It must be transcribed and stored in a separate case. Carry it with you, and ten thousand ghosts shall not draw near. When performing purification rites, employ boundless rituals.

The Dao spoke: “This *Divine Incantation Sutra* contains the names of all ghost kings, which is why the Most High esteems it. Wherever this sutra is transmitted, no evil ghosts may approach. Only the ancestral spirits, familial ghosts, and household deities of the living may remain; all others must not come recklessly. The great spirits within and beyond, all *wangliang* spirits, deities of life and death, auspicious male and female spirits, and tomb ghosts—from this day forward, banish them ten thousand *li* away. Should they disobey, you shall die ten thousand deaths, without mercy.”

The Dao spoke: “In the world, there are eighty thousand drowning ghosts, each three feet and two inches tall, moving in countless swarms to kill people in the waters. Those who do not believe in the Dao shall not be protected by benevolent spirits and shall die in vain. There are further ninety-eight myriad kinds of water-borne illnesses, thirty-two types of black, white, red, green, and yellow diseases that cannot be cured, and thirty-six kinds of sudden deaths—all afflictions of the sinful. The people of the world do not practice the Dao and law, bringing chaos to the land. Thus, the heavens gather the wicked, who refuse to contemplate goodness, and dispatch divine warriors to punish them with ten thousand diseases. From this day forward, where Daoists perform meritorious deeds and establish purification rites to save people, the demon kings shall all assist these Dharma masters in healing illnesses. If the affliction does not abate, the demon king Gao Linzhi’s head shall be shattered into ninety pieces.”

The Dao spoke: “You, all demon kings, from this day forward, if the men and women of the Middle Kingdom believe in the Dao, receive Our Three Caverns’ teachings, and propagate them across the ten thousand lands, healing the sick and transmitting the sutras wherever they go—you must convert the ignorant, assist in their meritorious works, turn back winds, and halt rains, preventing harm from approaching. Those who do so shall be elevated ten thousand ranks. Should you violate this oath, your heads shall be shattered into ninety pieces.”

The Dao spoke: “All divine kings and all demon kings, you share the same primordial *qi* of Non-Action as I. Yet your conduct differs, and in a hundredfold comparison, you do not equal even one part of Me. Though you possess great divine transformations, you remain My disciples. Why? Because you have not cultivated the natural Dao *qi* and have long harbored malevolent hearts, dwelling within the cycle of birth and death. It is only due to the great blessings accumulated in your past lives that you have attained the ranks of divine kings and demon kings. I, however, reside above the Three Heavens, governing all spirits. From past kalpas, I have pitied all beings as if they were My own children. My laws can give life to the good, perfect the good, slay the malevolent, and eradicate the wicked—not only among livestock and beasts, but also among the virtuous. Now, the great teachings of the Three Caverns spread throughout the world, and the good people of the land often encounter these scriptures. Where Daoists heal the sick and save people, you, demon kings, must assist them in their meritorious works, ensuring their vows are preserved and their virtues unbroken. Should you violate this oath, you shall be beheaded without mercy.”

The Dao spoke: “In the world, there are many great spirits and long-standing demon kings. You, too, share the same primordial *qi* of Non-Action as I. Yet your conduct differs, and in a hundredfold comparison, you do not equal even one part of Me. You have long submitted as My disciples, and your life and death rest in My hands. All people dwell within heaven and earth, yet many do not believe in the Dao. Now, the teachings of the Three Caverns spread throughout the world, and those who encounter these scriptures—where Daoists heal the sick and save people—you must assist them, ensuring their virtues are not broken. Should you violate this oath, you shall be beheaded without mercy.”

The Dao spoke: “The eight hundred million great demon kings, along with eight hundred million lesser kings, shall each proclaim this decree: from this day forward, wherever the Three Caverns’ teachings spread and Daoists heal the sick or transmit the sutras, you must all assist them. Ensure their treatments succeed, their works are accomplished, and heavenly beings protect them. Let winds and rains come in their proper seasons, without causing harm.”

Should any violate the precepts, showing disrespect for sacred words, and unleash their demonic soldiers to wrongfully kill good people or masters of the Three Caverns—causing unwarranted calamities, illnesses, or suffering, all contrary to their sworn oath—then the thirty-six demon kings, including Wuliuzi, shall be beheaded without mercy.

The Dao spoke: “Many in the land do not believe in the Great Dao. Those who receive the Three Caverns’ teachings—you must assist them, ensuring their good hearts ever flourish and never wane. Protect them, and heavenly beings shall come to their aid. Since ancient times, the people have suffered myriad illnesses, not merely one kind, afflicted by a thousand ailments and ten thousand torments: headaches, bodily heaviness, limbs that cannot be lifted, disorientation, vomiting, bloody rashes, and qi disorders. I know well the names of your ghosts—Rishen You’ai Zi, Jiao’er Pingwang, Axin of the Three Karma—and the thousand and ten thousand ghosts. Quickly withdraw your lesser ghosts and let the sick recover. Should they not recover, your heads shall shatter into eighty pieces.”

The Dao spoke: “In the *jiazi* cycle of years, seventy-two kinds of illness shall arise. The Xianbei in Chang’an shall slaughter the people wantonly. The south of Chu shall fall into ruin, its people scattered to other lands. Two barbarian hordes and the Three Hao shall unite to contend for it. Wise ministers in the lands east of the Yangtze shall once more aid the realm. The world shall know no joy; the people shall sigh in bitterness, and the lowly shall grieve. Wandering spirits shall come daily to claim lives, and the people shall perish utterly. Among them, if even one or two receive the teachings and practice the Dao, evil men shall mock them. Thus, immortals shall not appear, and the world shall know no immortals.”

The Dao spoke: “In the *jiaxu* cycle of years, the people of the land shall flee together to the lands east of the Yangtze, swarming around Chang’an. In Shu and Han, thirty thousand red demons shall slaughter the people, for they do not believe in the Dao. I once sent Dong Xuanko and Yin Zhongkan to transform the foolish of the world, yet the foolish did not believe. What is to be done? Heaven shall now send one hundred and twenty kinds of illness to kill them. If there are masters of the Three Caverns’ scriptures who come to transmit these divine incantations, the dead shall live again. I hereby command all demon kings and lesser kings: wherever a master heals the sick, you must restrain the lesser ghosts and let the sick recover. If they recover, you shall be promoted. If they do not, you shall die.”

Swiftly, swiftly, as the command of the Most High—so be it by law!

The Dao speaks: In the *jiashen* cycle of years, the world shall see forty-nine myriad black ghosts slaughtering people, many meeting violent deaths. When the time of *zi* and *chou* arrives, the appointed day shall draw near, and a great slaughter of eighty myriad red soldiers shall come to claim the people—yet the people shall not know. In the years *renwu*, *guiwei*, and *jiashen*, great floods shall drown the land, and plague and war shall gather. The great ghost king Jiang Gongyan shall come with them to kill. From this day forth, if lesser ghosts dare to afflict the sick, they must flee a thousand *li* at once. Should they refuse to depart, the great demon kings shall shatter their heads into eighty fragments.

The Dao speaks: In the *jiawu* cycle of years, thirty-six myriad Qiang and Hu ghosts of the Liao shall come to slay the people. Seventy myriad red crows shall fly across the heavens, and those who see them shall fall ill with plague, beyond all cure. For they do not believe in the sacred teachings, and thus they shall die of sickness. From this day forth, wherever in the land a single person receives the scriptures and transmits these divine incantations, the great demon kings and heavenly beings shall come to aid them, and the sick shall recover of themselves. If they recover, you shall be promoted ten thousandfold. Should they not recover, you, the great kings and lesser ghosts, shall be hewn into ten thousand pieces without mercy.

The Dao speaks: In the *jiachen* cycle of years, the world shall suffer ninety kinds of illness. Many shall die suddenly, and the six livestock shall be stricken with pestilence—for the people do not believe in the Great Dao. If one person receives the scriptures and practices the Dao, the foolish shall mock them. Therefore, Heaven shall dispatch thirty-nine thousand great ghosts to punish them, and the people shall fall ill as plague ghosts come to kill. If there are masters who transmit these divine incantations, eighty myriad billions of mighty heavenly warriors shall come to their aid. Should the sick not recover and die, the great demon kings shall first seize the lesser ghosts. Swiftly restrain your underlings, and do not harm the good people. This is proclaimed to all below—there shall be no pardon.

The Dao speaks: In the *jiayin* cycle of years, sixty kinds of illness shall strike, and nine out of ten shall die. Wang Jian shall lead them, bringing violent chaos upon the people, along with the red crow ghosts. From this day forth, wherever a Daoist transmits this scripture, the sick shall recover of themselves. Should they not recover and bring misfortune upon the people, the great ghost kings shall first seize the lesser ghosts and shatter their heads into forty-nine fragments.

The Dao speaks: The world is filled with wicked people, unfit for the abode of the sacred. Yet when a Daoist establishes the teachings of the Three Caverns, heavenly beings shall all come to protect them. From this day forth, if there are those gravely ill and in peril, the great demon kings shall sever the lesser ghosts of their households, and the sick shall recover of themselves. If they recover, the great demon kings shall ascend. If they do not, you shall be hewn into ten thousand pieces. There are countless lesser ghosts in the world—depart at once, and do not let the living die. Should you disobey this teaching, I shall now dispatch forty-nine myriad millions of red *ding* envoys to slay the great demon kings—there shall be no mercy.

Swiftly, swiftly, as the command of the Most High—so be it by law!

The Dao speaks: From the twenty-ninth day of the eleventh month in the *renwu* year to the third day of the tenth month in the *renchen* year, seventy-two myriad lesser ghost kings shall roam into people’s homes, spreading swift and grievous illness—all shall suffer. Li Xin and Li Ling, each leading forty myriad troops, shall come to claim lives. I now know your names—flee at once! Here, seventy-two myriad red slayer-warriors shall hew you. If you do not flee swiftly, your bodies shall be shattered into ten thousand fragments without mercy—depart ten thousand *li* at once!

The Dao speaks: The Daoist teachings take the Three Caverns as their foundation. Only by receiving these divine incantations may one enter the mountains or the world of men to slay all ghostly marauders. Without this text, ghosts shall not fear mortals. Now, thirty-six myriad violent ghosts come to kill—I know your names. Flee a thousand *li* at once!

Swiftly, swiftly, as the law commands.

*Scripture of the Divine Incantations of the Most High Cavern Abyss, Scroll the Second—Concluded*
*Scripture of the Divine Incantations of the Most High Cavern Abyss, Scroll the Third—Chapter on Binding Ghosts*

The Dao speaks: From this year of *wuyin* in the *guiwei* epoch, the great kalpic turn arrives. Wicked men disbelieve in the Daoist teachings, so Heaven dispatches plague ghosts to inflict seventy-two kinds of disease, slaying the evil. The world is vast, yet ghostly soldiers spread their poison—what is to be done? What is to be done?

If there be those who uphold the Three Caverns, I shall dispatch four hundred ninety myriad warrior-enforcers to bind the unjust and perverse ghosts for these Dharma masters. Wherever Daoists save lives and traverse the land, demon kings shall assist in binding these ghostly soldiers.

The Dao speaks: The Jade Women of the Three Heavens, together with the consort of the Great Brahmā Heavenly King—eighty myriad in all—descend to hear the scripture and swear an oath, saying: "From this day forth, wherever people of the world have Three Caverns Dharma masters perform rites to save lives and recite this *Divine Incantation Scripture*, we shall protect them, preventing plague ghosts and all demonic spirits from harassing the Dharma masters. Should they refuse to depart, we shall be the first to suffer the consequences."

At that time, the Great Demon Kings of the Nine Heavens, along with eighty myriad Jade Women, all descend together and address the Most High, saying: "From this day forth, wherever Daoists recite this scripture to save the sick, if any ghost comes to obstruct them and refuses to leave, we shall bind them together, ensuring the Dharma masters remain undisturbed and the sick recover. Those who recover do so by our power, and the multitude of sages rejoice." The demon kings each swear to bind the plague ghosts.

Then the Most High recites a gāthā:
*"Now I proclaim the divine incantations,
The spirits of the spells shall all be destroyed.
Those slain have their own masters,
For evil deeds, none shall be spared.
You have all sworn submission,
Come together to hear my scripture.
From this day, assist the Dao,
Each and every one, lend your aid.
Do not again conspire in malice,
Nor together plot wicked schemes.
If you plot wicked schemes,
The warrior-enforcers shall bind your spirits.
Boiled in cauldrons, burned by fire,
You shall ascend and descend the Knife Mountain’s pavilion.
If you follow goodness,
You shall not suffer such torments."*

The Dao speaks: In the *renwu* year, thirty-nine thousand red ghosts shall come to slay the wicked. Those who encounter Three Caverns Dharma masters shall have plague ghosts driven a thousand *li* away. From this day forth, for those afflicted by imprisonment or illness, merely recite this scripture. This scripture commands eighty myriad great spirits, thirty myriad warrior-enforcers, forty myriad Jade Women, and thirty myriad youths—all shall come together to guard wherever the scripture is recited, and demon kings shall bind the plague ghosts.

The Dao speaks: Long ago, in the Dark Radiance Palace of the Five Marchmounts, I expounded the *Samādhi Scripture* for all sentient beings. At that time, seven heavenly demon kings, thirty myriad in number, descended as one and swore: "From this day forth, wherever Dharma masters save the sick and recite this *Divine Incantation Scripture*, we shall clear the path, allowing no evil to approach. Evil ghosts shall flee far, and heavenly beings shall come to assist. Those who can be cured shall have their illnesses dispelled, and those imprisoned shall all be freed. If we fail to bring benefit, we shall willingly accept execution by waist severance, even in death having no regrets."

The Dao speaks: After the *renwu* year and the *xinsi* year, there shall surely come plague ghosts, eighty myriad in number, to slay the wicked. The wicked do not believe in the Dao. Thus, the Jade Women of the Three Heavens and the Great Brahmā Kings of the Nine Heavens—thirty-six myriad in all—descend together and address the Most High, saying: "From this day forth, wherever Dharma masters traverse, we shall protect them, ensuring the sick recover and those entangled in official matters swiftly gain resolution. If plague ghosts again scheme to harm the good people, we shall bind them as well."

The Dao speaks: From this day forth, those who uphold the Three Caverns shall have seven hundred myriad celestial soldiers of the Nine Heavens and seven hundred myriad Great Demon Kings of the Thirty-Six Heavens, each coming to protect these Dharma masters. For households afflicted by illness or official matters, hasten to recite this scripture. This scripture possesses great spiritual power, naturally dispersing official troubles and curing the sick. Should any refuse to submit, the Demon Kings of the Three Heavens shall come to bind them. Plague ghosts and red soldiers shall perish utterly, and the malevolent spirits of calamity—both within and without—shall be driven ten thousand *li* away. Warrior-enforcers from the ten directions shall shield the Dharma masters.

Then the Most High recites a gāthā:
*"The Great Vehicle of the Three Caverns,
The true principle declares itself.
Without eons of cultivation,
None may receive and hear it.
Recite and save the suffering masses,
Dispelling the hordes of ghosts.
Heavenly perfected ones surround and protect,
Demonic spirits dare not approach.
Should any violate the Dharma,
Their bodies shall be shattered into a hundred fragments."*

Another gāthā:
*"The Great Elephant is originally formless,
The scripture’s words become the Dao.
As the Dao turns within the formless,
No demon or devil shall not be swept away.
Purity and turbidity each have their place,
Heavenly officials come to examine.
You, who act with cruelty and treachery,
Cause me constant sorrow and vexation.
Bound in reverse, your heads shall be torn,
Embrace the Sword Trees—let this be your fate."*

The Dao speaks: Now I observe the world—wicked men multiply, the Six Barbarians invade one another, and they mutually destroy. By the *renwu* year, the world shall be in turmoil, the people unsettled. Blade and soldier, plague and *qi*, shall slay the wicked. The wicked do not believe in the Great Dharma, thus they are made to die.

From this day, those who uphold the scriptures of the Three Caverns shall attain transcendence as Upper Immortals. The people of the world are foolish and ignorant. They see Daoists die and the wicked die, yet fail to distinguish the difference, seeing only that both die, with no distinction. The wicked die to enter the Three Evil Paths. Daoists die to be reborn in heaven or among men, or to become great kings, or to ascend as immortals, never to be born in evil realms. Some ascend as immortals in broad daylight, having taken elixirs for a thousand years, first attaining youthful vigor. Those who uphold the Three Caverns, honor their teachers, receive the scriptures, endure hardship in practicing the Dao, and attain this immortality shall never die, even after ten thousand kalpas.

From this day forward, wherever Daoist priests save people, demon kings and their kind shall gather to seize and bind ghostly spirits.

The Dao speaks: In former times, I was among thirty thousand Chinese immortals, including Dongyue Zhilianzi, each holding the implements of faith to receive the scriptures. We ascended the mountains to build altars and pay homage to the Five Emperors of the Five Directions. To pledge our faith, we broke a silver ring, dividing it as a contract. We drank the cinnabar elixir with our masters and swore an oath, saying: "Today we drink the elixir, receive the scriptures, and make offerings, vowing never to transgress for life. For those afflicted by illness, urgent calamities, misfortune in their homes, disputes and lawsuits, or prisoners in jail, we shall recite the scriptures and perform fasts. All shall follow the purifying rites of the fast, and Daoist priests shall make this their constant practice." The immortals, having received and transmitted the scriptures, spread transformation throughout the land, curing the illnesses of the myriad people. All ghost kings then concealed themselves in hiding.

The Dao speaks: Many in the world do not believe in the Dao. When one person receives the scriptures, the multitude laughs at them, saying: "These demonic beings do not wish to live; they flee into the mountains to avoid people and do not seek official rank." They do not know that such a person was born from heaven, seeing the world’s defilement and filth, and seeks the Dao of immortality to deliver all people. Yet people, failing to recognize the truth, instead mock them. Alas, alas! Such people shall later incur grave sins, their transgressions plunging them into the scorching fires and boiling waters of the Red-Linked Hell, where they shall remain for three thousand billion kalpas without hope of release. Once their punishment is complete and they are reborn as humans, they shall possess human form but lack human sentiment. Some shall be foolish, deaf, mute, or unable to comprehend human affairs. Others shall be reborn as the six kinds of livestock, eating grass and drinking water, their flesh offered to humans. From birth, they shall endure hardship and suffering, with no one to whom they may appeal. Such is the cycle of these sinners, without end. Reflect upon my words, disciples.

At that time, the Most High then spoke a verse:
Obstinate and ignorant of the Dharma,
They see the world’s accumulators of sin.
Not only do they themselves refuse to believe,
But they mock those who cultivate the truth.
Unknowing that they came from heaven,
Soon they shall lie in the grass of men.
Disciples, you recognize nothing,
Yet together you pass judgment.
Words uttered, calamity enters,
Echo and response in but a moment.
In death, they receive the torment of poison,
Their sins bound in the Red-Linked Hell.
Turning through the Five Sufferings,
They face judgment for billions of kalpas.
Born without human sentiment,
Ensnared by the six afflictions.
Their bodies take the forms of livestock,
How could they again know form and spirit?
Their sins are not from cultivating the Great Vehicle—
How then could they escape bodily ruin?
Thus are the causes and conditions;
Reflect upon my words, disciples.

The Dao speaks: Many in the world harbor malicious intent and do not believe in true words. Heaven dispatches the generals of wanton slaughter—eighty million strong—to roam the world and seize these wicked people. Now, those who uphold the Three Caverns are protected by thirty thousand demon kings, who follow and shield them, aiding their deliverance. When they wish to perform a fast, on the day of its assembly, the skies shall be clear and bright, free from wind and rain, as heavenly beings assist them. Wherever Daoist priests go, people shall see and cherish them, their Dao-qi overflowing, warding off illness and pain. But those who curse and humiliate Daoist priests, bringing them disputes, lawsuits, or official deceit, shall have their souls and spirits seized and slain, to manifest the divine efficacy of the Great Dao. Hasten, hasten, as in the statutes and decrees!

The Dao speaks: In the world, there is the Ghost King Wuhuan, seven or eight feet tall, each commanding ninety million red-armored soldiers. Every month, they descend to take the qi and lives of people, causing unjust deaths throughout the land. During the *jiaxu* and *jiawu* ten-day periods, they descend to claim lives, spreading thirty-nine thousand kinds of disease that kill men, women, and children. From this day forward, wherever Daoist priests recite this scripture, you shall withdraw your soldiers and banish them ten thousand miles away. If you refuse, you shall be beheaded. Will the three hundred million soldiers of Wuhuan dare disobey?

The Dao speaks: During the *jiachen* ten-day period, the great demon kings of the Eight Thousand Nine Heavens, led by Weidu, descend with countless followers. Each month, they afflict people with nine thousand incurable diseases, joining forces with the death-generals and ghost-soldiers of the lower realms to slay humanity. From this day forward, restrain your ghostly soldiers and do not wrong the good people. Wherever male or female Daoist officials practice the Dao, you shall assist them. If you do not follow the Five Teachings, your heads shall be shattered into eighty fragments.

The Dao speaks: In the years *xinsi* and *renwu*, people shall die unjustly, the world shall be in turmoil, and the dead shall be many. The Ghost King Wuhuan and the red-qi of the underworld shall kill people, spreading widespread pestilence. In every household, three or four out of ten shall perish. Alas, alas! Only by holding grand purifying fasts in every village, paying homage to the gods of the Five Emperors, and protecting one’s household shall the heavenly gods take notice. Then the Ghost King Wuhuan shall submit and no longer kill.

The Dao speaks: From the moment one receives this scripture and the master provides guidance, if there is illness, perform a fast. For lawsuits, prisoners, homes haunted by many ghosts, stagnant official careers, or failed harvests of fields and silkworms, perform this fast. When this fast is held, heavenly beings shall come to protect you, and all your wishes shall be fulfilled without a single misfortune. Those who uphold this scripture shall cause ghost kings to submit. From this day forward, wherever the Dharma Masters of the Three Caverns practice, ghost kings shall protect them. If any Daoist priest falls ill, your heads, O ghost kings, shall be shattered into eighty fragments.

The Dao speaks: In the year *gengchen*, the ruler must be vigilant, and his ministers must assist him, so that the world shall be vast and all shall stand in awe. Yet petty men shall oppress one another, and the noble shall lack the Dao. Ninety kinds of disease shall afflict the world, killing the wicked. The Ghost King named Tanzhi shall lead thirty-six ghost kings, while the Great Demon King of the Seven Heavens, the Luminous Lord, shall descend to spread myriad diseases, all incurable. At that time, the wicked shall be many, and most shall not believe in the Dao.

Those who receive the scriptures—if they receive the Three Caverns—shall be protected by the Great Demon Kings and their forty-nine hundred million followers, who shall descend to assist these Dharma Masters.

The Dao speaks: When these Three Caverns Dharma Masters enter the gates and dwellings of the people, the myriad ghosts shall flee from them. They shall heal the sick and save the people, and none shall fail to recover. It is because the wicked are many that ghosts are permitted to kill. The Most High, in great compassion, pities all sentient beings and thus gazes upon these ghost kings, commanding them to restrain the myriad poisons.

From this day forward, if any Daoist priest encounters misfortune or falls ill, the heads of these ghost kings shall be shattered into eighty fragments.

At that time, the Most High spoke this verse:
The Dao’s law is true within the true,
Within the true, there is numinous power.
When the Three Caverns enter a person’s gate,
The myriad ghosts all vanish without form.
Demonic and false, turbid and impure,
The nature of the Dao is originally pure.
Saving and protecting all people,
Universally aiding all sentient beings.
The Most High extends great compassion,
Dispelling the armies of heavenly demons.
The myriad poisons restrain their qi,
Unable to expend your essence.
Heads shattered into eighty fragments,
Delivered to the Heavenly Soldiers.
The Heavenly Soldiers shall sever and cut,
For crimes incurred, there is no pardon.
The Most High has no self or other,
Distinctions make the Dharma clear.

The Dao speaks: The world is full of foolish people, for the sages do not instruct them. From this day forward, great floods shall come, approaching the misfortune of warfare. Within the realm, those who do not believe in the Dao shall wrongfully disturb the myriad people. The myriad people, distressed and suffering, not diligent and unaware, shall only appeal to the Most High. Fearing that ghost kings shall wrongfully kill and that the world’s good people shall perish, the Three Caverns scriptures are expounded to transform the world.

From this day forward, if any Daoist priest encounters wrongful misfortune, I shall assist them, ensuring that Daoist priests suffer no legal punishments, slander, or illness. Should they one day fail to act according to the law, the Great Demon King shall seize the people, and the ghost kings Wuhuan and their million followers shall have their heads shattered into twelve fragments.

The Dao speaks: From the year *renwu* onward, those in the world who received the Dao numbered thirty-nine thousand. In Qingzhou and Qinchuan, men and women who attained immortality included Wang Fang, Zhang Xuan, Du Gui, Shu Han, Luo Dao’an, Fei Touran, Li Ying, Zhang Shi, Sun Hongmei, Hou Jin, and Yuan Dao. In the year *jiashen*, they attained immortality. Each ghost king shall protect and assist these followers of the Three Caverns, ensuring they suffer no illness.

If any person harbors anger toward a Dharma Master, curses, humiliates, strikes, schemes to kill, or plots harm against them, such persons shall be utterly destroyed, their households extinguished. For seven kalpas, they shall have no form, drifting with the wind, clinging to rain, depending on dust, and attaching to grass. Only after ten thousand kalpas shall they regain human form.

The ghost kings shall protect and assist these Three Caverns Dharma Masters. If any do not believe my words, the Great Demon King Fudan and Wuhuan shall have their heads shattered into ninety fragments.

The Dao speaks: The thirty-six great demon kings and their ghosts, when the people of the realm do not believe, shall descend from heaven to protect those who uphold the Three Caverns. The Great Demon King and all ghost children shall guard them. If Daoist priests perform rituals to heal the people, you shall dispel evil qi, allowing the Daoist priests to cure illnesses swiftly.

From this day forward, those who do not submit shall have the heads of the great ghost kings Wuhuan and their followers shattered into eighty-nine fragments.

The Dao speaks: The ghost of gates and doors is named Chengbo; the ghost of opening and closing is named Alunran; the ghost of wells and stoves is named Zhenlianzi; the ghost of the four fences is named Shibogong; the ghost of the road is named Wuziding; the ghost of houses and dwellings is named Xuanzidu. Together, they descend, encircling people’s homes and dwellings ten thousandfold, not for the sake of one, but to harm the myriad people for a long time.

From this day forward, they shall be banished ten thousand miles away. If they seek to afflict people with illness, the heads of these ghost kings shall be shattered into twelve fragments.

At that time, the Most High spoke this verse:
I warn you, ghosts of gates and doors,
And you, spirits of wells and stoves.
You who wander the fences,
Do not harm the good people.
If you wish to do evil,
The wind’s power shall dissolve your bodies.
You should only assist the Dao’s transformation,
Banishing the lords of evil ghosts.
Do not again reveal your malevolent hearts,
Summoning the hordes of corpse-demons.
If you submit to the oath,
You shall be favored from time to time.
If you do not obey the command,
Your bodies and heads shall be sundered.

Another verse says:

The Dao’s natural law rewards the good and punishes the rebellious.
When the rebellious are punished, rebellion dissolves—
do not let them be severed from the Way.
Though you may wish to do evil,
the true Dharma will surely impose its reckoning.
Wielding authority, it commands the heavenly hosts,
exterminating all perverse and deviant forces.
If you depart of your own accord,
you may yet escape this calamity.

The Dao declares: In the world there are one hundred thousand Red-Linked Ghosts,
each three feet and six inches tall, numbering one million.
There are three hundred thousand Long-Headed Ghosts,
each brandishing a red staff, staff-slaying the myriad people.
From the ren-wu year to the ren-chen year, they kill humans—
then the great floods shall come.
If kings do not govern, the people will die violently;
in the jia-shen disaster, all shall perish utterly.
Alas, what is to be done?

Daoists transform the foolish,
guiding them to receive the Three Caverns—
only thus may they escape the nine calamities.

The Dao declares: The world is in chaos, the people perish utterly,
mostly slain by the ghost kings.
The good do not die; the wicked enter the Three Wretched Realms.
From this day forward, those who die unjustly—
Heaven too shall aid them.

From this day forward, those who become Daoist masters of the Three Caverns Dharma
shall be protected by the Great Demon Kings.
If any Daoist suffers peril, distress, or illness,
the ghost kings shall bear the guilt,
their heads shattered into eighty fragments.

The Dao declares: From this day forward,
ghost kings must not unjustly kill the myriad people.
Where Daoists travel to perform scriptures and heal the sick,
you must assist in their cure—do not let them remain unwell.
If they do not recover, it is because you ignored my words,
unjustly killing the good.
Your heads shall be shattered into one hundred and twenty fragments.

Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the Most High’s command,
dissolve disaster and protect the people—such is the ordinance.

*Thus concludes the third scroll of the* Most High Dongyuan Divine Incantations Sutra.
*Here begins the fourth scroll of the* Most High Dongyuan Divine Incantations Sutra.

**Chapter on Slaying Ghosts**

The Dao declares: Since the time of Fuxi, those who perished in ruined armies and defeated battalions, whose forms were maimed in battle, who died by the stench of blades and weapons—countless in their multitudes—have become wandering spirits. Some lie as exposed corpses, their bones disjointed, heads severed from bodies. Some drift or soar, their spirits unable to gather. Some have bodies without heads, feet without hands, mouths without eyes. By the thousands and tens of thousands, they roam and linger, clinging to themselves. They dwell by mountains and lean on trees, seizing the years of human lives. Unaware of their presence, people are plagued by strange disturbances, their hearts unsettled. These ghosts seek to wreak havoc, draining silkworms and fields, bringing every misfortune. They vex households, spawn strange omens, and afflict the living with illness—young and old alike—causing livestock to die suddenly, disputes and legal troubles to arise, and fires and floods to strike repeatedly, rendering all inauspicious. These are none other than the ghosts of those who died untimely in the mortal world, along with Li Ziao of the Clouds, who drift between the heavens and the shores of the sea, riding winds and mounting sparrows, snatching chickens and dogs. Birds and beasts act as portents, cutting short human lives to demand blood offerings. Folk diviners, through their divinations, terrify the living, claiming that deceased kin conspire in these calamities, thus giving rise to vulgar superstitions. When you lesser ghosts hear this, you seize the opportunity to hurl stones with reckless force, ensuring none remain unharmed, heaping misfortune upon misfortune, bringing ruin to the people. You boast: "Since your time, half of humanity has died unjustly."

From this day forward, the Great Demon Kings—forty-eight billion in number, each ruling over eight billion lesser kings—shall issue their decrees to gather all the lesser ghosts of the world. When a host falls gravely ill, teetering on the brink of death, you must swiftly seize the ghost afflicting them and banish it a thousand *li* away. Should you disobey, I shall dispatch the Great Slayer Generals—nine hundred million strong—to pursue and slay you without mercy. The Demon Kings shall hasten to apprehend you.

The Dao declares: From this day forth, if any ghost spreads slander among the living, the officials of the Great Yin—one hundred forty thousand strong—shall slay you, the *tuo* ghosts. If any ghost brings legal troubles, imprisonment, or shackles, the Venerable Lord shall send seventy-two thousand to execute you, the ghosts bound by wooden fetters and cangues. If any ghost stirs the *qi* of water or fire, I shall command Song Xianwen to lead the Generals of Wind and Water—two hundred eighty thousand strong—to annihilate you. Thus shall the *dingling* ghosts of shattered tiles, the *shantu muzi* ghosts of ominous trees, the *dayang zousi* ghosts of great calamity, the ghosts of livestock in human form, the *wumu baimei* ghosts of a hundred demonic woods, the *manyidi liao* ghosts of barbarian tribes, the *beidi qianglu* ghosts of northern savages, the ghosts of mountains, the ghosts of valleys, the ghosts of water, the ghosts of fire, the *shegong* ghosts of ten thousand kinds, the ghosts of twelve chaotic illnesses, the ghosts of livestock and servants, the ghosts of self-inflicted death, and all other great and small ghostly minions be driven a thousand *chi* into the earth.
