Never again shall you afflict the living with illness or legal strife; your ghostly *qi* shall disperse of its own accord. Should you refuse to depart, you shall be slain without mercy.

The Dao declares: From this day forward, when Daoists treat the sick and the patient’s family comes to summon you, first craft talismans to place upon the twelve earthly branches, doors, wells, and hearths, each inscribed in cinnabar and hung in its proper place. Then prepare twenty-one talismans for ingestion, to be taken by the patient thrice daily, including three times at night. Thrice daily, the Daoist shall face north in the central courtyard, recite the oral scripture, and perform the *zhuanjing xingdao* ritual, pacing the void in three intervals. If unable to conduct a grand fast, simply follow the Daoist in pacing the void thrice daily. If a grand fast can be held, all must proceed according to the proper method, including the recitation of almsgiving. Almsgiving allows celestial spirits to benefit humanity. Without almsgiving, the spirits of the scriptures will not protect, and the sick shall not recover.

**Sixteen Talismans**
Inscribe in cinnabar on white silk, and affix them according to their respective directions.

**First and second talismans** are to be affixed to the main gate. **Third** on the door. **Fourth** at *mao* (east). **Fifth** at *xun* (southeast). **Sixth** at *wu* (south). **Seventh** at *kun* (southwest). **Eighth** at *you* (west). **Ninth** at *qian* (northwest). **Tenth** at *zi* (north). **Eleventh** at *gen* (northeast). **Twelfth** in the central courtyard. **Thirteenth** above the hearth. **Fourteenth** above the privy. **Fifteenth** in water, to be ingested by the patient. **Sixteenth** should be inscribed as twenty-one talismans, to be taken thrice daily.

The Dao declares: Now there are the Great Masters of the Three Caverns, the most exalted of all masters. Among the Three Realms, if there are Daoist men or women who receive this, the Ghost Kings shall protect them. They shall cure all illnesses, and neither humans nor ghosts shall suffer harm. From this day forward, if there are Daoists who recite this scripture yet illnesses remain uncured, official ranks unchanged, or legal entanglements unresolved, the Ghost Kings, the Azure Perfected, and the Great Demon Kings shall shatter their heads into twelve pieces.

The Dao declares: All ghosts of the ten directions, every true or false spirit, the eighteen thousand *qi* of the Dao, and the thirty-six myriad red ghosts—from this day forward, each of you must gather your subordinate soldiers and pierce them through. Drive them away ten thousand *li*, lest they afflict the people with illness, including the local earth spirits. Where Daoists recite the scriptures, illnesses shall spontaneously heal, and all wishes shall be fulfilled. If even for a day they do not act according to the method, you great Ghost Kings shall shatter your heads into thirty pieces.

The Dao declares: The illnesses of people in this world are caused by Lianzi and his followers, for Heaven has dispatched twelve kinds of mighty warriors to seize them. From this day forward, when the Masters of the Supreme Three Caverns and Daoist priests save the sick by reciting scriptures and pacing the Dao, if the households of men and women holding fasts do not assist the Daoists, causing the sick to remain uncured, they shall be executed without mercy.

The Dao declares: Lianzi and his eighty million followers specialize in spreading toxic *qi*, afflicting people with severe pestilential illnesses. Now, three hundred sixty thousand Lianzi followers descend to cause eye diseases. From this day forward, gather your subordinates and sever them. If they do not depart, the Ghost Kings shall shatter their heads into sixty pieces.

The Dao declares: There are no truly good people in the world; good people descend from Heaven. Kings who greatly believe in the Dao also come from Heaven. Those who now uphold the Three Caverns must have profound karmic connections from past lives, which is why they now hear and see this. From this day forward, wherever Daoists propagate the teachings, the Ghost Kings shall pursue and assist them, curing the sick and preventing death. If even for a day they do not act according to the method, they shall be executed without mercy.

The Dao declares: People in the world do not believe in the Great Law, which is why there are so many sinners. Sinners enter hell, where ghostly soldiers run amok, unable to distinguish good from evil. Now, those who receive the Dao shall have the Great Demon Kings—Zizhen, Konglun, Marshal Mayan, and Chongqi Yuan—each assist and empower them, strengthening their resolve in the Dao. Kings shall uphold it, enlightening the foolish. Where Daoists treat illness, demonic *qi* shall withdraw of its own accord, driven away a thousand *li*. Those who do not submit shall be executed by the Demon Kings without mercy.

The Dao declares: The ghosts of the ten directions are all under the command of the Demon Kings. From this day forward, they must not unjustly kill the good or righteous, nor hide by day and move by night to abduct men and women. Where Daoists practice, the Ghost Kings shall assist, preventing evil people and malevolent ghosts from offending the Daoists. If any ghosts or humans harbor ill intentions toward Daoists, they shall all be executed, causing both humans and ghosts to perish, thereby manifesting the resolve of the Dao. These are the supreme words of the Most High—heed them well. If even for a day they are not obeyed, they shall be executed without mercy.

The Dao declares: Among the sinners of the world, there are eighty-nine kinds of killing ghosts. The great ghosts of mountains, forests, water, fire, wind, and earth—three thousand nine hundred in number—are led by the Great King of Harmonious Ghosts, who inflict ten thousand kinds of illnesses. The thirty-six kinds of ghosts of the six domestic animals are led by the Ghost King named Dunu, commanding eighty myriad lesser ghosts to spread malignant sores and bloody flux. There are also three thousand crow ghosts, led by the Ghost King named Wenqingzi, who spread red illnesses and white leprosy—diseases that cannot be cured. Those who commit evil, act rebelliously, and do not believe in the essentials of the Three Caverns shall all encounter these malevolent crows, which descend to inflict these diseases, rendering recovery impossible. From this day forward, wherever Daoists save the sick, illnesses shall be eradicated and cured, all wishes fulfilled, and the Ghost Kings shall be elevated to the rank of ten thousand merits.

The Dao declares: Within the Middle Kingdom, thirty-nine million people are destined for immortality. In the regions of Qin Chuan, Han Shu, and the Three Wu, among them are Sun Daoliu, Wang Zining, Tang Wansheng, Jiao Shizi, Liu Guang, Ma Chengqing, Xun Taichu, Sima Ping, Guo Xiu, Ding Tailun, Yue Fahu, Xie Ying, An Feihou, Wang Zilin, Yuan Boren, Yuan Sunzhi, and Daolin—three thousand in total—who followed Du Lanxiang to gather herbs and all arrived at the Wudang Palace. Now, Daoists who wholeheartedly receive the Three Caverns’ Law shall also encounter these immortals. Daoists must strive to save all people in distress, ensuring their safety. Wherever you recite scriptures and pace the Dao, the Demon Kings shall submit of their own accord. If they do not submit, they shall be executed without mercy, time and again.

The Dao declares: The essentials of the Three Caverns’ Law lie in divine incantations. Why is this so? This scripture subdues all great Demon Kings, who dare not disturb it. From this day forward, wherever Daoists recite and practice the scriptures, the forty-nine Demon Kings—including Wuchuan, Lianzi, Wenjixiu, Fenglinzi—and their three thousand six hundred lesser kings shall each protect these Daoists, preventing any offense against them.

Should you act accordingly, you shall be elevated to ascend as immortals in the realm of non-action. If you fail to aid these Daoists, assist in evil, and disrupt the true Dharma, preventing Daoists from healing and leaving their work unfulfilled—should even a single day pass with such transgressions—the Demon Kings shall all be seated and executed without mercy. Each and every decree follows the oral command of the Most High, swiftly as law and ordinance.

The Dao declares: Throughout the world, there are four hundred ninety thousand malevolent ghosts who bring lingering death upon people, spreading ten thousand kinds of pernicious qi that slay the living. Yet when Daoists recite the scriptures, their afflictions cease. Kings, too, shall come to believe in the Dao, reverently receiving the Three Caverns’ Law, and their descendants shall inherit nobility.

The Great Demon King’s prince, Wuchun Linqi, with his eight thousand myriad followers, in the years of *renwu* and *guihai*, leads ten thousand ghosts to kill. Now that they know your names, from this day forward, they must not unjustly slay the innocent. Should any among the Great Demon Kings, lesser ghosts, Huixin, or Fen Yang’s followers act thus, they shall each be executed without mercy.

The Dao declares: In the *renchen* year within the Middle Kingdom, a True Lord shall appear in the world, with thirty million followers, yet only one shall preside. In that era, many men and women shall suffer illness. In the *renwu* year, he shall enter the mountains to exhort the foolish. Yet the foolish shall not believe in the Dao’s Law, nor receive the Three Caverns. Floods shall drown and slaughter, blades shall clash in war. Alas, what is to be done? Only those Daoists who receive the scriptures shall be protected by the Demon Kings, never meeting untimely death. They shall be tasked with healing the sick, and no illness shall remain uncured. Should they violate the Law even once, the Demon Kings’ heads shall shatter into eighteen pieces.

The Dao declares: Many in the world are wicked, unaware of the Dao, and those who witness it do not follow—thus, many perish. Now, the Three Caverns’ Dharma Masters are revered by both humans and ghosts. From this day forward, wherever Daoists recite scriptures and pace the Dao, the Demon Kings must not disturb them. Should they disobey even once, the Ghost Kings shall be hewn by the Heavenly Axe without mercy. Swiftly, swiftly, as the oral command of the Most High, the law and ordinance decree.

The Dao declares: Let this be proclaimed to all—thirty-six Heavenly Demon Kings, the Demon Kings’ sons, and all others—reverently receive and uphold it.

*The Wondrous Spell Scripture of the Most High’s Cavernous Abyss, Scroll Four* concludes.
*The Wondrous Spell Scripture of the Most High’s Cavernous Abyss, Scroll Five* begins.

**Chapter on the Prohibition of Ghosts**

The Dao declares: While I was in the Du Yang Palace, expounding the *Great Expulsion Scripture* to the royal daughters and guiding all beings, a Perfected One from the Central Kingdom, Tang Ping, came forth and reported: "Of late, deaths have been rampant and disorderly, their causes unclear. From this day forward, in which year shall the plague abate?"

The Most High replied: "From this day forward until the year *wuyin* and the year *renwu*, plague ghosts shall slay the wicked. Only by the year *jiawu* shall it cease. By the year *guiwei*, pestilential *qi* shall spread, and within the kingdom, blades and warfare shall arise—fathers and sons, rulers and ministers shall harm one another. The people shall grow ever more wicked, disbelieving in the Great Dharma. Those who receive and uphold the Three Caverns are all descended from Heaven, not born of this world."

The Dao declares: "From this day forward, if any Daoist receives these Three Caverns scriptures, diligently practices the Way, seeks the Dao, reveres the Three Honored Ones, and saves the foolish, I shall dispatch the Heavenly Soldiers of the Ten Directions and the Thirty-Six Heavenly Mighty Ones to shield and protect them. Wherever the Dharma Master presides shall be forbidden ground. If plague ghosts do not depart, the Mighty Ones shall strike them down one after another."

The Dao declares: "From this day forward, if any man or woman afflicted by plague hears this Dharma Master reciting the scriptures and listens with a single mind, their entire household reverently believing, then all misfortunes within and without—every malevolent spirit, mountain and forest sacrifices, cold hearths and hot hearths, and the ten thousand calamities of the household—shall be subdued of their own accord. If there are those who do not recover, disturbing and disrupting the households of the living, the Heavenly Soldiers, Mighty Ones, and the Four Brahmā Heavenly Kings shall come together to execute them. I now command the Demon Kings to restrain the plague ghosts and their offspring, bidding them only to transform people and uphold this scripture. The year *jiashen* draws near, and great disaster is not far off. Daoists must strive to save the common folk."

The Three Great Demon Kings of the Three Heavens descend as one and swear an oath: "From this day forward, wherever Daoists save people and perform the scriptures, if plague ghosts dare to harbor malicious intent, causing sudden illness and suffering, or bringing hardship and strife to the people and officials, I vow that my head shall shatter into eighteen pieces. Where Daoists transform people, I shall assist them; where there is illness, I shall aid in its cure. If there are disputes or legal troubles, I shall resolve them."

The Dao declares: "From this day until the year *xinsi*, plague ghosts shall surely harm the people, and the people shall perish entirely. Alas, alas! The people of the world do not believe in the Dao and its laws. The wondrous scriptures of the Three Caverns, when their Dharma spreads, shall elevate blessings to Heaven, and the Heavenly Ones shall come to their aid—thus shall they be spared. Yet the foolish, stubborn of heart, refuse to receive them. When the disasters of *jia* and *jia* arrive, floods shall drown them. After death, their regret shall be too late. The wicked grow ever more numerous, and Heaven shall send eight hundred million Red Slayer Great Ghosts to spread pestilence and execute them. By the year *renwu*, the world shall be engulfed in great waves, and ghostly soldiers shall come to slay the wicked. Daoists shall save them, and the Heavenly Ones shall protect them, forbidding the hundred ghosts."

The Dao declares: "During the *jiazi* decade, eight thousand Red Plague Ghosts and thirty-nine thousand more shall come to kill people. Those who know this and receive the Three Caverns from an enlightened Daoist, who recites the scriptures for them, shall naturally banish the plague ghosts. The name of the Ghost King is You Lian. His body stands thirty-seven feet tall, and in his hand he wields a red rope. Entering people’s homes, he incites quarrels and strife. From this day forward, wherever Dharma Masters perform the scriptures, he shall be forbidden."

The Dao declares: "In the year *jiaxu*, thirty-two kinds of illness shall afflict and kill the wicked. From this day forward, wherever Dharma Masters recite the scriptures, the Three Great Demon Kings of the Three Heavens shall come to forbid them, preventing them from killing people. In the year *jiashen*, seven hundred thousand malevolent ghosts shall come to kill people. If Dharma Masters are present to save them, the Heavenly Ones shall all come to assist the Daoists in restraining the plague ghosts."

The Dao declares: "In the year *jiawu*, eighty kinds of plague ghosts shall come to kill the wicked. The wicked do not believe in the Great Dharma and harm my Daoists, whom the Daoists cannot transform. In the years *jiachen* and *jiayin*, three hundred sixty thousand plague ghosts shall come to kill the wicked, for the wicked are many. Heaven shall dispatch Mighty Ones to descend and execute them. Daoists must swiftly transform the foolish. Yet the foolish do not believe—this is great delusion, and the deluded do not awaken. Alas! From this day forward, wherever there is plague or legal strife, I shall send the Three Great Demon Kings and the Masters of the Ten Directions to descend and execute them. Wherever this scripture of the Three Caverns is recited, wherever healing and salvation are sought, the ghosts shall be driven out and forbidden."

The Dao declares: "The Middle Mystery: Here, the Most High expounded the scriptures, already seated in the Ninefold Chamber of the Eightfold Radiance Palace, contemplating in stillness. Which kingdom suffers or prospers? How near or far is the kalpa’s end? The multitude of beings drift aimlessly—where do they turn? The Three Calamities loom, yet the foolish remain unaware, deceiving one another, wantonly slandering, rejecting true words, and scorning the virtuous. Seeing others do good, they mock them instead. They shall enter hell, where fire chariots and sword trees await—this agony is unbearable. How can they submit? They have brought this upon themselves; no one can take their place. I now perceive all transformations and see everything—how can they not obey?"

Then, for the sake of all beings, the Great Dharma Masters, the Daoist adepts of the Three Caverns, the Immortals of the Ten Directions, the divine officials of the heavens, the great demons of the eight quarters, and the male and female demon kings of the precepts and incantations were assembled—lest the people of the world suffer unjust death. The great flood approaches, yet none know of it. The demon kings were commanded to cease their unjust harm upon the myriad families, to instruct and transform the foolish, and to cause them to receive this scripture. This scripture, the sovereign of all scriptures, contains divine transformations and divine incantations in four scrolls. The Most High expounded it for the turbid and chaotic ages to come. If, in this world, there are those with karmic affinity who encounter this scripture, it will dispel their disasters. Those who receive it shall not be among the afflicted; heavenly beings shall come to welcome them, and they shall behold the True Lord.

The Dao declares: "The Supreme Clarity’s Immeasurable Samadhi enables one to ascend as an immortal. The divine transformations and divine incantations subdue all demons. When Daoists receive them, they shall fear no exorcism, whether in the mountains or among men. Receiving these twenty scrolls, one need not rely on other scriptures, for this scripture swiftly grants immortality."

Upon hearing this, the men and women in attendance rejoiced greatly. Each sought to receive the scripture, rising together to ask: "We do not yet understand—how should one receive this scripture? What offerings and rituals are required? We only wish for the Heavenly Worthy to instruct us fully. We shall uphold it faithfully, and if we come to know its ways, we shall prepare the proper offerings accordingly."

The Dao declares: "This scripture subdues demons and eliminates all disasters. Those who receive it shall not be harassed by demonic forces and shall naturally dwell in peace. If one is entangled in official matters, stricken by illness, or long mired in suffering, with no relief for months, upon hearing or seeing this scripture, their afflictions shall dissolve of themselves, and all calamities shall vanish. Those who receive it shall have immortals attend them. They shall revere their masters as the sun and moon, and cherish the scripture as pearls and jade. First, they must sacrifice to the Five Emperors of the Primordial Beginning, then break the covenant to receive it. Only afterward shall they transmit it in accordance with the teachings. In households afflicted by illness, Daoists shall perform the scripture’s recitation. When reciting, they shall first inscribe the eight talismans and place them upon the eight gates of the household. Then, for the family conducting the recitation and the Way’s practices, all inner demons and outer [obstructions] shall scatter and perish upon hearing these divine incantations. Benevolent spirits shall aid them, and myriad blessings shall gather upon their bodies. The guardian warriors of the scripture shall naturally protect them."

The Dao declares: "The great kalpa draws near, waters shall rise to ninety thousand [leagues], and at the convergence of the Three Calamities, demonic forces shall drive the people to their deaths. The world’s people shall perish entirely. Now, I ride the Azure Dragon, leading four hundred eighty thousand heavenly warriors and celestial soldiers to intercept the plague demons, cast down the demon kings, and descend into the world to transform and deliver the foolish, causing them to receive this scripture. Those who receive it shall have their names recorded by immortals in the Jade Register, escaping the nine perils of the water’s calamity. From this day forth, all who hear, receive, and uphold this scripture shall have forty billion heavenly soldiers and celestial warriors constantly follow them."

The Dao declares: "Now, the people of the Middle Kingdom receive these twenty scrolls of the Divine Incantation Scripture, which shall circulate everywhere. Daoists who receive this scripture shall all ascend as immortals. Even the Hu lands shall uphold it. From this day forth, if any man or woman receives and upholds this scripture, the great armies of the ten directions shall guard it, and eight hundred million warriors shall protect the scripture’s masters and recipients, ensuring they do not suffer unjust death, and that evil spirits dare not approach."

The Dao declares: "In this turbid and chaotic age, the people are largely wicked and do not believe in the Dao and its methods. Yet if even one person hears of this, rejoices, receives, upholds, and makes offerings to it, I shall dispatch armored soldiers, celestial warriors, and forty-nine billion red cavalry from the ten directions to constantly follow them, granting them wisdom, fulfilling their heart’s desires, elevating their official ranks, and bestowing a hundred blessings naturally, delivering them from the Three Calamities and nine perils."

The Dao declares: "The three revolutions draw near, demonic forces run rampant, and the great waters surge—do you not know this? The Most High grieves that all beings shall be ensnared within them. How can this not be sorrowful? Alas, alas! The world is turbid, its people false. Each must guide and transform, exhorting all beings to escape the three destinies. You Daoists—if you receive this scripture but do not instruct others, you shall perish. My words are not empty. The wise shall receive it and urge others to know it. From this day forth, those who receive and uphold it shall have heavenly beings protect and assist them, celestial warriors guard their gates, and the hundred evils and plague *qi* shall not disturb them."

The Dao declares: "From this day forth, if any receive these four scrolls of the Divine Transformation and Divine Incantation Scripture, I shall dispatch armored soldiers from the ten directions, merit-recording messengers, immortal maidens, and red chariot warriors to constantly follow those who receive the scripture, ensuring no evil befalls them. When the great calamity arrives, dragons shall rise to welcome them. Those who receive this scripture shall not suffer unjust death. If one is gravely ill, they shall receive this scripture. If entangled in official matters, they shall receive this scripture. If men or women are unwell, they shall receive this scripture. If a household suffers misfortune, they shall receive this scripture. This scripture is like medicine, capable of curing all ailments. You Daoists, believe in and receive it. If you heed my words, what further concern shall I have?"

The Dao declares: "Now, I command the demon kings of the ten directions: from this day forth, when those in illness, distress, or peril are saved by Daoists reciting this scripture, you shall protect them and not allow unjust harm. I sternly instruct the Registrar of Life and Death: where this scripture is recited, if the sick are fated to die, you shall grant them life. If their names are inscribed in the Stone Coffin or their death registers are sealed, you shall expunge them. For long illnesses or official entanglements, you shall examine and absolve them in accordance with my teachings. If any disobey my words and harm the innocent, the demon kings shall sever them into ten thousand pieces, cleaving their bodies into a thousand fragments without mercy. Beware, beware!"

The Dao declares: "In the final revolution of the kalpa, the world shall be brief and its people wicked, with many disbelieving in the Dao. Those who receive this scripture shall escape great calamities, and immortals and jade maidens shall attend them."

When the waters come in their fury, dragons shall rise to welcome them. Their ascent shall span eighty-four thousand *li* in breadth and length, and such ascents shall number four hundred and ninety thousand. As they rise to receive the people, those who are destined shall ascend without awareness of their own ascent. The world shall be vast with water, nowhere untouched—only those who have received this scripture shall escape.

The Dao declares: In the year *jiāxū*, men and women of the Central Kingdom who believe in the Dao and receive this scripture, entering the mountains to refine their essence in meditation, shall be beyond count. The great assembly, hearing the scripture, rejoiced and all sought to receive it. Three hundred thousand arose as one, circumambulating the Most High seven times and bowing thrice, saying: "We wish to receive this covenant." The Most High replied: "Excellent, excellent! I shall bestow it upon you."

The Dao declares: In this age of the Five Turbidities, people die unjustly in great numbers, and none believe in the Dao. Ghostly soldiers drive them away, and great disasters draw near, yet the foolish remain unaware. If you can receive and venerate these twenty scrolls of scripture, when the great flood comes, immortals shall come to welcome you, and you shall have no fear of death. If you trust my words, what cause have I for worry?

The Dao declares: From this day forward, those who receive my scriptural covenant shall have divine spirits assist them. Their households shall be naturally protected, and no evil shall befall them. You, the Daoist priests, must believe this and exhort all, that even the foolish may escape the Three Disasters. If any receive and uphold this scripture yet fail to cross the Three Rivers, I shall not be called a sage, nor shall I remain in this world to transform it.

I solemnly command the great deities of the ten directions, all malevolent ghosts, demon kings, and evil spirits: From this day forward, wherever this scripture is recited, all illnesses shall be cured, and official entanglements resolved. Those who receive this scripture shall have their ten thousand wishes fulfilled.

The great assembly, hearing the scripture, rejoiced, and each received the covenant to practice it.

The Dao declares: You, the Daoist priests, need only receive these twenty scrolls of the *Divine Incantation Scripture*, and you too shall attain immortality. Why? Because this scripture subdues all demon kings, and benevolent spirits guard it. Those who receive this scripture—if they possess the immortal bones of past lives, descended from heaven—are no ordinary mortals. Among the men and women of the Central Kingdom and the six barbarian tribes of later generations, there shall be those who submit to its transformation. In the land of Wu and Shu, many believe in the Dao. The wise of the four directions, scattered and displaced, shall enter the mountains. In the years *jiǎshēn* and *rénchén*, the inauspicious fate shall be known. Daoist priests, diligently exhort one another and transform all beings. Those who personally receive this scripture shall have the protection of heavenly beings and shall never die unjustly.

The Dao declares: Even if you have received the *Wondrous Treasure Scripture of the Infinite Samadhi of Highest Clarity*, without receiving this scripture, you shall not attain immortality. Without receiving this scripture, you shall not be called a Daoist priest, nor shall you be able to cure the ten thousand illnesses. But if you receive this scripture and venerate it in your home, all ghosts shall submit, and in life and death, you shall receive grace. The Dao does not speak falsely—believe this.

The great and small in the assembly each sought to receive it. The Most High, moved by compassion for all, bestowed the precepts upon them. You who receive this scripture must not slight your teachers, nor disdain the scripture. Uphold it throughout your life, contemplate the spirits, and meditate upon the Dao. Thereafter, you shall ascend as immortals, welcomed by nine dragons.

Hearing this, the great assembly leapt with joy in their hearts, each rising in astonishment to bow thrice. The Dao declares: When you receive this scripture, you must copy its scrolls and set a date to recite it in a quiet chamber or empty dwelling, seated in a high place. On the first and fifteenth days of the month, burn incense and pay homage to the ten directions, as well as to your teacher. If the teacher has departed, bow four times in the direction of their departure. If the teacher resides with you, go and pay homage.

The assembly, having received the teaching, each bowed thrice and pledged to practice it.

*The Fifth Scroll of the Most High’s Cavernous Abyss Divine Incantation Scripture*
*The Sixth Scroll of the Most High’s Cavernous Abyss Divine Incantation Scripture*
*The Vow [Chapter]*

The Dao declares: From this day forward until the years *jiǎxū* and *rénwǔ*, people will face widespread suffering, hardship, and death, wandering the lower realms, while the Dao’s *qi* daily grows in power. Its flourishing will center in the lands south of the Yangtze and within Han and Shu, where the Three Caverns’ teachings spread, and the six barbarian tribes perish entirely. Ghostly soldiers will run rampant, poisoning and harming the people, spreading pestilence to kill—no single region spared.

From this day forward, those who uphold this scripture shall be protected by Heaven, and even malevolent spirits that bring omens shall be bound by my vow. All demonic essences, I shall swear against. From now on, wherever a Dharma Master saves a person, legal disputes shall be resolved, and the sick shall recover. Should they not recover, the Most High shall dispatch three hundred forty-nine thousand Heavenly Valiant Warriors to seize and banish all malevolent ghosts—male and female—beyond a thousand *li*. Where Daoists administer healing, none shall fail to recover, for the great deities of the ten directions shall aid these Dharma Masters in curing illness.

The Dao declares: From this day forward, wherever those afflicted by illness encounter a Master of the Three Caverns reciting this scripture, all plague spirits shall flee ten thousand *li*, forbidden from causing disturbance. Legal cases and imprisoned convicts shall naturally dissolve. Should any refuse to depart, I shall send a thousand myriad Heavenly Valiant Warriors and Celestial Soldiers to descend and slay you.

The Dao declares: In the years *xīnsì*, *rénwǔ*, and *guǐwèi*, seventy-two kinds of disease shall ravage the world, killing the wicked. The wicked, for their disbelief in the Dao and its laws, shall be slain. From this day forward, wherever in the Middle Kingdom a Dharma Master saves the afflicted, I shall dispatch the Lords of the Nine Heavens to enforce this vow, banishing all malevolent ghosts beyond distant lands, forbidding them from harming those under the Dharma Master’s care. Swiftly, as the Most High’s decree from the Central Heaven commands! Should any disobey, the Heavenly Valiant Warriors shall descend to execute you, slaying without mercy.

The Dao declares: From this day forward, wherever a Daoist recites this scripture and practices the Dao for others, that place becomes the Most High’s Mystic Hall, where heavenly beings reside. All afflicted by legal troubles or pestilence shall recover, disputes shall cease, and prisoners shall be freed. Why? Because these are the Most High’s wondrous words, spoken from the Golden Mouth, and thus the Heavenly Valiant Warriors of the Three Heavens shall execute the plague spirits.

The Dao declares: Now, there are Dharma Masters who forsake worldly office, seeking the Three Caverns’ teachings and devoting themselves to the world. Witnessing its perils, they heal and relieve with single-minded devotion, aiding those entangled in legal troubles or illness. Such persons possess great blessings from past lives, their fortune flowing through the Middle Kingdom, destined to be reborn as teachers of all beings. Wherever I see such Dharma Masters healing and saving, I shall swear against all plague spirits—they shall not return.

The Dao declares: From this day forward, the world shall face great floods, and ghostly soldiers shall roam. In the years *jiǎxū* and *rénwǔ*, many Red Accumulation Ghosts shall spread across the Nine Provinces, twelve hundred commanderies, eighteen thousand counties, and three hundred million villages, slaughtering the good and virtuous, inflicting swift and grievous illness, causing the Most High’s true people to die unjustly. From now until the years *jiǎzǐ* and *rénchén*, calamity shall surge like ten-thousand-*zhang* waves. All these are your demonic ghosts—ancient dead generals, rulers, great ministers, lowly officials, lingering *qi*, worldly bandits, male and female [spirits of]... disasters of water, fire, blades, and warfare... wandering ghosts. When people fall into decline, these spirits vie to possess them, scheming to harm the people, seizing their reputations, craving their blood and offerings. Countless billions infest homes, manifesting strange lights, inciting disputes and legal troubles.

From this day forward, should any refuse my words and linger in these dwellings, the Great Generals of the Ten Directions’ Slaying Ghosts—three hundred thousand strong—shall slay you, permitting no delay. Swiftly, as the Most High’s oral command! Should any refuse to depart, the Demon Kings’ *Jūliúzǐ* and their two hundred thousand followers shall shatter your heads into twelve pieces.

The Dao declares: The Twelve Demon Kings of the Three Heavens’ *Jùpóqiāng*, one hundred twenty thousand strong, shall descend to the world. From this day forward, if any Red *Dīng* Fire Ghosts, each leading seventy-eight myriad followers, spread pestilence and wrongfully kill the good, the *Jiànhé* Official Soldiers—thirty-six thousand strong—shall seize and bind them, delivering them to the Nine Heavens’ prisons. Thus shall the world’s good people recover from illness, their households know peace, legal cases cease, all matters resolve, and disputes vanish. Those who seek shall attain the boundless bestowal of the Great Dao. Should you disregard my words, the Hundred-*Zhang* Ghost King shall behead you. Swiftly, as the Most High’s oral command and statutes! Should you disobey, you ghosts who harm the people, the Seven Heavenly Demon Kings shall shatter your heads into twenty pieces.

The Dao declares: In the years *jiǎxū* and *rénwǔ*, there shall appear Black-Foot Ghosts, their bodies thirty-six *chǐ* tall, their eyes red and yellow. Some transform into red crows, called *Zúrì*. They spread myriad diseases, flying in flocks to alight upon roofs, inflicting swift illness. The afflicted suffer yellowing bodies, alternating chills and fever, dripping discharge, red-and-black dysentery, scorched and ashen faces. They come and go unpredictably, refusing food and drink, vomiting when they try, blood and urine flowing together. Their eyes redden, their heads ache, their sinews spasm, their hands and feet convulse—all these are the work of Black-Foot Ghosts. This ghost king is named *Dàtóulú*, leading a horde of eighty million brothers. I know your names—depart a thousand *li* at once! Should you refuse, you shall be slain without mercy. Swiftly, as the statutes command!

The Dao declares: From this day forward, in the year *jiǎchén*, forty-nine myriad Black-Faced Ghost Kings named *Zhāngcháng* shall descend among the people, along with forty-six myriad billion followers, roaming the world to spread dysentery.

Should some suffer pain in chest, back, or waist, with water flowing from their eyes, or find their food and drink obstructed—these ghosts bring poverty to households, tongues tied in want. Ghostly soldiers encircle dwellings, cling to doorways, lurk in the four directions and eight corners, snatching the young, the old, and the frail. Corpses lie scattered in ruin—all the work of these ghosts. From this day forward, should you refuse to depart, the Wrathful Spirits shall slay you, and the Ghost Kings shall not spare you: your heads shall shatter into eighty-six pieces.

The Dao declares: Furthermore, two hundred thousand Red-Cord Ghosts shall come, led by a Ghost King commanding forty-nine myriad female ghosts. In spring, they seize men; in autumn, they take women; in winter, they claim the young; in summer, they harvest the old. By day, they lurk in waters; by dusk, they lie in wait near homes. They may seize livestock—oxen and horses—spreading their baleful poison, bringing poverty and incurable illness, claiming lives each day. From this day forward, flee swiftly. Should you refuse, your heads shall shatter into twelve pieces, and the Ghost Kings shall be executed.

The Dao declares: In the *jiǎzǐ* decade, thirty thousand White-Bottom Ghosts shall descend, their Ghost King named *Chìdū*, roaming the world to spread seventy-eight kinds of disease—all beyond cure. They drive men to raving madness, bloody dysentery, and festering swellings; blood pours from their mouths as they die, their breath restless and unsteady. When crows and magpies circle a home, these are the ghosts. They cause sudden, violent deaths across the land, untimely and unjust, afflicting men and women with grave illness. From this day forward, you Ghost Kings, gather your ghostly troops and depart. Should you refuse, you shall die, your heads shattering into thirty-eight pieces.

The Dao declares: In the year *jiǎxū*, the Red-Cliff Ghosts shall come, their bodies eighty *zhàng* tall, forty-nine billion strong in a single horde. They transform into great fish, seven *zhàng*, two *chǐ*, and three *cùn* in length, then shift into a million flying crows, descending upon the world to spread the *qi* of sudden death. They incite warfare, fill prisons with the condemned, bring reckless slander and strife, and inflict pain upon every household. This is the vengeance of the Ghost King *Yuànzhū*—swiftly gather your troops! From this day forth, be banished ten thousand *li* away.

Should you refuse to depart, your heads shall shatter into thirty pieces.

The Dao declares: In the *jiǎwǔ* decade of the year, there shall come the Yellow Ox Ghosts, their Ghost King named *Chìshí*. When they gallop forth, they become red-headed crows, ninety million strong. They enter the homes of men, seizing the young, the old. They spread ten thousand kinds of illness, their *qi* of disease thick and heavy. These are the harms wrought by the Earth Lord, who calls himself *Lǐ Zǐ’áo*. *Zǐ’áo* and his brothers, a thousand thousand myriad strong, conspire to slay men, killing without reason. From this day forward, flee swiftly to other lands. Should you refuse, bringing sickness and death to men, strife to households, and blight to fields and silkworms, you shall die. Ghost King *Chìshí*, your head shall shatter into ten thousand pieces.

The Dao declares: In the *jiǎshēn* decade of the year, there shall come the Ghost Kings *Méng Tián* and *Wáng Jiǎn*, each leading thirty thousand red ghosts to traverse the world. They incite men to quarrelsome *qi*, afflict them with foul dysentery, swollen faces and eyes, fullness in the chest, vomiting, and restlessness. They cause infants to cry in terror, bring official disputes and slander, cast men into prisons, and spread a thousand illnesses and ten thousand afflictions—poverty, distress, and hardship, children who do not survive, fields and silkworms that yield no harvest, and ten thousand unfulfilled wishes. All these are the works of the Ghost Kings *Wáng Jiǎn* and his kind. From this day forth, should *Méng Tián*, *Wáng Jiǎn*, and the others fail to gather their ghostly troops, their underling ghosts shall perish utterly, and the heads of the Ghost Kings shall shatter into eighty pieces.

The Dao declares: In the *jiǎxū* decade of the year, there shall come five nations of Ghost Kings, their ghostly troops the dead generals of *Sòng*, *Zhào*, *Yān*, *Wèi*, and *Lǔ*. Each king leads thirty-six thousand ghosts, roaming the lands of *Shǔ* and *Hàn*, seizing women, children, and old men from all under heaven, spreading forty-six kinds of illness to kill men. From this day forth, we know your names: Ghost King *Huáinánzǐ* has returned, along with *Bái Gōng*, *Hán Shè*, *Sòng Xiàn*, and *Wáng Shàn*. From this day forth, should you stir your underling ghosts to continue killing men, your heads shall shatter into seventy-eight pieces.

The Dao declares: In the *jiǎyín* year and decade, there shall come thirty-nine thousand ghosts, their Ghost King named *Jùliúbù*, each leading eight hundred thousand ghosts to descend and spread sixteen thousand kinds of illness, maladies beyond cure. They cause kings to falsely accuse their people, oppressing the myriad folk, leaving none whole. Neighboring states send raiders, evil ghosts enter homes, rendering dwellings uninhabitable—all these are the works of such ghosts. From this day forth, you Ghost Kings and your underling ghosts, gather your ghostly troops. Should you refuse to depart, the radiant might of the Heavenly Capital shall slay you without mercy. You must not allow the people of the world to suffer unjust death and illness—swiftly gather your ghostly legions!

Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances.

The Dao declares: Should the world descend into great chaos, with floods soon to come, the people shall toil in hardship. Receive the Dao to enlighten the foolish. Ghost Kings, upon seeing you receive the scriptures of the Three Caverns, follow the teachings of the Daoist masters, and come to guard and protect, they shall not dare to encroach upon you. Daoists, strive diligently: receive the *Tàiqīng Zhōngxuán*, and a hundred ghosts shall not draw near to men. Those who receive the *Sānmèi* shall naturally attain immortality; those who receive the *Dǎohuà* shall see demon kings submit; those who receive the *Dàqū Jīng* shall be aided by heavenly beings; those who receive the *Wúliàng Pǐn* shall behold the True Lords face to face; those who receive the records of immortality shall be protected by immortals; those who receive the *Huángtíng* shall have the Most High come to them. These are the true essentials of the Three Caverns.

Daoists, both men and women of worth, who receive these scriptures and practice them wherever they go, healing the illnesses of the people, shall find none that do not recover, and Ghost Kings shall submit of their own accord. Should they refuse, the Mighty Ones and *Huáng Yīng* shall strike them down one after another.

The Dao declares: The world is filled with evil men, and thus there are these evil ghosts who violently slay men. From this day forth, men and women who receive the teachings of the Three Caverns shall be revered by Ghost Kings, who shall not dare to offend them, and all people shall make offerings to them. Those who violate these Three Caverns Dharma Masters—whether by speaking ill, deceiving, reviling, scheming, striking, or plundering—shall have their bodies tormented, their descendants extinguished, and their seven generations of ancestors consigned to eternal darkness. By the oral command of the Most High:

Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances.

The Dao declares: From this day forth, those who suffer illness are your doing, you thirty-two Demon Kings, *Wūjiū* and the rest. You and your underling troops shall not spread poison to kill men. Should you refuse to depart, eight hundred million red-clad minor officials and the true riders of the Nine Heavens shall be dispatched to slay you. Swiftly gather your underling ghosts, make your ghostly troops submit, that the living may be at peace and the world be at ease. Why do you not depart? Demon Kings, your heads shall shatter into ninety pieces.

The Dao declares: There are nine hundred fifty thousand minor ghosts who come to kill men. Yet those of great fortune, Daoists who receive the incantations of the Three Caverns and come to recite them, shall be aided by the Ghost Kings. The Mighty Ones shall issue commands to repel these minor ghostly bandits, reconcile the ghosts of the household, the lords of wells and hearths, the ghosts of kinship, and all others. The lingering dead within homes, ghosts from other lands, and those in households who receive no offerings—each shall be gathered and delivered to the Northern Prison of *Tiānyī* to be slain. Should you fail to heed my words, your great Demon Kings’ heads shall shatter into eighty pieces.

The Dao declares: From this day forth, should even a single person fall ill, it is entirely the work of your minor Ghost Kings. From this day forth, should a man or woman fall ill, and a Daoist come to recite scriptures and provide healing, you must swiftly depart ten thousand *li*, allowing the living to recover, and I shall promote you on high. Should they not recover, I shall hack you into ten thousand pieces without mercy.

Swiftly, swiftly, by the oral command of the Most High, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances.

The Dao declares: From this day forth, should even a single person fall ill, it is entirely the work of plague ghosts. The great Demon Kings have failed to exercise due care, allowing minor ghosts to kill men.

From this day forth, the great Demon Kings and lesser kings must swiftly aid the celestial beings. Wherever Daoists recite this scripture, let the living recover from illness, and let disputes of speech and official matters dissolve of themselves. Should they not recover, the Ghost Kings shall be hacked into ten thousand pieces without mercy.

Swiftly, swiftly, by the oral command of the Most High, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances.

The Dao declares: The world is filled with wicked men. In the year of *renwu*, when Daoists entered the mountains, they were met with mockery. Great floods came, and death arrived unknowing. Alas, alas! The Sage foresaw what was yet unseen, and thus first composed the essentials of the Three Caverns to instruct the myriad families. Those who do not use, accept, or uphold them shall flow away like mud. How grievous, how grievous! The Most High, in great compassion, acts for the sake of all beings in the ten directions.

The Dao declares: From this day forth, those who die suddenly from illness, official matters, or disputes of speech are all slain by the ghosts of Deng Hou and Liu Douwu, who also come to kill the myriad people. Heaven has dispatched the Red Thunder Generals, two hundred and eighty thousand strong, to lead the host in slaying them. From this day forth, great Demon Kings, swiftly restrain your lesser ghosts and drive them ten thousand *li* away. Should they not depart and the living remain unhealed, you shall die.

Swiftly depart, swiftly, by the oral command of the Most High, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances.

The Dao declares: From this day forth, eight hundred thousand lesser ghosts kill men. Should even one among them receive this divine incantation scripture, and a Daoist come to save them, you, lesser kings and great Demon Kings, must all come to assist, driving the lesser ghosts away in haste so that the sick may recover. Should they not recover and the illness worsen, the lesser ghosts shall die.

Swiftly, swiftly, by the oral command of the Most High, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances.

The Dao declares: From this day forth, there are four hundred and ninety thousand wicked men. These wicked men do not recognize the Dao and its laws; hearing them, they do not believe. Now, three hundred thousand Red Slayer Ghosts shall execute them. Should even one among them have faith, celestial beings shall come to transform them. When eight thousand plague ghosts enter a dwelling to take a life, and a Daoist comes to save them, the lesser ghosts shall perish.

The Dao declares: Wicked men do not believe in the Dao and its laws; thus, the world is filled with fools. Yet when there are those who believe in the scriptures and receive the Three Caverns, they come from Heaven above. From this day forth, should the sick not recover, the great Demon Kings shall be held accountable first. From this day forth, swiftly restrain your lesser ghosts.

Swiftly, swiftly, by the oral command of the Most High, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances.

The Dao declares: From this day forth, Daoists who uphold the Three Caverns shall first receive this divine incantation for the sake of all beings. Where there is illness and sentient beings in distress, should the celestial beings and Demon Kings not assist, you shall die.

The Dao declares: The people of the world are harassed by plague ghosts, beset by peril and distress, their lives hanging by a thread. From this day forth, wherever Daoists save lives, the great Demon Kings must swiftly ensure recovery. Should they recover, you shall be promoted on high. Should they not recover, you shall die.

The Dao declares: You Daoists, for the sake of all those in distress, hasten to go forth and save them. I shall dispatch thirty thousand celestial warriors to assist you. From this day forth, wherever Daoists save lives, celestial warriors shall protect and aid them, allowing the sick to recover. Should they recover, the celestial beings and Demon Kings shall be promoted on high. Should they not recover, you shall die.

Swiftly, swiftly, by the oral command of the Most High, in accordance with the statutes and ordinances.

*Scripture of the Divine Incantations of the Most High Cavern Abyss, Scroll Six* concludes.
*Scripture of the Divine Incantations of the Most High Cavern Abyss, Scroll Seven: The Chapter on Beheading Ghosts* begins.

The Dao declares: From the third to the ninth month of this renyear, the year of *renwu*, plague ghosts shall slaughter the people, taking three in every ten—a time of blade and warfare. The Six Barbarians shall perish, the Dharma of the Śramaṇas shall transform, and the qi of the Dao shall daily flourish, as the Three Caverns spread throughout the Middle Kingdom. The vast sun and moon shall lose their measure, the people shall toil in suffering, and the dead shall fill every household. If there are those who uphold the Three Caverns, converting and instructing the people to receive them, and if the sick recite the scriptures, the spirits of the scriptures shall save them, and their illness may be cured. From this day forth, wherever this scripture is recited, I shall dispatch the mighty warriors of the ten directions to transform and admonish the plague ghosts and all evil spirits, compelling them to seize these ghosts. The sick shall be spared, their illnesses cured, and no further harm shall befall them. Those imprisoned or sentenced to penal servitude shall be naturally released. Should they not receive this grace, the Demon Kings shall be the first to face judgment, and they shall be beheaded without mercy.

The Dao declares: After the year of *jiayin*, there shall appear thirty-six myriad and three three-legged ghosts, each nine *zhang* in height, wielding red staffs. They shall enter the homes of the people, inflicting sixty-two kinds of illness, sickening and killing the wicked. Their name is *Quyin*, and each commands three hundred and sixty vertical-eyed ghosts, their eyes all red. Some ride the winds and clouds, seizing lives wantonly, slaughtering livestock in an instant. There shall be one thousand two hundred green plague ghosts, and the plague ghosts’ brethren shall number eighty million. Male and female ghosts, nine hundred million strong, shall enter the homes of the people, lying in wait for the young, causing sudden death. There shall also be two-headed ghosts, named *Dangjin*. *Dangjin* is violent and cruel, constantly terrorizing the common folk, afflicting them with illness. These ghosts falsely devour the people’s pigs and chickens, deceitfully posing as great spirits to delude the foolish. The foolish believe them, slaughtering livestock to offer sacrifices to these ghosts. The ghosts seize the opportunity, turning it into custom. If they do not receive offerings, they cause illness and pain. From this day forth, wherever there are those who uphold this scripture, I shall dispatch thirty-nine thousand celestial soldiers to harmonize and admonish these ghosts, driving them a thousand *li* away. Should they not depart, the Great Demon Kings of the Three Heavens and the lords of the ten directions shall hack them into ten thousand pieces, and there shall be no pardon.

The Dao declares: In the year of *renwu*, there shall already be thirty-six kinds of great ghosts, named *Black-Headed Blazing*, also called *Red Canopy*, and *Aju* as their third name. Each shall lead thirty-nine thousand followers, all wielding white staffs and ghost-slaying blades seven *chi* long. They shall enter the homes of the people, seizing lives wantonly, inflicting one hundred and twenty kinds of illness, sickening and killing the wicked. Sixty kinds of malign qi shall enter the bodies of the people, causing sudden death. From this day forth, wherever those afflicted with such illnesses find masters of the Three Caverns reciting scriptures and performing the Dao, they shall all be cured. Should the ghosts still refuse to yield, causing the people’s illnesses to persist and official matters to remain unresolved, the Great Brahmā Heavenly Kings and the lords of the ten directions shall behead them without mercy.

The Dao declares: In the year of *renwu*, there shall already be thirty-seven thousand red crows, spreading thirty-nine thousand kinds of illness to sicken and kill the wicked. There shall also be eighty-two kinds of illness, bringing misfortune to the wicked. When afflicted by these illnesses, if there are masters of the Three Caverns reciting scriptures and performing the Dao, they may be cured. Wherever scriptures are recited and the Dao is performed, the thirty-six Brahmā Heavenly Kings shall come to assist and protect you. The armies of plague ghosts shall naturally disperse. Should they not depart, I shall dispatch the warriors of the Three Heavens and one hundred thousand *Red Ruin* soldiers to seize and behead them. Daoists who uphold the Three Caverns must swiftly convert all people to the Dao, for the celestial beings shall rejoice. Should you corrupt even one person’s good heart, the celestial beings shall punish you, and you shall not attain human form—how then could you become an immortal? From this day forth, wherever there are those who heal the sick, celestial beings shall come of their own accord to assist and protect you.

Three celestial maidens, numbering five thousand myriad, shall descend together, accompanying *Magu* to roam *Duyang Mountain*, traversing the Five Marchmounts. They shall witness the people of the world suffering from illness and death, not merely a few. The Mysterious Woman exclaims in alarm: “Alas! Celestial calamity! The people shall perish entirely—how can they be saved?” Grieving together, they come to the *Mystic Capital* and report fully to the Most High. The Most High says: “Go among the people of the world and convert them all, instructing them to uphold the Three Caverns. The scriptures of the Three Caverns can deliver sentient beings from all hardships. If you all go to the lands and convert the people to the scriptures, they shall come to revere and believe. When they fall ill or face official troubles, recite the scriptures for them. After one night of recitation, the dead shall revive, and official matters shall resolve themselves. From this day forth, wherever there are masters saving the people, I shall dispatch celestial beings to transform and admonish them, and the plague ghosts shall naturally depart.”

The Dao declares: These three maidens were greatly blessed in their former lives and have now become holy women, teaching and converting all people. They are the most revered in the ten directions. They transform a hundred times in a single day, and none can match them. From now on, if people of later generations hear the names of these three maidens, these women shall also come to save them. Should they suffer from illness or official troubles, recite this scripture, and the great spirits of the ten directions shall come to their aid, preventing any misfortune. If you have the merit of converting others, Heaven shall know of it.

The Dao declares: From the year of *gengchen*, there shall already be ninety hundred million black slaying ghosts, each six *zhang* in height. Each shall lead eighty-four thousand lesser ghosts and red-headed plague ghosts to lie in wait for the people. Their name is *Yingnü*, their eyes all red. They shall roam the ten directions, entering the homes of the people to seize the young, inflicting one hundred kinds of illness to kill them. From this day forth, wherever there are masters reciting this scripture to treat illness, the plague ghosts shall swiftly depart a thousand *li* away. Should they not depart, the great spirits of the Three Heavens shall admonish them. Should they still refuse to leave, the warriors shall bind them, and there shall be no further pardon.

The Dao declares: In the year of *renwu*, during the third and tenth months, there shall be one hundred twenty thousand red-skied plague ghosts, each leading thirty-nine thousand warrior soldiers. There shall also be seven million black-tailed ghosts, named *She She*. Each shall command eighty-six thousand, descending from above to slay the wicked. From this day forth, wherever there is dire illness, should Daoist masters perform scriptural rites to save the afflicted, these ghosts shall seize and bind them. Should they refuse to depart, the warriors of the Three Heavens shall surely behead them. In an instant, the warriors of the Nine Heavens shall also execute them, with no further pardon.

The Dao declares: From this day forth, there shall be eight hundred thousand three-legged ghosts and twelve-headed plague ghosts, coming to kill the people and inflict seventy-nine kinds of illness. Wherever there are masters of the Three Caverns performing the Dao to save others, these ghosts shall naturally be seized by the heavenly beings. Should they refuse to depart, the warriors of the Three Heavens shall surely behead them, with no pardon whatsoever.

The Dao declares: In the ninth month of the year *xinsi*, there shall be thirty million red-eyed ghosts, named *Jiaozi*, each leading forty-nine hundred million lesser ghosts to kill the people. Those afflicted by this plague must swiftly seek masters of the Three Caverns, who upon entering the home shall cause the ghosts to depart of their own accord. Should they not depart, nine hundred thousand *Tianding* warriors and celestial soldiers shall successively behead them, with no pardon whatsoever.

The Dao declares: In the year of *jiawu*, there shall be eighty million *Xiaoling* ghosts, named *Red-Head*, each leading eight hundred thousand to descend and inflict ninety kinds of illness, afflicting the wicked with swelling, sores, and carbuncles. From this day forth, wherever there are masters treating illness, these ghosts shall submit and swiftly flee ten thousand *li* away. Should they refuse to depart, the warriors of the Three Heavens shall execute them without exception. The Daoist masters shall transform the people, causing these ghosts to depart of their own accord.

The Dao declares: From the year of *gengchen* to the ninth and tenth months of the year *renwu*, many people shall fall ill. There shall be nine million three hundred thousand yellow-bodied ghosts, named *Bai Long*, each commanding twelve thousand kings to descend and afflict the people. From this day forth, wherever masters recite the scriptures, these ghosts shall depart of their own accord. Should they refuse to leave, the *Tianding*, celestial warriors, and the great armies of the Three Heavens shall join to behead them, and the Demon Kings of the Nine Heavens shall punish them.

The Dao declares: From the years *xinsi* and *renwu* onward, there shall be ninety-six kinds of slaying ghosts coming to kill the people. In every village, there shall be four hundred sixty thousand yellow-plague ghosts entering the settlements, causing people to vomit blood, suffer from dysentery and cholera, sudden heart pain, jaundice, throat obstructions, and even death. Wherever there are masters performing scriptural rites to save the afflicted, the great spirits of the Three Heavens shall harmonize and admonish these ghosts, banishing them to distant lands ten thousand *li* away. Should any refuse to depart, their heads shall be shattered into sixteen pieces. The great armies of the Three Heavens and the warriors of the Nine Heavens shall never spare them. The Daoist masters shall transform the people and admonish the ghosts.

The Dao declares: Since the end of the Great Han, there have been five great *wutong* ghosts, named Wang Jian, Bai Qi, Han Zhang, Le Yang, and Chu Kuang. There are also Hao Jing, Nü Wa, and Zhu Rong, thirty-nine thousand in number, each commanding eight hundred million. These ghosts, since the time of Fu Xi, have overseen emperors, ministers, and generals, with this great ghost host commanding twelve thousand. The lesser ghosts of the world rely on them for sustenance, serving as soldiers for their ghost kings to harass and disturb the people, bringing them suffering. They lurk in households, seizing men and women, causing illness, sudden misfortune, slander, legal troubles, fires, and floods. Countless in number, they wrong the good people, killing the innocent, deceiving and driving away family, hastening the Stove Lord, disturbing the household spirits, obstructing every matter, and inflicting myriad illnesses, swift and severe. Riding the wind and mounting sparrows, they recklessly create strange lights and omens. Since recent times, their offenses have been beyond count. Now, the *Zhengyi Gongcao*, the *Daming* Envoys, and the *Yanshen* Envoys, each leading nine hundred million iron-faced cavalry officers wielding great halberds and ghost-slaying implements, shall descend together with the forty-nine thousand mighty warriors of the Most High. They shall capture and execute the dead generals of this land, all demons and evil spirits, the millions of specters, and all inauspicious omens that come to harm the households of the living. Each shall be seized, bound, and slain, purging the households of slaying ghosts. The ghost kings shall all exert their strength to successively bind them. Should any ghost refuse to depart, the ghost kings shall execute them a thousand times without pardon. Swiftly, swiftly, as in the statutes and decrees.

The Dao declares: In the land, there are great ghost lords such as Deng Ai, Zhong Shiji, Zhao Shan, Wang Mang, Li Ao, Du Zhou, Liu Douwu, Wang Li, Xiahou Ying, Jiang Gongyan, Ye Gongli of Nanyang, Xia Tanzhi, Xiao He, Shentu Bo, Han Xin, Tian Jin, Liang Hong, Gao Pei, Sun Wen, Sima Jiong, and Liu Yuanda. These great ghosts command the people of the world. Some have temples dedicated to Emperor Wu and King Wen, with continuous offerings and unceasing sacrifices. Each commands armies to haunt the people of the world, afflicting them with illness and death, year after year, month after month, inflicting thousands of kinds of illness. Some cause heaviness in the limbs, alternating chills and fever, dysentery, swelling, watery distension, blackened diseases, pain in the head and eyes, burning heat in the chest and back. Some bring jaundice, coughing, and throat obstructions. All manner of illnesses kill people without measure.

The Dao declares: These individuals were all once great generals and officials who, after their deaths, had temples built and were continuously worshipped.

Now a hundred ghosts cling to them, amassing into vast hordes, ever lying in wait for the chance to seize a human form and slaughter the common folk. They bring upon people disasters of water and fire, strife of words and tongues, and ten thousand misfortunes of official entanglements. When calamity strikes, it swiftly kills, and many lives are lost—this has occurred time and again.

Now the Red Cinnabar Great Prohibiting Soldiers are dispatched, their bodies ten thousand *zhang* tall, eight hundred thousand in number, each leading three hundred million troops, descending to capture these ghost-kings. Once seized, they are beheaded without mercy.

The Dao declares: Wherever the Three Caverns’ Dharma Masters recite scriptures to save people, ninety trillion divine soldiers shall be commanded to guard the households of the living, protecting every member within. Should there be illness, official disputes, or imprisonment, each shall be resolved and freed, their ailments cured without further harm. On the day they recover, the ghost-kings shall ascend. If they do not recover and remain in peril, the Great Demon Kings Mao Di and others shall have their heads shattered into ninety fragments.

The Dao declares: From this day forward, when there are the sick or where this divine incantation scripture is recited, forty thousand Valiant Harmonious Force Soldiers and three hundred sixty thousand Hundred-Tongued Officers shall be dispatched to the homes of the afflicted and the imprisoned. They shall mediate and reconcile the sufferer’s kin, their great-grandparents, and all internal and external misfortunes—whether those who have made offerings or those who have not—distinguishing and resolving each matter clearly.

Moreover, the ghosts of prisons and punishments—Gaoyao, the Lords of Wooden Shackles, the Twelve Commanding Officers, eight hundred ninety thousand generals, all the Long-Hou officials, the Three Dukes and Nine Ministers, the high and low ministers, and the overseers of the ten directions—shall swiftly open the gates of the prisons, release the incarcerated, and transform their fates through reconciliation, bringing joy to the rulers of the age. Freed, they shall depart, and the deceased shall ascend, escaping the Three Wretched Paths to join the ranks of Daoist ghosts, roaming freely and without care, aiding and benefiting the living. Illnesses shall be cured, and all matters resolved.

From this day forth, We have rendered judgment with the ghost-kings: should any remain unhealed, the Great Demon Kings Li Hong and others shall have their heads shattered into three thousand five hundred fragments.

The Dao declares: I address the Great Demon King Fu Ren: Now there are the living, afflicted by illness and suffering. Their four limbs and eight bodily parts are stricken, their mouths and throats obstructed. Their heads ache, their eyes blur, and their chests and backs burn with pain.

Their limbs grow stiff and unyielding, their five viscera scorched. Qi assails the heart in sorrow, leaving them listless and joyless, their eyes unable to open. They refuse food and drink, only retching in nausea. Their dreams and waking hours are restless, as if pursued by the dead. Both within and without, from the greatest to the smallest, all fear their lives may not be preserved. The hour of death approaches swiftly, drawing near without delay.

Now, with sincere devotion and pitiable sorrow, We dispatch the Great Slayer, the Marquis-Kings, and their vast armies—eighty million strong—to summon the ghostly legions of the underworld. For those afflicted by illness in the homes of the living: what ghosts are these? If they be the great-grandparents of the living, they ought not to haunt them. If they are not among those properly worshipped, they are bound by their own attachments. If they be earth or hearth spirits, their sacrifices are observed in due season. If they be household ghosts, they ought not to harm the living. In this age of clarity and fortune, ghosts may not come wantonly.

If there be lingering qi of old misfortune in the dwelling, or calamities from the four directions, all malevolent ghosts—those of mountains, forests, marshes, and pools—shall be seized and delivered to the Three Heavenly Hells. There, the *Ghost Laws* and the *Nüqing Ordinance* shall judge them, ensuring they may not afflict the good with sudden illness.

From this day forth, swiftly gather your ghostly minions. Should the living remain unhealed or their legal troubles unresolved, the Great Demon Kings shall execute them with a thousand cuts, showing no mercy.

The Dao declares: In the *jiǎzǐ* decade of years, eight hundred thousand red-sickness ghosts slay the living. Thirty-six myriad black ghosts and ghost-kings, each leading one hundred twenty thousand barbarian ghosts, invade the homes of men, bringing chills and fevers, swelling of the limbs, and burning heat. They cause infants and women in childbirth to die suddenly.

The Three Dukes shall punish themselves; the realm shall fall into chaos, with floods and droughts unbalanced. Cruel ghosts shall come only to seize men. The sovereign shall fall ill, seated amid unjust oppression, while the people wail to heaven. Heaven, enraged, shall dispatch thirty thousand black-faced lesser ghosts to slay the living.

If you wish to escape this ghostly suffering, receive the Three Caverns’ true scriptures. Should one accept the register of a single general, ghosts shall not dare to kill wantonly.

The Dao declares: In the home of the afflicted, if there be those ensnared in prisons, fearing death, first establish this fast. Let the officiants—whether three, five, ten, or eight—prepare fine registers and accounts. In a purified chamber, arrange the Three Treasures, incense, lamps, and offerings, ensuring all is clean and complete. Summon the masters of the Three Caverns.

Among the masters, choose one of keen and lucid understanding to serve as the officiating priest, chanting the Dao with the host. Set up two high thrones, where one shall intone the sacred titles on behalf of the host. The remaining Daoists shall circumambulate in order. The master upon the high throne shall hold the *Step of Emptiness*, chanting in harmony, while those below move slowly in procession. Gaze upward to the heavens, listening for the wild cries in the clouds. If you hear a clear, ringing resonance, it shall resemble the songs of the Heavenly People in the Palaces of Dark Radiance.

The Dao declares: Where this scripture is recited in the home of the afflicted, all Great Demon Kings and lesser ghost-kings shall swear: From this day forth, should any perform the fast and conduct the rites to heal the sick—even those in grave peril, beset by legal strife, imprisonment, or torture—summon the myriad ghosts before them. Which ghost is responsible? Drive them swiftly away, that the afflicted may naturally recover, their legal troubles resolved, and all their wishes fulfilled.

From this day forward, should legal troubles remain unresolved or illnesses persist, the Great Demon Kings and lesser ghost-kings shall execute them without mercy.

The Dao declares: In the *jiǎxū* decade of years, three thousand nine hundred white crows shall descend, spreading sickness and slaying the wicked. Throughout the land, men and women shall die suddenly, struck by eighty kinds of pestilential qi. The ancient dead generals Meng Da, Ma Yuan, Li Qing, Wang Feng, Yan Zhen, Zuo Qiu, thieves, fishermen, Hua Yuanji, Cheng Hong, and others—each leading a thousand myriad—shall descend to spread red dysentery, sapping the strength of the living and unsettling their homes. They shall lurk at doors and thresholds, seizing the young.

Should the kin of a household take fright, and their kin in turn fear them, then official ranks shall not advance, households shall suffer depletion, groundless quarrels shall arise, every encounter shall turn inauspicious, legal troubles shall follow one after another, imprisonment shall drag on, fields and silkworms shall yield nothing, and ten thousand wishes shall come to naught. All this stems from these ghost-kings failing to restrain their underlings, allowing them to torment the living thus.

From this day forward, each of you shall keep your ghostly troops in check and forbid their cruelty. Let the living see their legal troubles resolved and their illnesses ease. On the day their illnesses ease, you shall ascend. Should they fail to recover even for a day, you shall be executed ten thousand times over, your heads shattered into eighty-six pieces.

The Dao declares: In the *jiǎshēn* decade of years, great disasters shall arise. Waters from the northwest shall surge forth, and of ten stricken by illness, eight or nine shall die. Thirty-nine myriad red ghosts shall descend, spreading sickness among the people. Those afflicted shall turn sallow, and women and children shall be especially unfit to bear it. Yet should the ruler of the land believe in the Dao, uphold the scriptures, and receive them, they shall be spared. Pestilential qi shall billow forth, and thirty-nine myriad kinds of illness shall slay the people. Those who flee into the mountains shall number thousands upon thousands. The people shall know no peace, cut down by blades, plagues, and ghostly slaughter—killed without reason.

Heaven shall dispatch seven hundred thousand red-clad soldiers, each wielding a bronze halberd, to slay the wayward ghosts and gather all the world’s calamities. Should the Three Heavens’ Great Demon Kings wrongfully execute any, each of those demon kings—Wūwán and the rest—shall be executed without mercy. Begone ten thousand leagues hence!

Swiftly, swiftly, as in statute and command!

The Dao declares: The world teems with wicked men, and Heaven dispatches warriors to execute them, first inquiring into their good and evil. How could the vast hosts of Heaven’s soldiers be resisted? Yet should Daoist priests recite scriptures to save them, let them live, and cease the slaughter.

From this day forward, should any in the world suffer illness or imprisonment, wherever Daoist priests perform petitions and recite scriptures to heal them, the Great Demon Kings and lesser ghost-kings shall aid in their recovery, resolving all matters. Should any fail to recover or be released, and quarrels persist unbroken, the great ghost Yìzhēn and his kind shall hack them into ten thousand pieces, without exception or mercy.

Swiftly, swiftly, as in the Most High’s oral command and statute!

The Dao declares: The great gate’s ghostly officer, Lord Dàzhēn; the small gate’s ghostly officer, Lord Xiǎozhēn; the chamber’s guardian, Yī Wén; the rear guardian, Wàn Lún; the hearth’s guardian, Yán Jǐng; the road’s guardian, Shī Gòng; the great ghosts within and without; the household’s calamities; the male and female guests who perished; those slain by water, fire, metal, or wood—each shall restrain themselves. What ghost now comes to sicken the living? The people are in peril.

The Most High dispatches a hundred million red-clad soldiers, warriors who bind ghosts and beat them to death with bronze cudgels, then deliver them to the Warding Off Evil?—handing them over to the Heavenly One’s Northern Prison. Fearing wrongful harm, He commands that all the people be instructed: should any household suffer illness, swiftly release the afflicted. Let them be treated according to the Dao, that the living may recover and neither people nor ghosts come to harm. Should any ghost refuse to depart, the sick shall not recover. The Great Demon Kings and lesser ghost-kings shall be hacked into a hundred pieces, without mercy.

All as in the Most High’s oral command—no delay permitted!

Swiftly, swiftly, as in statute and command!

The Dao declares: Nowadays, the world’s people die wretchedly from pestilence. From this day forward, We swear with the demon kings Xià Yín, Wūwán, Wū Yán, Chì Bō, Hóng Qiū, and others: In this age, sickness abounds, and sinners die unaware, ignorant of their own salvation. We now command the Three Caverns’ Dharma Masters to enlighten the foolish. Among the foolish, there shall be those who believe—men and women of office. Should they hold to these incantations, observe fasts and lectures in their villages, practice the Six Periods’ rituals, perform the Dao, give alms, and meditate, then in such places, you ghost-kings shall aid in enlightening the foolish. Do not let them fall ill; should they fall ill, let them recover swiftly, and permit no hundred evils to assail them.

All as We have spoken—you may ascend. Should you defy Our teaching, your heads shall be shattered into ten pieces, without mercy.

All as in the Most High’s oral command and statute!

The Dao speaks: In the *jiǎ-wǔ* decade of years, the six barbarian tribes—Dī, Liáo, Qiāng, and Hú—shall unleash their ghosts to roam, spreading sixteen thousand kinds of disease to sicken and slay the wicked. Great disasters shall bring unrest; the people shall face peril and plague, and many women shall die. The ghost-king Dèng Ài and Liú Dǒu-Wū shall come, spreading twelve kinds of dysentery. The Earth Lord shall kill men, and the divine dragons shall ascend to heaven. Great floods shall rise, and the Five Phases shall cease their motion. Ghostly bandits shall harm the people, causing many to die violently, perishing without reason.

From this day forth, the Most High and the Great Demon Kings—thirty-six kings, including Xún Gǔ, and one hundred twenty thousand ghost-lords—shall decree: If any household, man or woman, falls ill, you shall drive away the affliction, dissolve official disputes, and restore peace to the people. Should you fail even once to act according to the law, you shall be beheaded first, your bodies shattered into ten thousand pieces without mercy.

All as in the oral command and statute of the *Nǚ Qīng Sháo Shū*.

The Dao speaks: As the great celestial cycles converge, demonic soldiers shall run rampant. From this day forth, for all under heaven—men and women whose illnesses linger and deepen, all evil ghosts and household spirits who fail to protect them, and those harmed by the hundred evils of mountains and forests—you shall ensure their swift recovery and spare them unjust death. If, from this day forth, any cause unjust death or untimely demise, the Great Demon King and lesser ghost-kings shall sever your heads into ten thousand pieces to atone for these wrongs.

As the Most High has orally commanded, there shall be no mercy. All shall be as the *Ghost Statutes* decree: seize them and deliver them to the Northern Prison of Heaven One for punishment. Hasten, hasten, as the statutes command!

The Dao speaks: From this day forth, eight hundred thousand three-legged ghosts and twelve-headed plague ghosts shall come to kill, spreading seventy-nine kinds of disease.
