Moreover, there are the Thirty-Six Heavenly Demon Kings, including Jupoqiang, numbering one hundred twenty thousand; the forty-two Demon Kings of the Radiant Heavenly Capital, such as Wumingjiu, who slay ghosts and cure diseases; the Valiant Soldiers of the Three Heavens and the Crimson Armies of the Ten Directions; and the Three Heavenly Jade Maidens and the Generals of Urgent Advance, fifty million in total, who ever dwell upon the Five Peaks to gather all plague demons.

There are also the Demon Kings of Beaked Heads, the Great King Wuyan, the Great King of Long Noses, the Great King of the Central [Realm], the Great King of Small Eyes, the Great King of White Faces, and the Great King of Red Faces, each wielding their divine transformations, sovereign might, and boundless power. Before the Most High, they prostrate themselves with utmost reverence, jointly vowing with the King of Samādhi Divine Mantras to traverse the Three Realms, the earth above and below, and the sacred mountains, rivers, and grotto-heavens. They pledge to eradicate the Six Heavenly and Nine Ugly [Demons], the perverse *qi* of the Five Pestilences and rebellious forces, the harms inflicted upon the people, and all monstrous anomalies, as well as the outbreaks of warfare. "We possess the power to crush and annihilate them, to transform their hearts, and to sever all demonic *qi*. We only beseech the Heavenly Worthy to show mercy upon us and all our retinues, elevating us to the ranks of the Dao, that we may never regress."

Thereupon, the Perfected One Weiming declared to the King of Samādhi Divine Mantras: "We, who now gather and extinguish perverse *qi*, capture ghosts, and cure diseases, must reveal the names of the plague-spreading demons, so that people may recite and invoke them. When these plague-spreading demons hear their own names, they will feel momentary shame and fear. Amidst the assembly before the Three Treasures, they will be humiliated by their own evil and dare not cause harm. Now, by the Heavenly Worthy’s compassion and majestic command, the luminous might of the Three Heavens and Five *Qi*, and the rectifying deities who scrutinize the myriad spirits, we shall disclose their names. I shall instruct the Direct Supervisors and Recorders to itemize and inscribe them, making them known to all devout men and women under heaven."

Thereupon, the King of Samādhi Divine Mantras universally proclaimed to the Three Realms, the Five Paths, the Six Deng, the Nine Dark Springs, and the curved abodes of all ghostly kings, the Dragon Kings of Water and Earth, the Avian Kings, and all spirits—whether those who neither ascend to heaven nor dwell upon the earth, who roam the world, ride the Eight Winds, mount the *qi* of the Nine Uglies, rely on trees as dwellings, or absorb human essence and pursue blood offerings to incite disasters—commanding them all to reveal their names and dare not conceal themselves.

Thereupon, the Ancient Spirits of the Five Directions and the Five Harmful Ghostly Thieves conferred among themselves: "We are of lowly status in the mortal world, our virtue and power meager, our strength insufficient. We know not where to flee. If we do not submit our names, we shall be reduced to ashes, our retinues plunged into suffering. Beset by calamities before and behind, we can only beg for great compassion, that you grant us leniency. We wish to exhort one another to abandon the mundane, return to the Dao, submit to your teachings, and never again cause harm."

Thereupon, the Three Heavenly Wicked Kings led four hundred eighty thousand, while the Six Heavenly Wicked Kings and the Three Heavenly Great Wicked Kings numbered nine hundred million.

Moreover, there are eighty thousand one-footed ghosts, each three feet tall, forming bands that dwell in waters to spread *qi*-induced illnesses. There are also Shenyou Aizi, Jiao’er Pingwang, Axin Sanye, and thirty thousand Red Ghosts who spread the plague of warfare. There are forty-nine kinds of Black Crow Ghosts that constantly incite terror, causing unease. There are seven million Red Crows that flock together, flying to spread epidemics. There are thirty thousand Hu Ghosts that come to slay people, spreading the plague of famine and exile. There are forty-nine billion Red Ding Messengers. There are ghosts from the lower realms who died in battle or from wounds, each leading four hundred thousand to spread diseases and toxins. There is the Ghost King Wuyuan, seven *zhang* and eight *chi* tall, each with a retinue of ninety million Crimson Soldiers who spread various plague *qi*. There are the Nine Heavenly Demon Kings and the Majestic Capital Generals who descend to spread nine thousand kinds of illness.

There are the Gate and Door Ghosts, named Chengbo, and the Locking Ghosts, named Alunran. There are the Well Ghosts, named Zhenlianzi. There are the ghosts upon the four walls and fences, named Shibogong. There are the Road Ghosts, named Wuzi Ding. There are the House Ghosts, named Xuanzidu. There are the Crimson-Linked Ghosts of the Ten Directions, each three *chi* and six *cun* tall, forming bands of a million. There are three hundred thousand Long-Headed Ghosts, each wielding a crimson staff to violently beat and kill people. There are the ghosts of those who died by the sword in battle, such as Li Ziao of the Cloudy Realm, who wander the seashores of the four directions, riding winds and mounting sparrows to create anomalies and spread plagues.

There are the ghosts of Gaoyao’s wooden fetters, who practice punishments and executions, turning all implements of harm into ghostly spirits. There are the Lianzi Ghosts who spread malaria and sores. There is the Ghost King named Youlian, three *zhang* and seven *chi* tall, wielding a crimson rope to incite quarrels and agitate human hearts. There are the Red-Turbaned Ghosts who spread plague toxins across the Eight Directions. There are three thousand nine hundred ghosts of mountains, forests, water, fire, wind, and clouds, with the Ghost King named Dunu Wenqingzi, who spread miscellaneous plagues. There are the Red Ding Fire Ghosts, each leading seven hundred thousand to spread febrile illnesses. There are the Black-Footed Ghosts, three *zhang* and six *chi* tall, with red and yellow eyes, sometimes transforming into red crows, named Rizu Ri, who spread pestilential plagues.

There is the Ghost Master named Datou Lu, whose brothers number eighty million, forming bands to spread plague *qi*. There are four hundred ninety thousand Black-Faced Ghosts, with the Ghost King named Zhangchi, leading thirty-six billion lower ghosts to spread black pestilence. There are twenty thousand Red-Rope Ghost Kings named Baishou, leading thirty-nine thousand female ghosts to spread diseases. There are the Crimson Capital Ghosts who spread seventy-eight kinds of illness, sometimes transforming into crows and magpies to circle human dwellings, exhaling *qi* to spread disease.

Again there are the Crimson-Cliff Ghosts, eighty *zhang* tall, sometimes transforming into flying crows to spread disease, or into dead fish, crows, beasts, or wild fruits—whoever consumes them contracts poisonous illnesses. There is the Yellow-Ox Ghost King named Red-Stone, leading red-headed crows to spread toxic diseases. There are Li Ziao’s brothers, numbering a thousand billion ghosts, who band together to kill humans. There are the three Jūliúnà Ghosts, each leading eight million ghosts to spread various toxic illnesses. There are the ghosts of Deng Hou and Liu Douwu, who also come to spread disease and harm the people. There are the Three-Legged Ghosts, three *zhang* tall, with human bodies that move sideways. There are the three hundred sixty Quyin Ghosts, the Cross-Eyed Ghosts, the Fillet-Headed Ghosts, and the Dangjin Ghosts, all spreading pestilential diseases. There are the Head-Burning Ghosts and the Red-Canopy Ghosts, wielding white staffs and long blades to spread plague and kill humans. There are the Red Crows, spreading thirty-nine thousand kinds of illness. There are the Black-Slaying Ghosts, six *zhang* tall, along with the Ying Girl Ghosts, the Jiaozhi Ghosts, and the Bald Ghosts, all with red eyes. There are one hundred seventy thousand Black-Corpse Ghosts named She-She. There are the Three-Legged, Twelve-Headed Plague Ghosts and the Red-Eyed Ghosts named Horn-Child. There are the Xiaoling Ghosts named Red-Head. There are nine hundred thirty thousand Yellow-Bodied Ghosts named Hundred-Dragons. There are the Red-Reed Great-Prohibition Soldier Ghosts, ten thousand *zhang* tall, numbering eight hundred thousand. There are the Dūlúnà Ghosts, three *zhang* tall, with vertical eyes, horizontal mouths, ears six *chi* long, wielding iron staves, sometimes transforming into giant crows to spread disease and kill humans. There are the Great Red-Nosed Ghosts named Aconite, nine *chi* tall, with three faces and one eye. There are the Two-Headed, One-Bodied Ghosts named Red-Eye. There are the Three-Headed, One-Bodied Ghosts named Great-Wild. There are the ghosts named Heavenly-Pond and Big-Headed Walker, who kill with blades and weapons. There are the ghosts named Great-Dawn, three *chi* tall, wielding red staffs to kill humans. There are the White Crows, shaped like cartwheels, whose flocks kill humans. Some transform into large fish dead upon the water—whoever eats them dies. Some become wild crows dead in the grass—whoever eats them dies. There are Feng Zidu and his band of thirty-nine million, spreading sudden-death illnesses. There are one hundred twenty kinds of hunting ghosts in the clouds, seventy-two kings, the Hook-Star Ghosts, the Wu-Huo Ghosts, the Night-Walking Ghosts, and the Flying-Running Ghosts, who roam the world spreading madness and deviance. There are the Nine-Ugly Ghosts, the Di-Star Mad-Clouds, the myriad demonic gallopers, the bell-horses and shadow-shouters, nine brothers in all. There are Liu Yuanda, Zhang Yuanbo, Zhao Gongming, Li Gongzhong, Shi Wenye, Zhong Shiji, and Shaodu Fu, each leading two hundred fifty thousand plague-spirit ghosts to spread pestilential diseases.

These ghost kings, upon hearing the names of the Three-Modes Divine Mantra Heavenly Kings, the Radiant-Net Realized Ones, the Many-Heard Heavenly Women, and the Great Demonic Kings of the Three Heavens and Six Heavens—all emanations of malevolent *qi*, thieving spirits, and harming essences—were greatly alarmed and terrified.

Further, the Hunting Hook-Star Nine-*Qi* Ghosts cried out in unison: “We and our kin have, since ancient times, relied upon our bodies, speech, and lives for sustenance, feeding only on human essence-*qi* and the blood and flesh of the six livestock, using them to sustain ourselves and driving ghostly souls as our servants. If we now uphold the precepts and cannot roam freely, seeking to preserve others while facing our own deaths—even if we do not die, our bodies will waste away, neither large nor small remaining. Our kin will be filled with sorrow, weeping in distress. We beseech the Great Kings and peerless divine lords to grant us life.”

Then the Three-Modes Divine Mantra King addressed the ghost kings: “You all, from the past until now, have not believed in the supreme Dao, nor followed the true and correct. Instead, you harm and kill one another, cycling through karmic retribution, your kalpas exhausted, your evil karma not yet spent. Now, in the Nine Dark Realms, you suffer great retribution. If any among your kin could take your place, would that be just? There is no such principle. I, following the Heavenly Worthy, traverse the Three Realms, the Thirty-Two Heavens, the lands of the ten directions, the Five Paths and Eight Gates, witnessing all good and evil as clearly as an echo responds to sound, with no escape. If you now can universally instruct your kin not to harm the people, I will command the people of the world to prepare, according to their means, rare delicacies and fine foods, whether by day or night, in their cities, villages, hamlets, or tranquil dwellings, to set out offerings for you, ensuring you are sated and forever free from hunger and thirst. They will also provide you with clothing, money, and silk, for your use. Without incurring deep enmity, you will receive food and sustenance, your lives fully provided for. Is this not joyous?”

Thereupon, the plague-spreading ghost kings and all their kin rejoiced, bowing their heads to the Dao Lord and the Three-Modes Divine Mantra King: “We will follow your teachings and obey your commands.”

At that time, the Realized One Wei Mingluo and the Three-Modes Heavenly King, bearing the mandate of the Most High, addressed the Five Marchmounts’ Chief Administrators, the Four Seas’ Wardens, and the Village Community Deities: “You must now universally proclaim to all in the world: when the Three Calamities are about to arise and pestilence is set to spread, at the beginnings of the four seasons or in places afflicted by illness, the people—good men and good women, in cities, villages, hamlets, or noble and humble dwellings—should unite in mind and recite together, inviting Daoist masters. They should also have men and women wear talismans and amulets, bathe in fragrant waters, abstain from alcohol, meat, pungent and raw foods, and maintain purity while setting up vegetarian feasts. They should perform prostrations, chant praises, and high-ranking Dharma masters should contemplate the true, donning reverent attire, hanging silk banners and canopies, burning incense and scattering flowers, lighting lamps, and offering thanks. Some may play pure music to summon the hidden and manifest, setting out pure vegetarian delicacies to offer to the Three Worthies and the thirty-six heavens’ spontaneous deities, ensuring all are sated. According to their wealth or poverty and local resources, whether abundant or modest, they should express their sincere devotion, burning incense while circumambulating or sitting upright, silently contemplating, sounding drums, practicing breath control, reciting the names of the ghosts, and invoking the names of our divine kings. They should focus their minds in prostration to the Three-*Qi* Three Heavens’ Sovereign Deities, the Primordial Four Directions, the Thirty-Six Heavens’ Nine Palaces, the Five Marchmounts’ True Officials, and the Correct Deities—spontaneous, perfectly true, the source of great wisdom, responding to circumstances and seizing opportunities, wielding boundless divine power and majesty. They will swiftly arrive, entering the ritual space to receive the offerings and fulfill the vows, bringing harmony and joy, so that humans and ghosts rejoice together, neither harming the other.”

Having heard the Dharma-sound and beheld the Heavenly Writings of the Three Sovereigns and the Jade Texts in Five Scrolls—all imbued with numinous *qi*—each is content in their lot, embodying the Dao in its spontaneity. The four seasons harmonize, the world attains Great Peace, and both the sovereign and the people receive the Dao of Non-Action, ascending in name to the Jade Purity. The divine and the perfected commune in unity, and all is tranquil.

Thereupon, the Heavenly Maiden, the Great Brahmā King, the thirty-six heavens’ lesser kings, the boundless flying deities of the Three Realms, the Five Marchmounts’ Chief Administrators, the sons of Brahmā, the Heavenly Maiden of Many Hearings, and all demon-kings pay reverence to the Heavenly Worthy.

They further hear the Heavenly Kings of the Samādhi Divine Mantras, who entreat the essential teachings to deliver and uplift sentient beings, granting blessings in life and death. Heaven-dwellers and humans rejoice, praising what they have never before heard or seen. The *Dongyuan* Divine Mantras, majestic in power, defy description. As one, they rise, bow their heads in reverence, prostrate themselves, and kneel in devotion, vowing to cultivate the Way, each awakening gradually to the Perfect Truth.

Then the Heavenly King of the Samādhi Divine Mantras commands the thirty-six heavens’ flying deities and other divine kings to each strike the celestial instruments, the great music of cloud-like *fangtian* chimes, in praise of the Dao Lord.

Thereupon, the Radiant Perfected One of the Azure Net offers a hymn, singing:
The Perfect Truth’s essence is formless,
What name could it ever possess?
Adapting to things, it takes shape,
Majestic, foremost among all.
Taking refuge, transgressions dissolve,
Disasters gathered—no fault but one’s own.
Non-being is not the absence of non-being,
Being is not the presence of being.

The Heavenly Maiden of Many Hearings also offers a hymn, singing:
Profound grace, ever serene,
Supreme among the exalted.
Universally bestowing the medicine of non-birth,
It heals all undying souls.
Called a mantra, yet still a mantra,
Its vehicle races, its body too flees.
Forever transcending the Five Sufferings’ abode,
It ultimately enters the Gate of Spontaneity.

The Divine King Juliu offers a hymn, singing:
The Crimson Chaos of the Great Non-Being’s Origin,
The numinous treasure’s divine name.
The myriad existences are Non-Action,
The spontaneous, true, unified Dao.
Good arises not from another,
Evil is born from self-examination.
Mastering the Four Delusions’ confusion,
Why sever the Three Afflictions?

The Divine King Jumin’s son offers a hymn, singing:
The Perfect Truth, formless in name,
Forcibly called the Dharma King.
Its responsive bodies follow the myriad existences,
Deliverance is truly without limit.
With a sincere heart, uphold the divine mantra,
Evil ghosts transform into goodness.
The Six Sensations free from attachment—
What worry that life will not be long?

The Flying Celestial Brahmā-son offers a hymn, singing:
Excellent is the land of the Square Cauldron,
Fortune and blessings descend from the celestial perfected.
Pitiful are those who race in competition,
Valuing others while demeaning themselves.
Not knowing true knowledge, they seek illusory gods,
Wandering in delusion, chasing external spirits.
Return to the land of the True Unity,
Preserve the people of spontaneity.

All the immortals, perfected beings, and celestial multitudes rejoice, praising what they have never before heard or seen. They bow twice, prostrate themselves, and chant their assent, vowing to uphold and practice.

Thus concludes *The Supreme Dongyuan Divine Mantras Sutra*, Scroll Eleven.
*The Supreme Dongyuan Divine Mantras Sutra*, Scroll Twelve.

The Chapter on the Host of Sages Protecting the Body and Dispelling Disasters

The Primordial Heavenly Worthy addressed the Five Venerable Lords of the Five Directions, the Nine Celestial Divine Kings, the Perfected Beings of the Ten Directions, and the assembly of divine immortals and sages, saying: "I have often observed that within the Three Realms and the myriad existences, across the Five Paths and Eight Gates, whether celestial beings or humans, men or women, all sentient beings possessing consciousness and nature—whether in the heavens or hells—experience suffering and joy as cause and effect, like echo answering sound, interdependent and endless. Sinking into the cycles of death and rebirth, they cannot liberate themselves. Yet when reflection arises in the heart, the Dao transforms and awakens, guiding those who turn toward it into the source of the Way.

Since time immemorial, I have acted as a compassionate father and mother to you, the beings of the Three Realms and Five Paths, and all living creatures, teaching and guiding you across kalpas through karmic conditions. At times, I manifest in various forms—bodies, names, titles, voices, and speech—responding to the needs of beings, harmoniously expounding the teachings. The Dharma-voices of the Three Caverns, the ten divisions of wondrous scriptures, and the Dharma-boats I have established universally ferry all beings. I open the celestial vehicle of the Dao, gathering those with aspiration, delivering the multitude from the net of craving, shattering deluded views, and transcending the dualities of emptiness and existence.

Yet all sentient beings, lifetime after lifetime, bind themselves through habitual karmic conditions, deluded by false perceptions. Their natures drift, their emotions wander, and in their ignorance and confusion, they obscure their own minds. The Three Corpses and Nine Worms cannot be cast aside; karmic retributions for evil deeds follow them, causing self-inflicted birth and death, chronic illness, prolonged misfortune, bodily and mental afflictions, and the torment of demonic qi and malevolent spirits, which seize upon transgressions and sink them into entanglement.

If one wishes to dispel these, one must contemplate one’s own body, observing the root of arising and ceasing, the advance and retreat of good and evil. Extinguish thoughts and still the void; contemplate the Three Treasures, cultivate kindness, frugality, and yielding, and turn toward the Seven Perfected. Embrace the Void and the Utmost Real—the Dao within the Dao.

Noble lords and ladies, Heavenly Worthies of the Ten Directions, by your divine names and titles, the Eight Purities of the Great Simplicity, and the Nine Qi Primordial Ladies—arouse the mind, visualize, and adorn your appearance and attire. Follow the flourishing of qi, practice exhalation and inhalation, recite and chant, keeping the mind undistracted. Receive and uphold the precious scriptures and talismanic contracts, hang banners and erect floral offerings, burn incense and light lamps. With tranquil intention, focus the mind and voice to make vows, repenting and atoning for the sins of past lives and the deceased, the karmic roots of transgressions, the retributions of misfortune, and the consequences of past deeds. Gradually, these will be dissolved.

If a Daoist cultivating immortality recites this scripture, wisdom will open and the six senses will become clear. For chronic or stubborn illnesses, reciting this scripture will fill one with true qi, restoring health. When tormented by demonic or malevolent spirits, recite this scripture while sounding the drum of command, striking bells and chimes. Malevolent entities will vanish, and the hun and shen will stabilize. In hunger, thirst, cold, or heat, or when lodging alone in the mountains or wilderness, recite this scripture, practice exhalation and inhalation, and swallow saliva. Divine medicines will descend, warming the cold and sating hunger. When heaven and earth undergo transformation, the Five Phases announce disasters, the stars and constellations manifest omens, or strange signs appear in the hidden or manifest realms, recite this scripture, and malevolent intentions will submit. In times of war, pestilence, or the spread of death and disease, recite this scripture, and blades will blunt, demonic spirits will perish.

You, the perfected immortals, entrusted with governance, should proclaim these secret essentials to save the multitude of beings. Let those with aspiration transcend all obstacles and afflictions, attain peace in this life, and later achieve the perfection of the Dao. Extinguish thoughts and forget them; practice benevolence, filial piety, and respect. Put others before oneself, promote goodness and transform evil. Sail the great Dharma-boat into the sea of wisdom, unstained by the Three Bonds, guarding the True Unity. Return the two halves to their original state, merging obscurely with spontaneity."

Thereupon, the Five Venerable Lords of the Five Directions, the flying celestials of the Ten Directions, and the Seven Sage Immortals all rose, bowed, circumambulated three times, knelt before the Dao, and each presented what they had received in the past—the essentials of the Dao, divine mantras, talismanic recitations, and true instructions. After the Three Dragons, they saved myriad beings. For faithful men and women who, with sincere devotion, humility, and perseverance, have yearned for years with unwavering resolve, spurning wealth to honor the Dao, and those of single-minded sincerity, they should follow the Bright Regulations of the Four Poles and the ancient canons of the Three Primes, purifying themselves for three months. If royal duties intervene, complete one seven-day period or three seven-day periods. Transcribe and secretly transmit these teachings; careless disclosure or disrespect will bring the wind-blade to examine the body. How can one not be cautious?

**The Meaning of the Divine Mantra and Talisman for Protecting the Body by the Mysterious Perfected**

The Seven Perfected said: "We have expounded that all the celestial sages who have attained the Dao, from countless eons past, have transmitted and received these teachings. Daoist men and women, regardless of status or age, who uphold, remember, and recite them—when ill, recite; when in disaster, recite; when facing misfortune, recite; when in peril, recite; when in distress, recite; when in sorrow, recite; when in joy, recite.

Long ago, with the Mysterious Perfected, we expounded the scriptures of the Three Treasures, which have already been fully recorded. Those who uphold them to save the world treasure them in their hearts, preserving the body and nurturing nature to attain the Dao of non-action. May the Heavenly Perfected save me, the Orthodox Perfected sustain me, the Utmost Perfected guard me, the Mysterious Perfected protect me, the Wondrous Perfected remember me, the Jade Perfected shield me, the Golden Perfected aid me, the Seven Perfected deliver me, the Nine Perfected preserve me. May the Dharma-mirror illuminate me, the Mysterious Spirit shade me, the Flowing Gold radiate me, the Dharma-vehicle transport me, the Dharma-power defend me, the Dharma-merit perfect me. May the morning lamp shine upon me, its brilliance dazzling me. May the misty qi hasten me, the light of compassion crown me, the cloud encampment cover me. May the Mysterious Sages comfort me, the Dharma King receive me. May the celestial spirits dispel disasters for me, the myriad spirits deliver me from peril, the earth deities ward off evil for me, the myriad emperors eliminate misfortune for me, the host of sages avert calamity for me. May the Seven Perfected grant me bodily peace, the Nine Perfected ensure my longevity."

**The Hymn of the Mysterious Perfected for Dispelling Disasters and Averting Misfortune**

The Golden Perfected descends through empty space,
Divine tigers inspect the cloud encampment.
The Jade Emperor dons green mist,
The myriad heavens command divine soldiers.
The Nine Stars turn their celestial chariots,
The ten thousand demons bind their demonic forms.
The Nine Subtleties swiftly send forth mist,
Divine generals seize malevolent spirits.
The Nine Primes open the cloud paths,
Divine might summons all spirits.
Flowing Gold hurls its keen blades,
All evils dissolve and vanish.

**Divine radiance illumines the celestial lodges,**
**Eradicating the demon kings’ armies.**
**The Five Symbols unleash wind and fire,**
**Vanquishing poison as the Golden Horse appears.**
**Should any calamities dare encroach,**
**The Northern Emperor records your name.**
**The sagely Dao is vast and unobstructed,**
**Divine might slays demonic essences.**
**Dragon-riders arrive from the ten directions,**
**Divine clouds encircle the demon city.**
**The sages teach me to recite,**
**Flying talismans ascend through the heavens’ expanse.**
**The ten directions safeguard the kalpa’s fate,**
**Granting me smoothness, prosperity, and integrity.**

**The Hymn of the Mysterious Perfected for Dispelling Malevolent Spirits and Demons of the Five Directions**

**Dharma drums shake heaven and earth,**
**Divine smoke subdues the Nine Perfected.**
**Flowing Gold scatters and falls,**
**The Great Image follows lightning’s birth.**
**Demon winds cannot reverse fate,**
**Cloud Lords gleam with fire-bells.**
**Resplendent, divine power seizes,**
**Celestial lodges remain unwaning.**
**Swift wheels and fire-armor surge,**
**Divine lightning slays demonic forms.**
**Purple radiance guards against poisonous dragons,**
**Banishing demons to the northern frontier.**
**Divine winds rage through the Nine Gorges,**
**The Eight Paths naturally brighten.**
**Suddenly, the Nine Heavens open,**
**Demons wail and collapse.**
**Thousands upon thousands come bound,**
**Myriad upon myriad do not linger.**
**This talisman is bestowed upon heaven’s people—**
**Recite it to safeguard ten thousand ages.**
**Above, celebrate the eternal absence of kalpas,**
**Compassionate hearts bring great peace.**
**Observe purity in silent stillness,**
**Countless eons shall flourish.**
**Circulate it swiftly as lightning,**
**The myriad heavens benefit your name.**
**Let each person recite it once,**
**To protect their children with eternal prosperity.**

**The Hymn of the Seven Perfected Commanding the Ten Heavenly Emperors to Seize the Six Heavens’ Demon Soldiers**

**I command the Ten Heavenly Emperors,**
**Vast and mighty, to display their might.**
**Divine generals traverse the earthly paths,**
**Seizing the Six Heavens’ demonic hordes.**
**Smoke and flames arise in the void,**
**Brocade clouds brush the divine winds.**
**Above, protect the heavens’ blessings—**
**How could the mysterious signs ever end?**
**At the center, secure the emperors’ foundations,**
**Spiritual transformations dance with divine bells.**
**Below, save heaven, earth, and humanity,**
**Flying riders subdue demon lords.**
**The Seven Luminaries hurl divine light,**
**No evil can bring misfortune.**
**The Ten Heavens dispatch the talisman,**
**The myriad emperors respond like cloud-dragons.**
**Gently passing through the Eight Perils,**
**The Five Paths are all cleansed.**
**The Five Emperors issue their decrees,**
**Swift as water, fire, and wind.**
**Guard against the Three Calamities,**
**The ten directions rejoice in abundance.**
**Universal celestial jubilation,**
**Boundless protection and grace.**

**The Seven Perfected say:**
**Should heavenly beings take refuge, receive, and uphold this talisman, inscribing it once and reciting its incantations, it shall accompany them at life’s end, ensuring their souls avoid the Ten Sufferings, Eight Perils, Three Realms, Five Paths, and Six Destinies. In death and life, they shall be guided, the talisman escorting their spirits to the Ten Directions’ Hall of Non-Action and Blessing. Recite it nine times for divine peace, ten times for clarity, a hundred times to dispel calamities, a thousand times to avert afflictions. Whether worn or recited, the myriad spirits shall pay homage, day and night ever guarding, the four limbs wholly at peace. Constant recitation brings bodily ease, preserving form through ten thousand kalpas, crushing all evils. The myriad heavens heed, the demon kings of the ten directions dare not ignore its sound.**

**The Seven Perfected say:**
**Now, this Dharma is eternally transmitted to future generations, safeguarding and delivering boundless heavenly beings through endless kalpas.**

**At that time, among the assembly were Heavenly Soldiers, Divine Warriors, and the Sentient Sons, who together rose, bowed, and knelt, focusing their minds to address the Heavenly Worthy:**
**"We reflect upon our karmic fortunes through countless kalpas, having the fortune to behold your august countenance and partake in this joyous gathering. Witnessing the Great Kings expound the essential Dharma, we rejoice beyond measure at their vow to save all beings, deliver them from suffering, and guide them into the Dao’s gate.**

**"Formerly, in the land of Sudarśana, we received divine incantations from the Nine Heavens’ Perfected. Though we received their teachings, our minds remained confused and uncomprehending. Only through long devotion, strictly adhering to the oral instructions—bowing, reciting, and meditating without cease—did our spirits accumulate resonance, and the Dao’s qi gradually flow. Gradually, we attained awakening, though our minds’ understanding remained incomplete. Observing our own bodies and minds, we saw only illusory emptiness, growing ever more alarmed and terrified, with nowhere to turn. We then sought the True Sovereign, beseeching compassionate aid.**

**The True Sovereign gazed at us for a long while, eyes smiling, and said:**
**"You demon kings, since ancient times, have followed qi’s ebb and flow, transforming at will, believing yourselves eternal. Yet your minds drift and wander, falsely distinguishing right from wrong, arising and ceasing in karmic bonds. Deluded and racing, you seek to harm others, yet only harm yourselves, lingering in the Five Paths, bound at the Eight Gates. How could you ever escape?**

**"If you can cease the Six Passions, follow the Two Existences, cultivate the true Dao’s reality, and refrain from generating thoughts of approach or aversion, then you may enter the Dao. Yet even this ‘entering’ is but a name—only by harmonizing with all dharmas and aligning with nature can you be free from fear.**

**"Your bodies and minds are but temporary constructs of the Two Existences, fundamentally unreal. How could deluded minds give rise to terror?"**

**The Sentient Sons said:**
**"Now, by the Heavenly Worthy’s grace, you have shown us the path of non-arising, the Dharma of non-mind, granting us the fearless mantra. We shall cultivate with true resolve, free from attachment to approach or aversion, practicing skillfully without defilement, harmonizing our endeavors to guide others into the Dao’s source.**

**"Now, we proclaim this divine incantation, universally bestowing it upon heavenly beings. Those who aspire with devoted hearts shall attain peace."**

**And they spoke the incantation:**
**Primordial Great Unity,**
**Nine qi transform and give birth.**
**Radiant essence surges and shines,**
**Flowing Gold and fire-bells.**
**Vibrant and resplendent,**
**Embracing the moon and spitting stars.**
**Poisonous dragons hurl fire,**
**Raven-Mother holds the vase.**
**Summon and seize the Six Feng,**
**Behead and slay demonic forms.**
**Ānā sounds the drum,**
**Divine clouds erect the bells.**
**Search the heavens with axes,**
**Long fangs array tassels.**
**Bind wind and fire,**
**Hunt and capture demonic essences.**
**Gather and record radiance,**
**No names are spared.**
**The Six Heavens’ old qi—**
**What rebellion remains unquelled?**
**The Five Emperors’ talismanic decree,**
**Golden Horses speed the message.**
**Hasten! As the Most High’s Law commands!**

**The Three Heavenly True Kings’ Incantation for Dispelling Epidemics and Transforming Celestial Lodges**

**Radiant essence’s central king,**
**Might shakes the Nine Heavens.**
**Golden tigers obscure the sun,**
**Flying dragons encircle the heavens.**
**Yellow spirits wield halberds,**
**Green-teethed ones brandish whips.**
**The Jade Balance and Five Ladles,**
**Harmonizing the Seven Primes.**

**Seize and capture the Nine Shameful Ones,**
**Slay and extinguish the Six Heavens.**
**Hands grasp the Three Radiances,**
**Feet tread the Nine Mysteries.**
**Eight Mighties spew poison,**
**Heavenly Soldiers lead the way.**
**Hunt and examine demonic essences,**
**Consign them to the Nine Springs.**
**The Ten Heavens guard the realm,**
**All things secure in peace.**

The Three Heavenly True Ones declare:
In future kalpas, those who study the Dao and seek truth—devout men and women—whether dwelling in official rank, secluded in mountains and forests, or hidden in court and marketplace, when they encounter the *yang jiu bai liu* (the baleful cycle of nine and six), the juncture of adversity and prosperity, when their destined term arrives and karmic misfortunes converge—blade and warfare, flood and fire, epidemics and famine—when myriad disasters arise, they should steady their minds, guard their resolve, and disengage from worldly affairs. Purify themselves in fasting rites, burn incense and light lamps, or practice visualization and breath regulation, sounding drums and striking bells and chimes. With every four words, bow once; inner and outer spirits unite. From the crown, nine lights emerge, illuminating the Three Realms. The head bears the Seven Stars, the *qi* of the Northern Dipper surging before them. The kingly *qi* and cloudy radiance issue from the Five Viscera, enveloping the body, filling the Eight Extremities, transforming into dragons, tigers, lions, and demon-quelling beasts. They charge before and behind, each conforming to its directional color, exhaling their kingly *qi*, streaming forth golden fire and ringing bells, dispelling calamities.

Thereupon, the celestial hosts—supreme sages and perfected immortals—universally descend. The Five Emperors escort them, delivering them from pestilence and disaster, guiding them into the source of the Dao. A universal proclamation is made to future generations: devout men and women who turn their hearts toward this path shall surely attain peace. Cultivate non-action, nurture the spirit, and naturally return. Hold fast to my Three Treasures, focus the mind without distraction. For one seven-day period, two seven-day periods, or even three months, burn incense and bow in worship to the Most High Jade Emperor, the Eight Pure Dao Lords, the Ten Directions’ Numinous Treasure Boundless Heavenly Worthies, the Nine Palaces’ Four Poles’ Supreme Clarity Divine Officials, and the host of perfected saints. Invoke their names, chant and recite their praises. With the three karmas established in goodness, ascend to the mysterious and profound. With sincere intent, one’s self evokes response—**the Dao does not forsake humanity.**

Thereupon, the Heavenly Worthy extols the Three Worthies in verse, saying:
**The Great Dao has no coming or going,**
**Things naturally follow and welcome it.**
**Silent, it cannot be named,**
**Yet breath and utterance are its names.**
**Eternally abiding, without end or extinction,**
**How could its responsive movement have a beginning?**
**Now I bow my head in reverence,**
**Pledging my life to the Jade Emperor’s court.**

**Resplendent with dragon and phoenix script,**
**Majestic radiance illumines the Ten Heavens.**
**When resonance departs, it hides in golden registers;**
**When mechanism arrives, it unfolds jade chapters.**
**Empty sounds swell in splendid echoes,**
**Manifesting and concealing as steps and pipes.**
**Chanting and reciting, singing of nature and destiny,**
**Harmonizing and flowing into the mysterious and profound.**

**Majestic and towering, the Dao’s honored one,**
**Whose merit and conduct are already complete and equal.**
**Descending to receive me,**
**Masters and guardians escort me side by side.**
**With compassion, bestowing the Dharma-water of wisdom,**
**To wash away delusion and confusion.**
**Forever crossing to the Three Clarities’ shore,**
**Ever parting from the Five Turbidities’ mire.**

The Perfected Sovereign then extols the Three Worthies, having uttered his vows, saying:
Today, for the sake of future kalpas, I employ the Orthodox Dharma to nurture and protect all beings. Adapting to worldly customs, I teach and transform, practicing the Great Vehicle’s Dao, entering all directions in accord with their affairs. Through karmic conditions and retributions, I offer skillful means and benefits. Establishing fasting rites and practicing the Dao, I enable the cultivation of vows and mindfulness. The Four Great Elements unite in virtue, merging into a single source.

**First vow:** May the Great Dao’s profound profundity, the true source’s emptiness and stillness, remain undiminished in wisdom though realms rise and fall.
**Second vow:** May the Nine Heavens be clear and bright, the Seven Luminaries lofty and luminous. May primordial essence harmonize and descend, nourishing all beings.
**Third vow:** May the Nine Earths be tranquil, mountains and rivers fertile. May myriad plants ever flourish, sweet springs increase, and all sentient and formed beings receive sustenance and nurturance.
**Fourth vow:** May the Heavenly Sovereign govern with sagely assistance, the unseen and manifest realms receiving grace. May all things—moving and still—thrive in harmony, preserving the great foundation in abundance and peace.
**Fifth vow:** May the Three Masters and Dao companions universally attain the Six Penetrations. May virtue fill them, wisdom and eloquence enlighten the ignorant. In hidden or manifest worldly paths, may all things harmonize. May minds remain unstained, bodies soar in the Great Void.
**Sixth vow:** May the Eight Gates and Five Paths’ karmic retributions be dissolved. May evil destinies be forever severed, good fortunes eternally abide. May souls don crowns and sashes, clothed and fed from the celestial kitchens.
**Seventh vow:** May crawling, flying, wriggling, and moving beings—born or unborn—be nourished by primordial essence, preserving their natures in peace. May all enjoy joy and prosperity, receiving delight and glory.
**Eighth vow:** May all be universally uplifted, ascending together to Jade Clarity. With minds fixed on the mysterious and tranquil, may people attain perfection through the Dao. May all return to blessed fruits, the Dao’s *qi* prolonging life.

**The Five Elder Thearchs’ Divine Incantation for Protecting the Realm and Dispelling Disasters for Immortal Aspirants**

At that time, the Five Elder Thearchs rose together, bowed again, adjusted their robes, composed their countenances, and knelt before the honored one, addressing him thus:
For kalpas uncounted, we have followed the cycles, manifesting and concealing, receiving the Numinous Treasure and constantly employing skillful means to deliver and cross over sentient beings, guiding them into the Orthodox Dharma of non-action and spontaneity. We clarify the worldly path’s origins, ends, conditions, and karmic retributions. Formerly, we received the true scriptures, incantations, and oral transmissions, treasuring them in mind and mouth, never daring to lightly disclose or leak their texts. Now, obeying your edict, we dare not conceal them. There is a divine incantation for protection and pacification, the wondrous root of the Three Caverns, the primordial essence of the Nine *Qi*, blending with the hundred spirits. Its inner name is hidden, its merits, wisdom, and radiance complete and luminous. Though mentioned in other scriptures, when practiced and recited, it inwardly mirrors body and mind, outwardly dispelling disasters. Only the lofty perfected sages can fully comprehend its profound principles, which are not revealed to lesser immortals. Later learners and ordinary deluded ones may transmit it only with sincere faith, closing their minds to practice it. Through pure fasting, silent meditation, visualizing the spirit-*qi*, sounding drums, regulating breath, focusing the mind in recitation, the true numina will swiftly descend, immediately enabling ascent to immortality. How much more so for minor calamities and dangers—how could they not be averted? With single-minded sincerity, one’s self evokes response—**the Dao does not forsake humanity.**

Now reverently recited:

The primordial essence blends in chaos,
Azure *qi* scatters and divides.
Twelve divine youths guard and stabilize
The liver’s *hun*-soul, its root secure.
Two sevens, four fives—transforming cloud encampments,
Nine hearths, nine altars, ancient trees unyielding.
The divine tiger spews venom,
Sword cast, fire burns.
Sweeping away azure afflictions,
Dispersing ominous vapors of light and shadow.
Mind unshaken by delusion,
Securely safeguards the Imperial Lord.

Crimson radiance unfolds the chart,
Fiery essence fans the whirlwind.
Three youths in one dwelling,
Resplendent, floating and soaring.
Overseeing gains and losses,
Myriad emperors pay homage to the宗.
The vermilion phoenix breathes fire,
Metal and stone melt away.
Flying bells, flashing lightning,
Slaying crimson demons in their domain.
Binding the Nine Uglies,
Ash covers, fire burns.
Purifying the imperial reign,
The Dao and virtue wander free.

Golden essence awakens once,
Venus divides sevenfold.
The Imperial Lord’s numinous palace,
Drifting with pale clouds.
Summoning dragons to bear water,
Quenching the blazing smoke.
Long-fanged, colossal beasts,
Hunt and capture the malevolent horde.
The hundred spirits pacified,
I attain spontaneity.

Mysterious radiance vast and clear,
Five *qi* flow and circulate.
Before the twin gates of the Emperor,
Myriad spirits transform and arise.
Calm the will, guard wisdom,
Gaze upon and consume fiery essence.
The azure dragon spits lightning,
Shattering the yellow troops.
Brilliant and crystalline, brandishing swords,
Fire sparks fly in pursuit.
The mighty warriors of the Three Heavens
Seize and extinguish the ten thousand spirits.
Protecting households, pacifying the realm,
The Dao governs, ascends to peace.

Chaos, the primordial One,
Yellow images rush in profusion.
Moved by the True Elder’s grace,
Transforming into the infant.
Nurturing the nine *qi*,
Giving birth to the Two Modes.
Sun and moon ascend,
Stars and constellations descend.
Wind and fire clash,
Blades and swords race in chaos.
The Six Heavens, Nine Uglies—
Scattering the heart’s disunion.
The Most High’s talismanic command,
How dare one not follow?

All beings dwell in peace,
Entering the Dao’s non-action.
At this time, the Perfected One, Weiming Luo, by the Heavenly Worthy’s decree, addressed the great assembly, saying: “All perfected immortals and transcendents! If in future ages you universally succor the multitude of immortals, rescue the distressed, cure illnesses, establish fasts, perform the Dao, recite incantations, and offer reverent worship, you must also prepare cinnabar and vermilion, plain paper and ink, to inscribe and paint divine talismans. Hang them for protection, wear them on your person, present memorials, and summon the divine officials, soldiers, and encampments of the Great Clarity and Great Ultimate to decisively punish malevolent spirits and demonic thieves.

Yet the celestial writings are profoundly wondrous—all are the precise forms of the nine *qi* and the names of the hundred spirits, their shifting appearances and signs, the intricate patterns of their script, the hidden rhymes of their inner names. Established by the majesty and power of their numinous efficacy, they can extinguish calamities and anomalies, preserve and nourish primordial harmony, and guard the twelve double-hours, gates and doors, wells and hearths, latrines and cesspits.

The reason is this: when ordinary people dwell in the world, they may become confused and lost, not yet having entered the Orthodox Unity’s covenant of awe-inspiring might, the numinous treasure’s fountain of grace. Their natures and emotions drift and taint, their minds unsettled, deludedly giving rise to fear. The Six Heavens and Nine Uglies, perceiving their hearts in motion, thereby generate disasters and harms. Thus, one must employ divine talismans for protection, true *qi* for defense, aligning with spontaneity to attain stability.

For those suffering illness, they should also swallow the talismans, cultivate visualization, recite the incantations, perform the Dao thrice daily, face north in the courtyard, invoke the divine soldiers, present memorials and petitions, burn incense and light lamps, hang silk banners and floral streamers, circumambulate while singing hymns. The majestic rites of the Dharma-realm should fully accord with the Three Records, the Four Poles’ Luminous Perfection, the precepts, statutes, and laws. To lightly divulge or negligently profane them brings calamity extending to the nine generations.”

Weiming Luo, the Perfected King, stepped before the great assembly, bowed twice, and knelt. Raising a jade table, he opened a golden casket, burned a hundred precious incenses, sounded the drum, and held his breath, demonstrating the ritual norms to the assembly. He unfolded the jade tablet and inscribed it to transmit the announcement.

Thereupon, the thirty-six Heavenly Lords of Julou and others all rose, bowed twice, and addressed the Heavenly Worthy, saying: “From former times until now, we have received the essential incantations of the Dharma’s savor and truth, all of which we have expounded. Now, may the great assembly of heavenly beings, humans, and divine immortals, each in their own lands, rescue and deliver those in suffering, exalt the sagely Dao, protect the state and pacify the people, broadly propagate the great Dharma, and universally deliver the boundless.

We clearly proclaim to the men and women of future generations and the latter age: those who can turn toward and single-mindedly believe should receive the command, silk, cinnabar, and pigments, establish vows and fasts, and report as the statutes of the Luminous Perfected prescribe. Also offer precious, fine, and sweet fruits—the flavors we present—to the Five Emperors, the thirty-six Heavenly Lords, and the venerable divine lords of spontaneity, to seek their desired blessings.”

The various Perfected Kings, unable to contain their joy, with different bodies but one mind, sang in praise:

Wisdom’s abyss, deep and clear as the sea,
Dharma-water ever brimming full.
Silent, no one calls its name,
Yet when moved, it bears merit’s fame.
The nature of form stirs the divine incantations,
Revealing the *Dongyuan* scriptures’ depths.
Harming none, aiding all beings,
Thus moved, the Worthy manifests form.
Descending to transform the lands of Fangzhu,
Ascending in flight to the Jade Capital’s Dao.
Neither coming nor going,
Neither perishing nor arising.
Resplendent with dragon-phoenix script,
Separating and uniting, tracing divine talismans.
Worldly sentiments distinguish noble and base,
But the Dao makes no distinction between wise and foolish.
With sincere heart, blessings arise,
Through divulgence and negligence, fortune departs.
Good and evil are not others’ opposites,
Rising and sinking accompany the self.
In the end, all return to our Three Treasures.
Dark grace may yet support.
Hard to encounter, now we attain it—
The sagely Dao’s incantations and talismans.
A lifetime’s joy and fortune,
Ten thousand kalpas’ finest affinity.
Sentient beings receive as they feel,
Unmoved hearts do not meet transmission.
The Eight Gates sever karmic retribution,
Nine generations together ascend.
Dispersing and gathering, rejoicing in song,
Bowing before the Imperial Lord.

At the Dharma assembly’s conclusion, the Heavenly Worthy commanded the Five Elders to harness their chariots to the ten directions. The divine immortals all rose and bowed twice. Transforming into Eight Radiance bodies, cloud carriages flying like wheels, resplendent and dazzling, the celestial harmony resounded. Heavenly perfected ones led the procession, riding the void, ascending to the Jade Clarity.

Thus concludes the twelfth scroll of the *Highest Clarity Wondrous Incantations of the Abyssal Cavern*.
Beginning the thirteenth scroll of the *Highest Clarity Wondrous Incantations of the Abyssal Cavern*.

**Chapter of the Dragon Kings**

The Dao spoke: Long ago, upon the Three Heavens, I observed the world below. I beheld the myriad heavens and earths, where pestilential qi spread unchecked. People suffered from illness, lands endured scorching droughts, and the five grains failed to yield. In twos and threes, none knew what to do.

At that time, the Heavenly Worthy rode upon a five-colored cloud, descending upon the lands. Manifesting great divine power, he radiated luminous brilliance, accompanied by over seven thousand two hundred Dragon Kings, immortal youths, and jade maidens. Proclaiming the true Dharma, he universally delivered all beings. A great deluge poured forth, timely and sweetly moistening the earth.

You must not harbor disbelief, lest calamity sink nine generations of ancestors, their suffering souls bound within the offices of ghostly officials, never to escape for a hundred kalpas or a thousand rebirths. But if you diligently cultivate the heart, receive, uphold, recite, and chant, the merit will be profound and far-reaching. The people will know no disaster, each extending their years in longevity, free from harm.

The Dao spoke: When a kingdom faces peril, weapons clash, people devour one another, heaven and earth quake, and the sun and moon lose their light—then in the auspicious direction of blessings and virtue, within palace gardens or where springs and pools reside, establish the positions of the Nine Dragons and the forms of the Five Sages. Turn your thoughts to this sutra, and pay homage to the August Emperor of the Void to pacify the realm. The Heavenly Dragons will respond: demonic vapors will vanish of themselves, warfare will cease, ruler and ministers will follow the Dao, dragon virtue will aid them, and the world will know great peace, ever abiding in prosperity.

At that time, the assembly of immortals, hearing this exposition, all received benefit and universal grace. All sentient beings bowed in reverence, each vowing to receive and uphold it.

**The Supreme Abyssal Summons of the Myriad Heavenly Dragon Kings, Most Wondrous Chapter**

East: Azure Emperor, Azure Dragon King
South: Vermilion Emperor, Vermilion Dragon King
West: White Emperor, White Dragon King
North: Black Emperor, Black Dragon King
Center: Yellow Emperor, Yellow Dragon King
Sun and Moon Dragon Kings
Constellation Dragon Kings
Heavenly Palace Dragon King
Dragon Palace Dragon King
Heavenly Gate Dragon King
Yama Dragon King
Hell Dragon King
Heavenly Virtue Dragon King
Earthly Virtue Dragon King
Heavenly Being Dragon King
Flying Being Dragon King
Lotus Dragon King
Flower Grove Dragon King
Five Marchmounts Dragon King
Mountains and Rivers Dragon King
Additionally:
Demon-Slaying Dragon King
*Kāla* Ghost-Swallowing Dragon King
Lesser Auspicious Dragon King
Greater Auspicious Dragon King
Golden Radiance Dragon King
Golden Hue Dragon King
Yang Qi Dragon King
Yin Qi Dragon King
Medicinal Dragon King
Lion Dragon King
Realm-Preserving Dragon King
Dwelling-Preserving Dragon King
Wealth Dragon King
Well and Hearth Dragon King
Gold and Silver Dragon King
Treasure Dragon King
Storehouse Dragon King
Prosperity Dragon King
Five Ridges Dragon King
Five Grains Dragon King
Golden-Headed Dragon King
Clothing and Sustenance Dragon King
Official Rank Dragon King
Official Emolument Dragon King
River and Sea Dragon King
Cloud Sea Dragon King
Huai Sea Dragon King
Mountain Sea Dragon King
Abyssal Sea Dragon King
Land Dragon King
Prefecture and County Dragon King
City Dragon King
Spirit Altar Dragon King
Wind Earl Dragon King
Vibrating Dragon King
Cloud and Rain Dragon King
Great Rain Dragon King
Scattering Water Dragon King
Heavenly Rain Dragon King

The Dao spoke: I declare to all beings—when reciting the divine incantations and wondrous sutras of the Heavenly Dragon Kings I have expounded, you must burn incense and chant for three days and three nights, universally summoning the Heavenly Dragons. In times of drought, rain will fall. Though thunder and lightning arise, no harm will come. The dragons will descend, fulfilling every wish. Whether seeking blessings, virtue, longevity, official rank for sons or daughters, healing for the people’s illnesses, protection for dwellings in peril, resolution of all enmities, or legal disputes—none will fail to prosper.

As for you, demon kings and all wayward ghosts: if you hear this sutra and do not depart, your heads will shatter into seven pieces, your roots utterly severed. Those this sutra subdues will submit; those it dispels will retreat.

If lands, cities, towns, or villages frequently suffer from heavenly fires, let every household first inscribe the names of the Four Seas’ Dragon Kings and place them at the four corners of their dwellings. Then, burn incense and uphold the recitation, and the Water Dragons will come to guard. The Eastern Sea Dragon King of the East, the Southern Sea Dragon King of the South, the Western Sea Dragon King of the West, and the Northern Sea Dragon King of the North—each will soar through the void, manifesting divine transformations. In an instant, they will spew ten thousand *shi* of water. The fire spirits, upon seeing it, will plunge a thousand feet into the earth. There is also the Great Water Dragon King, who presides over the center, guarding and pacifying each direction, sweeping away inauspiciousness.

The Dao spoke: For households of good men and good women who serve the Dragon Kings—if you inscribe the name of the Ever-Peaceful Dragon and place it within your storehouses, offering pure water and fresh fruits in timely devotion, or on the days of the new and full moon when dragons are worshipped, recite this sutra and invoke the Dragon Kings—your home will prosper in wealth, free from loss, your storehouses overflowing. The efficacy of this sutra is beyond measure.

At that time, the fourfold assembly, hearing this exposition, rejoiced immeasurably. Eighty-four thousand Dragon Kings leapt forth as one, heaven and earth trembled, divine dragons gathered, and a great deluge poured forth, universally delivering all beings. All heavenly and human beings simultaneously praised it, bowing their heads in reverence and vowing to uphold it.

The Dao spoke: By decree of Wang Lu and Li Zhong, the Daoist priestesses and female officials of Nanhai and Hailing, along with all Daoist followers, are to be universally informed. Since my transformation began fifty-three years ago, I have been sent by the Most High to traverse the Five Marchmounts, converting the ten directions, circling the world without fail, desiring to inaugurate a reign of Great Peace under a non-acting emperor. Yet the hearts of people today are shallow: the good are few, the wicked many.

From this time forth until the *renwu* year, I shall dispatch seventy-two disciples to roam the world, teaching and transforming all beings, bestowing upon them the Dao’s qi.

For these people, greedy for wealth and sensual pleasures, falsely claim to be sages and worthies, deceiving and misleading the common folk—though they speak a thousand words or ten thousand, not one response shall they receive. Since the *jiazi* year, I have eliminated them by the Law, and of the remaining thirty-six, I now bestow upon them the Dao’s *qi*, that they may protect and sustain the ruler and the people. Exhort them to goodness—revere this, revere this!

At that time, the world’s fate pressed close, and evil men abounded. In the *jisi* year, on the third day of the third month, I dispatched ghostly soldiers from the ten directions to drive out the wicked, beginning at Huayin’s Western Marchmount. Now they have reached Mount Heng’s Southern Marchmount, erasing all traces, leaving not one in ten, their corpses strewn by the myriad, unburied and unhidden. Do you yet know this?

From this time forth, every third day of the third month, I shall send a million ghostly soldiers from Mount Song, driving out the wicked between the lands of Nan, Ji, Ding, Guo, Huang, Bao, and Han, erasing all traces, leaving not one in ten. Now, with Mount Heng’s Northern Marchmount, I fear all shall be swept away. I tell you now: of foolish scholars, fewer than a hundred can see, and fewer than a thousand can act—yet they claim to know the distant past. How pitiable are the deaf and blind among the common folk!

From Qing and Qi southward, to Yangzhou and north to Yan, these are lands of fortune. You must diligently perform purification rites, sweep and purify the altars—do not treat this as ordinary. In the *jiashen* year, I shall unleash a great flood to scour away the bones of the wicked. At that time, the myriad people shall be swept away. I now speak this especially to you, the faithful, that you may each know and instruct the Daoist followers, teaching and admonishing the disciples of the Law. Apply yourselves earnestly—do not treat this as ordinary.

I see into your hearts: you have taken the incense and lamp offerings to feed your families and sustain yourselves, not as those of true devotion. I admonish you now—each of you must reform your hearts, diligently bestow charity upon the poor and needy, and never use wealth gained by unrighteous means. Waste nothing without reason. Poverty is not due to lack of fortune, nor is wealth the result of cunning—all is by my power, descending the Dao’s *qi*, my numinous might overshadowing, bringing it to pass.

I come from the void, formed of accumulated *qi*, my movements leaving no trace, my presence casting no shadow, my hearing producing no sound, my sight taking no form. At times, I rise three feet from the heavens, or hover three feet above the earth; at others, I float three feet above men’s heads, witnessing all within the great earth below—what is there I do not see? How could you know whether my spirit is near or far? I do not reach the heavens above nor touch the earth below, drifting beside the Gate of Heaven and the Starry River. What do I seek? What do I desire? Only this: the myriad people are forlorn, the great flood approaches, a thousand calamities converge, driving out the wicked factions—ten thousand deaths, no life spared.

When Great Peace emerges, heed my drum’s call. I shall instruct you, the Daoist priests and priestesses, and all of good heart among the various peoples. I know the celestial tribulation draws near, its time appointed. The year’s fate presses close—each of you must apply yourselves earnestly; do not treat this as ordinary. In the *renshen* year, I shall send forth a hundred diseases to purge the wicked.

I speak now to those of good heart, that all may know. In the *guiyou* year, I shall dispatch three disciples, bearing a million talismans of divine truth, to traverse the Five Marchmounts. Those who receive these talismans shall be untouched by the myriad disasters, and no hundred ghosts shall draw near. In the *jiaxu* year, there shall appear a kind of yellow-robed messenger, indistinguishable from the wicked. You must tend to your incense and lamps diligently—do not be deluded by those who share your practice, mimicking this form. Before the incense and lamps, you shall witness Great Peace.

I proclaim to the Daoist priests and priestesses within the Five Marchmounts and the Nine Provinces: at the end of the nine calamities, when the hundred-and-six count is exhausted, men and ghosts shall contend, the evil age shall be hard to endure. Teach one another, that all may turn to goodness. On the third, fifth, seventh, and ninth days, diligently perform purification rites, sweep and purify the altars—let nothing be lacking.

On the first day of the first month, I shall dispatch a million ghostly soldiers to drive out the wicked factions. Thirty thousand ghostly soldiers, each wielding a red staff, shall slay the evil upon the roads. Another fifty thousand ghostly soldiers, each bearing yellow medicine, shall inflict heart pains and epidemics, killing only those of wicked hearts. Seven thousand ghostly soldiers, each holding yellow medicine, shall spread plague—those afflicted shall find their limbs withered, unable to stretch. Six thousand ghostly soldiers, each bearing green medicine, shall roam the world—those stricken shall choke, their mouths sealed, unable to speak, until their lives end. Ten thousand ghostly soldiers, each holding white medicine, shall wander the world—those who contract this sickness shall suffer dizziness and deafness, dying upside-down. Twenty thousand ghostly soldiers, each bearing black medicine, shall roam the world—those afflicted shall burn with fever, rave in madness, and die without sleep. Five thousand ghostly soldiers, each holding red powder, shall traverse the world—those who fall ill shall die suddenly, unable to speak.

A million child-spirits, each wielding thunder chariots and lightning bolts, shall I dispatch every third day of the third month to slay the unrighteous. Do you, the people of the world, know how many I command to be killed in a single day? When the hundred disasters converge and deceptions arise, if you wish to survive these calamities, then before the incense and lamps, do not trust those who deceive. I send forth thirty-six disciples to roam the Nine Provinces and Five Marchmounts, teaching and transforming all people. I bestow upon them the Dao’s *qi*—my disciples’ heads shall bear a sign: not yellow but red, not green but white. If you see their light, revere my gate with a single heart.

After Great Peace, a non-acting emperor shall govern the realm. Then shall there be thirty-six thousand who become immortals.

Moreover, there shall be one thousand white youths, who shall erect fifty-eight thousand banners, each banner three feet in length, its head adorned with a coiling dragon. These shall command fifty-eight thousand stalwart men, each bearing such a banner. They shall also lead one thousand one hundred female officials, each holding an incense burner, and all shall proceed in three ranks clad in yellow robes. At such a time, joy shall be unceasing, the world overflowing with abundance, and the sagely transformation so vast that the myriad people shall harbor no grievance.

I inaugurate the beginning of Great Peace, first arising upon Mount Meng; thereafter, governance shall return to simplicity. How could you know the reason for this? My great cycle is fixed, my great covenant abides. Each of you must apply your heart and never grow remiss.

I charge you, Daoist priests and nuns who follow the Dao’s stream: do not adhere to ordinary intentions. Each year, I thrice traverse the world to observe your cultivation. How could you know this? Sometimes I appear as a wandering scholar, sometimes as an urgent imperial messenger, sometimes as a destitute old man, sometimes as a forlorn orphan. Who can discern the true from the false?

I customarily tread upon your altars on the first day of the first month, drifting north and south, or east and west. How could you fathom which altars I do not ascend, which chambers I do not enter? Within the fasting altars, I dwell in every place.

I take pity on you, fearing you may not attain the highest good. Thus, I traverse the world, passing through every place, lest you abandon the true for the false, lead the multitude into wrongdoing. When Great Peace is revealed, yellow-robed followers shall appear in succession. The good shall receive fortune, the wicked shall wither of themselves. Punishment shall extend to the three clans—whom then shall you blame?

I reside upon the Nine Heavens, at times riding cloud-cranes, driving crimson dragons, bearing extraordinary scriptures. The grotto-heavens of the Five Marchmounts and the renowned mountains under heaven—sometimes I wander among the common folk, concealed within the dust, refining conduct and cultivating essence. How could the foolish or wise know me? Sometimes I appear as an infant child, sometimes as a white-haired elder. By day I conceal myself, by night I roam, yet the hearts of the myriad people do not follow.

Before Great Peace is fully revealed, the sea’s treasury shall open the great flood. Xiangzhou shall shake with the sound of bronze drums, and the world shall tremble with dread. The impoverished shall lead the Daoists to restore my original palace. Lotus blossoms shall canopy the nine chambers, white deer shall graze upon the verdant pines. Phoenixes shall perch upon their sunny slopes, and qilin shall come to pay homage. Banners and flowers shall gleam like the sun and moon—who among those who see them would not follow?

If you wish to behold my form, devote your heart to emptiness. I dwell upon the Nine Heavens, briefly wandering the Five Marchmounts. When the multitude of worthies gathers to discourse, the ford of Meng shall be leveled, and the ditches of Lu made smooth. Blood shall flow to form rivers, and white bones shall pile into hills. The regions of Qing and Qi shall rise in great floods, while Ji and Ding shall become torrents. Between Dunhuang and the Baohan, the myriad people shall drift and float.

Of old, there were ten great trials, through which my body was tempered a hundredfold. Reflecting thus, why should I bear grudges from former days? The sea’s treasury shall open the great wilderness, and in one stroke, the Nine Provinces shall be pacified. The Eastern Sea shall become mulberry fields, and Yuzhou shall rise with green towers. Those who witness Great Peace shall rejoice without sorrow.

The eternal mountains—Hua, Heng, and Song—I first traversed long ago. If you wish to know the vast and boundless, seek only among the fords and ditches. Jade maidens weave by the river, standing at their looms to craft brocade. If you do not believe this, go and ask Zhang Qian. Trust also in Dongfang Shuo, whose heart and intent are ever proclaimed.

Heaven and Earth shall unite in harmony, and gatherings shall form karmic bonds. Ghostly soldiers, numberless as the infinite, shall carry stones to fill Kunlun. What mountain could rise higher than this? I alone shall stand with Heaven. Linked and joined, I shall cleave the Great Void, erecting altars of gold and silver. White jade shall guard the four corners, and immortal palaces and temples shall line the way.

The August Elder shall ascend the altar, and the good shall return to Chang’an. At that time, the Most High expounded this scripture and incantation, causing all sentient beings to turn their hearts toward goodness.

Here ends Scroll Thirteen of the *Most High’s Scripture of the Wondrous Spells of the Abyssal Grotto*.
Here begins Scroll Fourteen of the *Most High’s Scripture of the Wondrous Spells of the Abyssal Grotto*.

**Chapter on the Hymn of the Ghost-Slaying Steps**

The Dao spoke, saying to the Perfected One of Luminous Net: "From this day forward, if any person of good heart suffers misfortune or plague, they should invite a Daoist of the Three Caverns to recite the scriptures on their behalf. They must abstain from meat and pungent foods, forsake carnal desires, purify body and mind, and focus their thoughts in silent recitation, allowing no stray thoughts. They must constantly visualize the Five August Emperors, the spirit officials, the generals and attendants, and the guards on either side. The sponsor of the fast must devote themselves wholeheartedly, prostrating with reverence. The Dharma Master must summon the Perfected Immortals and Heavenly Worthies to descend and deliver the people from their afflictions. If their hearts are not sincere, their offerings of silk and treasure will be wasted, and the immortals and sages will not protect them. But if they follow my decree, they shall forever remain free from harm.

"Upon reciting this precious scripture once, the Heavenly Soldiers shall descend, and the Demon Kings shall be bound. If they do not heed my words, the Demon King Wulinzi shall have his head shattered into three hundred pieces."

At that time, the Perfected One of Luminous Net entreated the Five Emperors and the divine immortals with their armies to descend into the ritual arena and search out and capture the demonic thieves.

The Azure Emperor of the East, Lord of the Nine Yi, with the Azure Spirit General and his host of eighty-one times ten thousand, along with the divine immortals and spirit officials of the eastern realm, all descended together to seize the azure plague spirits of wood in the east.

The Vermilion Emperor of the South, Lord of the Eight Man, with the Vermilion Spirit General and his host of sixty-four times ten thousand, along with the divine immortals and spirit officials of the southern realm, all descended together to seize the vermilion plague spirits of fire in the south.

The White Emperor of the West, Lord of the Six Rong, with the White Spirit General and his host of thirty-six times ten thousand, along with the divine immortals and spirit officials of the western realm, all descended together to seize the white plague spirits of metal in the west.

The Black Emperor of the North, Lord of the Five Di, with the Black Spirit General and his host of twenty-five times ten thousand, along with the divine immortals and spirit officials of the northern realm, all descended together to seize the black plague spirits of water in the north.

The Yellow Emperor of the Center, Lord of the Three Qin, with the Yellow Spirit General and his host of nine times ten thousand, along with the divine immortals and spirit officials of the central realm, all descended together to seize the yellow plague spirits of earth in the center.

All shall be swept away and utterly destroyed, so that the afflicted may recover from their illnesses and the people enjoy peace and health.

Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the oral command of the Most High, let the Five Directions’ divine generals slay the ghosts and pacify the people. Such is the law.

The Dao spoke: "The common folk and officials, the gate wardens and household guardians, the left and right pavilion chiefs, all the high and low ministers and grandees, the thirty myriad spirits within the home, the Three Generals who guard the dwelling, and the Broad Han upon the roof—let the master of the household, together with all its members, be freed from all misfortune: the nightmares and disorienting dreams, the frequent apparitions of malevolent spirits, which have persisted for so long without respite.

"Moreover, it is feared that the ancestors of the household—those who have passed before or after, the seven generations of forebears and the nine lineages of descendants—may have encountered inauspicious days or ill-fated hours, transgressed against Heaven and Earth, or offended the Three Luminaries, the great deities of the ten directions, and the Perfected Sages of the eight extremities. Thus, the household suffers from illnesses great and small, calamities arising in due season, curses and schemes, locusts and drought, epidemics among the six livestock. Therefore, the scriptures are recited, memorials presented, and offerings made to dissolve disasters and resolve all matters.

"From thirty-six generations past, the demonic thieves of the mountain forests and earth altars, the malevolent spirits of household shrines and temples, the thousand ghosts and ten thousand specters, the inner and outer kin of the family—all shall receive the merit of the scriptures, their calamities dissolved and resolved. From this day forward, after the recitation of the scriptures, they shall receive ten thousandfold blessings. Their wishes shall be fulfilled, their careers advanced, their desires granted. The sick shall recover, dreams shall be auspicious, legal entanglements resolved, plagues and banditry shall not arise, ghostly *qi* shall vanish, and evil spirits shall be extinguished.

"If you, demon kings, do not follow my teachings, your heads shall be shattered into one hundred and twenty pieces."

The Dao spoke: "From this day forth, as the Three Caverns spread their transformative influence, if any Daoist can establish a fast and recite the scriptures for the afflicted, present memorials, and perform offerings, wherever the Dharma Master conducts the ritual, evil ghosts shall hear of it and flee of their own accord. Young and old alike must devote themselves sincerely, prostrating toward the north to listen to the Dharma Master’s chanting of the hymns. When demonic spirits hear it, they shall naturally retreat far away, driven off for ten thousand leagues, never daring to return.

"Children, be earnest and reverent, and listen with respect:

The Azure Emperor of the East,
Goumang, how vast and green!
People grow like a hundred grasses,
Fragrant by nature as the seasons turn.
The good ascend to Heaven,
The wicked fall into boiling cauldrons.
Like seeks like by its *qi*,
Unlike cannot long endure.
Outward discord brings no harmony,
But accord is like the mandarin ducks.
Disdain leads one far from the Dao,
Reverence ascends to Heaven’s halls.
Honor the master as sun and moon,
Filial piety moves the ten directions.
Those who disbelieve the Three Caverns’ law
Shall tread blades of frost for ten thousand kalpas.
Seven generations sink into the Nine Darks,
Endless night stretches on.
Alas for the foolish mortal—
Death brings calamity to descendants.
Those who slander the Dao of immortals and sages
Shall suffer hardship for ages unending.
Do not believe? Then know this:
The unrighteous find no peace.
Practice goodness, ascend to Heaven’s halls,
Receive the registers, join the ranks of immortals,
And behold the August Most High.
Chronic illness breeds evil ghosts—
Invoke the sacred hymns.
Seven generations of ancestors shall be freed,
Gazing upon the light of sun and moon.
Establish fasts, aid the poor,
Drink the jade pool’s nectar.
Heavenly spirits all descend,
Commanding every king:
Each must restrain their ghosts,
Lest they act with reckless force.
Seize the venomous, capture the myriad ghosts,
Crush the wicked and conceal them.
Today, slay the evil ghosts,
Submit to the Azure Vastness.
Plagues flee ten thousand leagues,
Ghosts depart, people thrive.
Rebellion and compliance each take their place,
Blessings bring eternal prosperity.
Divine soldiers heal the sick,
Disciples pay homage to the East.

The Vermilion Emperor of the South,
Yandi, how deep and distant!
The jade consorts of the Three Heavens,
Perfected immortals descend to wander.
Heaven and Earth endure long,
Human life is brief as morning dew.
The mysterious transforms the bright world,
Yet fools do not cultivate.
The deluded do not know the Dao,
And the Dao cannot save them."

The wise scorn glory and wealth,
The foolish crave riches untold.
The wise ever tremble in fear,
The foolish know not sorrow’s hold.
When waters rise nine myriad leagues,
Pestilence and ghostly hosts flow.
If the Dao’s assembly is spurned in the heart,
One departs for ten thousand kalpas—no return.

Illness binds the yang,
The sage’s heart hesitates in pause.
The Dao is the refuge of all beings,
Ten thousand kalpas pass in but a moment’s cause.
Today, I command the ten directions:
Demon kings, ghost lords, and all their kind,
Each must gather your essence true.
Let the sick recover, swift and sure,
As divine spirits bestow their myriad powers.

When great floods and disasters rise,
Heavenly beings and nine dragons welcome the tide.
Reciting scriptures dispels all evil,
The master of rites bows to the South.
The White Emperor of the West,
Rushou, how desolate and vast!
The Three Caverns teach the world’s deluded,
Divine radiance illumines the celestial court.
Heal the sick, and illness fades,
Great waters naturally subside.
Follow the master, wear the talismans,
The immortal Dao is naturally attained.

Those who slander and defame the scriptures and Dharma,
Their sins shall never be absolved.
Wisdom and folly divide Heaven and Earth,
Merit is not built in a single form.
Revere the master, cultivate good karma,
How could the immortal Dao not be achieved?
Today, I present this oral petition,
Jade maidens descend to welcome thee.
Devoutly bow to the West,
Fortune and blessings arise naturally.

The Black Emperor of the North,
Xuanming, how deep and distant!
Only the lofty ones are seen,
Who study the Dao and ever cultivate.
They revere the master, the mysterious sages,
Entrusting their hearts to the wandering Perfected.
Command the demons to cure all ills,
Ten thousand ghosts dare not draw near.
Those who defy shall all be slain,
None shall remain.
The Heavenly Soldiers speak to the Valiant Ones,
"Seize all who oppose with evil intent."
The Most High commands the ten directions,
"Not a moment shall they linger."
Household gods and door guardians,
Above and below, seek one another.
Shelter and protect, ensure life’s prosperity,
All evil shall be dispelled.
Jade maidens of the heavens descend,
True immortals accompany them below.
If illness does not abate,
The demon kings shall themselves be slaughtered.
